<pb n="b001"/>
<head>br̥hatī</head>
<head>prabhākaramśriviracitā ।।</head>
<head> prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<p>uktaṁ kāryamarthaṁ pratipādayatō vēdasya prāmāṇyam । yasya punaḥ kāryēṁ'-
rthē'nvayō nāvagamyatē'kāryatayā, tasya yaḥ pratipādakaḥ tasya kathaṁ prāmāṇyaṁ
sō'rōdīdityēvamādēḥ ? । mā bhūttasya prāmāṇyaṁ; na tadapramāṇatayā pramāṇa-﻿<pb n="b002"/>
mapramāṇaṁ bhavati । pramāṇasya hi anapēkṣatvamuktam; na cānyasyāprāmāṇyāt
pramāṇē tadapaiti । atha manyasē sakalasya vēdasya prāmāṇyaṁ na prāpnōtīti,﻿<pb n="b003"/>
kēnēdaṁ pratijñātaṁ ? yatō'rthāvagatiḥ tasya tallakṣaṇataivēti pratijñā । sā
cānapēkṣatayā sādhitā । yatastvarthāvagatirēva nāsti tadapramāṇamēva । yatō
vā pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayaivāvagatiḥ tasyāpi tata ēva prāmāṇyamityuktaṁ,﻿<pb n="b004"/>
viparyayē cāprāmāṇyamiti । tasmādasaṁbaddhaivēyaṁ cintā—akriyārthānāṁ katha-
miti ।</p>
<p>tadviparyayāt svādhyāyavidhērānarthakyamiti cēt, na svādhyāyaśabda-
vācyasyādhyayanaṁ vidhīyatē nārthavatō'narthakasya vā humityēvamādīnāmiva ।
tasmātkō'yamupālaṁbhaḥ ? । svādhyāyavidhēḥ prayōjanaśūnyatā prāpnōtīti cēt ?﻿<pb n="b005"/>
tanna, niyōgārthanirvr̥ttēḥ kimanyat prayōjanaṁ sarvavidhīnāṁ, sa cākṣaragrahaṇēnaiva
nirvr̥ttaḥ । arthajñānaṁ cārthājjātaṁ, na niyōgataḥ pratipannam । na hi artha-
jñānakāmasya niyōgaḥ, nahi paśvādīnāmiva vēdārthasyānyataḥ prasiddhirasti
yēna tatkāmasyādhyayanaṁ vidhīyatē । nanu ca vēdavadvēdārthasyāpi svādhyāyādanya-
taḥ prasiddhirasti । na hyaprasiddhasya kāraṇatā śakyatē vaktum । prasiddhaścēt﻿<pb n="b006"/>
sutarāmēvaṅkāmasya vidhānaṁ nōpapadyatē jñēyatayaiva hi tat kāmyatē । jñātasya ca
jñēyatayā kāmyatvaṁ nōpapadyatē । niyamārthō vidhiriti cēt । na । anyataḥ
parijñānābhāvāta । grahaṇāntataiva svādhyāyaśabdēnōcyata iti cēt । kēna
cōktaṁ svādhyāyaśabdēna grahaṇāntatōcyata iti । agr̥hītāttarhyarthajñānamasti;﻿<pb n="b007"/>
nāgr̥hītādarthajñānamasti agrahaṇē varṇamātragrahaṇāt । vākyāvagamāditi cēt,
gr̥hītaṁ tarhi vākyam । na hyagr̥hītaṁ vākyatvēnāvagamyatē । tasmānna niyamasyāyaṁ
gōcaraḥ । nāpyarthajñānakāmasyāyaṁ vidhiḥ ataḥ prāmaṇaṁ pramāṇamēva, apramāṇa़ṁ
apramāṇamastu । satyamēvaṁ yathōktaṁ pitr̥matā—tadēva tu prāmāṇyamakāryārthasaṁba-
ndhamavagamyatē । tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tataḥ akāryārthatā vēdasya prāpnōti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b008"/>
<p>nanu ca kāryārthatāpyasti । na । akāryapūrvakatvāt । akāryō hyarthō
hētutāṁ pratipadyatē kāryārthasya । pradarśita caitat—rudraḥ kila rurōda ।
atō'nyēnāpi rōditavyamiti । tasmāttatprabhavaṁ prāmāṇyaṁ tacca pramāṇāntarāpēkṣa-
miti anapēkṣatvamēvākṣipyatē ।</p>
<p>nanu caitat prāmāṇyasiddhyarthamupanyastaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa । kimityanyatraivōpa-﻿<pb n="b009"/>
nīyatē । satyam । siddhasya sādhyaikavākyatā pradarśyatē । tadēkavākyatvē
ca kāryārthatā nāstītyētadēva pradarśyatē ।</p>
<p>kathaṁ tarhyayaṁ granthaḥ adhyāhārēṇa vēti ? kiṁ vāsya granthasya ? ida-
masya, kartavyatvānēkavākyatvādaprāmāṇyaṁ na punarakartavyataikavākyatvāditi ।﻿<pb n="b010"/>
uktam-anēkavākyatvē acintanīyō'yamartha iti । atrāpi cānarthajñō bhavān ।
atrēdamēvākṣipyatē । nahi siddharthānugamāt kartavyatā'vasātuṁ śakyatē—
yathā asminnēva tāvat—kiṁ śakyantē rōdanādayaḥ kartum ।</p>
<p>nanvaśakyatayā na śakyantē na punaḥ siddhānugamāt । siddhatayaiva
hyaśakyatōktā । siddhasya pramāṇāntarāpēkṣatvāt tasya cātrāsambhāvādiṣṭa-﻿<pb n="b011"/>
gādēḥ pramēyasya sambandhinō'sambhavāta; rudrasambandhīṣṭaviyōgādigrāhakapramāṇāntarābhāvāditi
yāvat । <q>tathā ca pramāṇāntarābhāvaṁ darśayati</q> । <quote>“na hyātmanō vapāmutkhidya tatastasyā vapāyāḥ
prahr̥tāyā utthitēna tūparēṇa śakyatē yāgaḥ kartuṁ”</quote> iti ।</p>
<p>yadyatrāpi siddhānugamādēvāśakyatā, kimiti <q>tarhyavāntaravākyōpanyāsaḥ mahāvākya
ēvaitat</q> sidvānugamēnāśakyatvaṁ kimiti punarna darśitam । uttaram&mdash;<q>avāntavākyakalpanā-
yāmapi ētasmātsiddhānugamānna <note n="1"><dn>A mucyāmahē</dn></note>mucyata</q> ityabhiprāyaḥ । sarvaprakāramaprāmāṇyaṁ darśayituṁ
avāntaravākyōpanyāsaḥ । yadi mahāvākyaṁ yathāśrutamāśrīyatē tathāpi siddhānugamaḥ; athā-
śrutamapyavāntaravākyamāśritaṁ tathāpi sa ēva siddhānugama iti sarvathaivāprāmāṇyāt । <q>tadidaṁ</q>
siddhānugamēnāprāmāṇyaṁ <q>ucyatē&mdash;āmnāyasya kriyārthatvādānarthakyamatadarthānāmiti</q> ।</p>
<p>atra cōdayati&mdash;<q>kimidamatadarthānāmiti viśēṣābhidhānam</q> । ēkagranthēnāha&mdash;
<q>nanu ca sarva ēvēdānīmatadarthō vēdaḥ</q> । sarva ēvākāryārtha ityaktam । <quote>‘<q>vasantāya kapiñjalā-
nālabhata iti nāsti siddhānugama iti cēt</q> । vasantāya kapiñjalānālabhata iti siddhārthānu-﻿<pb n="b012"/>
<p>gamābhāvāt <note n="1">C <dn>kāryārthamēva ।</dn></note>kāryārthamētat; tēnaitadvyudāsāya <quote>‘ava/?/darthānā’</quote>miti viśēṣābhidhānam ।
ākṣēptā āha&mdash;<note n="2">A <dn>āyāta ।</dn></note><q>tadēvēdamāpatitamacintanīyō'yamartha iti</q> । yadi kiñcitkāryārthaṁ kiñci-
ccākāryārthaṁ tadā nēdamadhikaraṇamārabdhavyam । yasyaiva kāryārthatvaṁ tadviṣayatvēnāpi cōdanā-
lakṣaṇapratijñōpapattēḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu yadi siddhārthānugamābhāvādānarthakyaṁ kapiñjalānālamēta ityādivākyānāmacinta-
nīyamidaṁ, tadā bhavatvacintanīyaṁ; naitāvatā <note n="3">C <dn>siddhānugamaḥ ।</dn></note>siddhārthānugamaḥ kapiñjalādivākyānāṁ śakyatē
<note n="4">A <dn>avagantuṁ ।</dn></note>vaktumityāśaṅkyāha&mdash;<q>na kapiñjalādivākyānāmapi kāryārthatvam; tēṣāmapi siddhārthēnaika-
vākyatvāt</q> । <quote>‘vasantāya kapiñjalānālamata’</quote> ityaṅgavidhaya ētē । aṅgavidhayaśca pradhāna-
vidhinaikavākyatāpannāḥ । pradhānavidhiśca siddhārthēnaikavākyatāpanna iti sarvēṣāmapi
sākṣādēkavākyatāpannaṁ vidhyantaragataṁ vā siddhārthamastyēvaikavākyatāpannaṁ <note n="5">C <dn>padamiti ।</dn></note>padajātamiti
sarva ēvākāryārthō vēdaḥ । <q>atō'tadarthānāmiti na nivartyaṁ kiñcidavasīyatē</q> ।
samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>idamavasīyatē-siddhasādhyārthatayā vākyānāṁ siddhārthamukhēna ayamākṣēpaḥ</q> ।
yēnaiva rūpēṇāsāvākṣēpaḥ tadēva dyōtayituṁ atadarthānāmityuktam, na punaḥ kasyacidvyā-
vr̥ttyartham । <q>ata idamuktam ānarthakyamatadarthānāmiti । yathā ca siddhārthāpēkṣitayā''kṣēpaḥ
tathōditam;</q> vivr̥taṁ ca bhāṣyakārēṇa <quote>‘tānyēkadēśākṣēpēṇākṣipyanta’</quote> iti । ēka&mdash;﻿<pb n="b013"/>
vākyatvē hi sati ēkadēśatā bhavatyarthavādānām<note n="1">C <dn>vādapadānāṁ ।</dn></note> । anyathā <note n="1">C <dn>svātantryēṇaikadēśatvānupapattēḥ ।</dn></note>svatantrasyaikadēśānupapattēḥ ।
tēna ēkadēśaśabdaṁ prayuñjānēna bhāṣyakārēṇa ēkavāktāśrayaṇēnāyamākṣēpa iti vivr̥tam ।
yadyēkavākyatvāśrayaṇēnāyaṁ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ, <q>kathaṁ tarhi rāddhāntē ēkavākyatāṁ prati praśnōttarē</q> ।
pr̥cchati&mdash;kō'bhiprāyastava kathaṁ tarhi rāddhānta ēkavākyatāṁ prati praśnōttarē iti vadataḥ ।
<q>uttaram&mdash;ayamabhiprāyō mama; ēkavākyatānibandhanō'yaṁ prāmāṇyākṣēpō na bhavati;</q>
kintu <q>bhinnānāṁ vākyānā</q>marthavādātmakānāṁ <q>kā pratipattiḥ</q> ? kīdr̥śī varṇanā ? iti
cintāyāṁ pūrvapakṣē akriyārthatvēnā<q>narthakyamabhidhāya atra rāddhāntē stutyarthatvē</q>naikavākyatvā-
<q>darthavattōditēti</q> । yadi hyēkavākyatāśrayaṇēnākṣēpō bhavēta naikavākyatāśrayaṇēna samādhānaṁ syāt;
tasmāt bhinnavākyatvēna pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ēkavākyatvēna rāddhānta ityavagamyatē । pariharati&mdash;﻿<pb n="b014"/>
<q>ahō ajñānakātaryamāyuṣmataḥ pradarśitamasmābhiḥ&mdash;tānyēkadēśākṣēpēṇākṣipyanta iti</q> ।
ēkavākyatvāśrayaṇēnāyamākṣēpa ityētatpradarśanaparaṁ bhāṣyam । tēna ēkavākyatvāśrayaṇēnaivāyaṁ
kr̥tsnasya vēdasya prāmāṇyākṣēpaḥ । <q>rāddhāntē tu yē praśnōttarē tatraiva</q> rāddhānta ēva <q>cōdanīyē</q>
kathamētē praśnōttarē iti । bhavatā tu ajñānakātarēṇa pūrvapakṣāvasthāyāmēva yaccōditaṁ tat tava
kātaryaṁ kēvalam । kiñca <q>parihartavyē ca</q> samādhātavyē ca ētē praśnōttarē rāddhāntakāla ēvā-
smābhiḥ । tēna cōdyāvakāśa ēvātra nāsti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b015"/>
<p><q>yatpunaridānīṁ udāharaṇabhēdēnānarthakyamuktam śāstradr̥ṣṭavirōdhācca</q> ityēvamādibhiḥ
sūtraiḥ tat pūrvapakṣē <q>hētuprapañcārthaṁ</q> pūrvapakṣahētūn prapañcayitum । <q>hētuprapañcasya prayōjanaṁ</q>
śabdādhikaraṇa <q>uktam</q>&mdash;sarvē pūrvapakṣahētavaḥ upanyasya nirākāryāḥ । anupanyastē hi kasya
cinmandadhiyaḥ punarutkōpō bhavēditi । <q>asmiṁstvayamaparō viśēṣaḥ parihārāntarapariharaṇīya-
tvam</q> &mdash; yathā yāvantaḥ śabdāḥ nityatvahētavaḥ ēkēnaiva pratijñōpanyāsēna parihriyantē tathaitē
ānarthakyahētavō na bhavanti nānāparihārapariharaṇīyatvātḥ tasmāt pr̥thamupanyastāḥ pr̥thak
pr̥thak parihāradānāyēti ।</p>
<p><q>tasmādanityamucyata</q> iti sūtram; tadanupapannamiva pratibhāti । yadi tāvadvākyasyā-
nityatvamucyatē tatsiddhāntinō'pi sammatamēva । anityaṁ hi kāraṇavattvamucyatē; yaddhi kāraṇavat
tadanityam । vākyañcānu<note n="2">C <dn>ānupūrpīviśēṣa ।</dn></note>pūrvyaviśēṣaparigr̥hītavarṇātmakapadasaṅghātātmakaṁ ānupūrvyasya kāraṇattvēna
kāraṇavat । na ca tādr̥śē'nityatvamucyatē, tadaśakyaṁ varṇānāṁ nityatvāt । padārthānāñca yadyapi
kēṣāñcidanityatā tathāpi kēṣāñcidgōtvādīnāṁ nityatvādityāśaṅkyāha&mdash;<q>tasmādanityamucyata iti ।
siddhārthāpēkṣitayā pramāṇāntarasavyapēkṣārthatvaṁ anityatvaṁ, śabdārthayōrnityatvāllōkē vēdēpi</q> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="16"/>
ataēva bhāṣyakārēṇāpyayamarthō vivr̥taḥ । <quote>yadyapi nityāni na nityakāryaṁ
kurvanti</quote> iti । kiṁ punarnityasya kāryaṁ ? pramāṇāntarānapēkṣaṁ svārthaprati-
pādanam । ataḥ pramāṇāntarānapēkṣataiva nityatōcyatē । tēnāsyā
ēvāyamākṣēpaḥ—tasmādanityamucyata iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="17"/>
<p><q>vidhinā ।। vidhyuddēśēnaikavākyatvāt iti ।</q> kasyēdaṁ vyākhyānam ?﻿<pb n="18"/>
vidhinētyasya ? nanu ca nōpapadyatē vidhirvidhyuddēśaḥ । satyaṁ,
lakṣaṇayōcyatē । kimiti lakṣaṇā ? ēkavākyatvāditi vacanāt ।
ēkavākyatvaṁ vidhinā nōpapadyatē । vidhinaiva hi sarvasyaikavākyatā ।
satyaṁ kartavyatānvayaḥ yasya । na ca stutēḥ kartavyatā'vasīyatē ।
kiṁ tarhi ? stutyēna saṁbandhaḥ । kiṁ vidhyarthō na stutyaḥ ? na
brūmō na stutya iti । kṣēpiṣṭhatvādayastu guṇāḥ vidhēyē stutimutpādayanti;
ta ēvātadarthānāmityākṣiptāḥ; ākṣēpasamādhānārthaṁ caitat sūtram; tasmāt﻿<pb n="19"/>
yuktā lakṣaṇā । ata ēva ca <quote>kathamēkavākyatvaṁ</quote> iti praśnaḥ ।
kimidaṁ ? idamidam vidhyuddēśēnaikavākyatvam । vidhyuddēśasya ca
tadanēkavākyatvācca na kartavyatāvagamaḥ akartavyatāvagamē ca nāsti
prāmāṇyam । atō'yaṁ praśnaḥ kathamēkavākyatvamiti ।</p>
<p>itara āha—<q>uktaṁ vidhyuddēśēnēti । nanu caivaṁ siddhārthatā prāpnōti,
na kāryārthatā । kimidaṁ siddhārthatā na kāryārthatēti ?
uktam—na kāryārthatayā pratīyata iti । kutastarhi kāryārthatāvagatiḥ﻿<pb n="20"/>
vidhyuddēśāditi brūmaḥ । maivaṁ vōcaḥ, nāyamabhisaṁbandhō vivakṣitaḥ
ālabhēta bhūtikāma iti । ālabhēta yatastatō bhūtiḥ—iti ।
kimanēnōktam ? na vidhyuddēśāt kāryāvagatiḥ । kiṁ tarhi ?
sastutipadāditi vadāmaḥ । taduktaṁ<q>—bhinnāvimāvarthāviti ।</q>
kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ—syādvidhyuddēśādēva kāryāvagatiḥ yadyē-
karūpāvagatiḥ syāt sastutipadāt kēvalapadācca । iha tvanyarūpai-
vāvasīyatē । ālabhēta bhūtikāma ityēkō'vagatyupāyaḥ । ālabhēta
yataḥ tatō bhūtirityayamanyaḥ । ayamapi cōdvidyāt kathamānartha-
kyamatadarthānām ।</p>﻿<pb n="21"/>
<p><q>kimarthā stutiriti cēt ?</q> iti tulyē kāryāvagamē kimupāyāntarā-
śrayaṇēna । kathaṁ cōpāyāntaratvaṁ ? kasyātrōpālambhaḥ, kēna vēdamāśritaṁ﻿<pb n="22"/>
kēna cōtpāditam kintu śabdādēvāvagamyatē । anēkapadābhidhānē hi
na padāntaranirapēkṣādarthāvagatirdr̥ṣṭā । tathā darśitam-<quote>paṭō bhavati raktaḥ paṭō
bhavati</quote> iti । na raktapadanirapēkṣāt padadvayādavagatiḥ dr̥śyatē । saiṣā
autpattikī śaktiriti ।।</p>﻿<pb n="23"/>
<p>nanu ca vināpi tēna sidhyēditi punarānarthakyamēva cōditam ।
satyaṁ vakturayamupālaṁbhaḥ na pratipattuḥ; na ca tairvinā pratipattirityuktam;
pratipattāraśca vayam na vaktāraḥ, vēdē vaktā nāstītyuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="24"/>
<p>nanu ca satsvapi stutipadēṣu pūrvasya vidhisarūpattvāt vidhirabhiprētaḥ
syāt; na vivakṣyēta stutipadasaṁbandha iti kimatra cōditam ? । idamatra
cōditam । kimavāntaravākyānvayō nāsti padārthānvayavādinō hi
naivēdamarthāntaram ।</p>
<p>anarthāntaratvē ca siddhaiva । avāntarānvayāt kāryāvagati-
rnasiddhyati । sakalapadārthāvagatau satyāṁ kathamavāntarānvayasya nimittatā
śakyatē kalpayitum । tasmāt sakalapadapadārthānvayanimittaiva kāryāvagatiḥ﻿<pb n="25"/>
na avāntarānvayanimittā bhavitumarhati ।</p>
<p>1<q>nanu nirapēkṣādvidhimavagamiṣyāma iti ।</q> kimidamanuktamuktam ।
<q>idamanuktamuktam ।</q> nanvavāntarānvayasyāpi nimittatvamabhyupagataṁ
bhavatā । bāḍhamabhyupagatam । kō dōṣaḥ ? nanvayaṁ dōṣaḥ । atrāpi
tadapahnōtuṁ na śakyatē । satyaṁ, pratīyamānaṁ hyapanhōtuṁ na śakyatē na
punarapratīyamānamapi । na cātrāvagatidvayamasti vākyabhēdaprasaṅgādi-
tyuktam । <q>atha yaduktam na ca kriyā'vagamyatē, kriyāsaṁbaddhaṁ vā
kiṁciditi ।</q> nanu kartavyatā stutipadānna gamyatē । kartavyatāṁ ca
vēdaḥ pratipādayatītyavaidikatvam ।</p>﻿<pb n="26"/>
kēna cōktaṁ vaidikatvaṁ ? vēda ēvāyaṁ, yatō hi kartavyatā'vagamyatē sa
vēdaḥ asmācca kartavyatāvagamyata ityuktam । prāmāṇyasya cāyamākṣēpaḥ
kr̥taḥ । sa cāyaṁ pratisamāhitaḥ । kimatra vaidikatvēna ।</p>
<p>nanvēvaṁ sati vidhyuddēśasyāpyavaidikatvaṁ, tadapi hi pratipattau
nimittam, asāvapi vēda ēva । bāḍhaṁ nimittatayā, na tu naimittikatayā,
stutipadārthastu nimittamēvēti viśēṣaḥ ।।</p>﻿<pb n="27"/>
<p>tulyaṁ ca sāṁpradāyikam ।।</q> kadācidiyamāśaṅkā syāt vidhyuddēśa-
stutyarthaṁ bālānāṁ pravr̥ttayē prakṣiptānyarthavādapadānīti । tadayuktam ।
tulyaṁ ca sāṁpradāyikam । naiva kaścit prakṣēpamarthavādapadānāṁ smarati ।﻿<pb n="28"/>
vidhyuddēśānāmivāvagatyantaraṁ nāstītyuktam । ēvaṁ cēdrōdanānupapattiḥ parihr̥tā ।
pratyuta kāryāvagatāvayaṁ dōṣaḥ na punaḥ siddhārthāvagatau ।।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṁ sati pramāṇamātraparyavasāyiṣu arthavādapadēṣu mr̥gyaṁ pramā-
ṇāntaraṁ stutyavagatau, na ca tadasti yathā avakā vidhīyantē āpaśca stūyantē ।﻿<pb n="29"/>
ēvaṁ cārudati rōditīti śabdaḥ । ēvaṁ sarvatra stēnādiṣu ।
tasmāt punarapyanupapattirēva ।। nēyamanupapattiḥ । vidhyarthēnaikavākyatvē
sati yathā pramāṇāntarēṇa saṁbandhō'vagamyatē tathā vyākhyēyam । taduktam
—guṇavādastviti । hētupracayaparihārastu hētuvadēvāvagantavyaḥ ।।</p>﻿<pb n="30"/>﻿<pb n="31"/>﻿<pb n="32"/>﻿<pb n="33"/>﻿<pb n="34"/>
<p><q>vidhirvā syādapūrvatvādvādamātraṁ hyanarthakam ।</q> uktaṁ bhūtārthānāṁ
kāryārthapratipādakatayā prāmāṇyam । yatra punaḥ kāryataivāvagamyatē
kāryāntarēṇa caikavākyatvaṁ tatra kathaṁ ? yathā 'auduṁbarō yūpō bhavati'
iti । <quote>ūrgvā uduṁbara urk paśavaḥ ūrjaivāsmā ūrjaṁ paśūnāpnōti
ūrjō'varudhyai</quote> iti yūpōduṁbarayōḥ sādhyasādhanatā'vagamyatē, paśūduṁbarayōrapi ।
gamyatē ca ēkavākyatvaṁ yasmādudumbarēṇa paśavaḥ sādhyantē tasmādaudumbarō
yūpaḥ kartavya iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="35"/>
<p>kimatra yuktam । sādhyāvagamē saṁbhavati siddhāvagatirna yuktā ।
kasmāt ? vidhyarthatvādvākyasya vidhēśca sādhyākāṁkṣitvāt । na caṁ
mukhyē'rthē saṁbhavati lakṣaṇā yuktā ।।</p>
<p>nanu ca sādhyadvayamēkasmin vākyē na saṁbhavati । vayamapyētadēva
brūmaḥ । tasmānnibījamēvēdamarthadvayaṁ pratīyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="36"/>﻿<pb n="37"/>
<p>nanu cānēkasminnapi pratipādyē'rthē saṁbhavati ēkavākyatā dr̥ṣṭā
yathā dēvadatta gauḥ krayyētyēvamādiṣu laukikēṣu vākyēṣu । viṣama
upanyāsaḥ tatra hi arthavaśādvākyanirṇayaḥ । iha tu śabdādēvāvagantavyaḥ ।
ataḥ saṁbhavadvidhēyānāṁ stutyarthēna prāmāṇyaṁ durghaṭam ।।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē-<q>uktaṁ tu vākyaśēṣatvam ।।</q> satyamuktaṁ, tattu nōpapadyatē;
dvayōḥ sādhyatvēnāvagamādityapyuktam । kimidaṁ viruddhaṁ pralapyatē ।﻿<pb n="38"/>
na hi dvayōḥ sādhyayōḥ guṇayōriva samatvāt saṁbandhaḥ । kathaṁ
tarhyēkārthāvagatiḥ ? yadyavagatirasti tadanurūpaṁ nimittaṁ kalpanī-
yam ।। nanu ca sādhyadvayaṁ pratīyatē । na tarhyēkārthāvagatiḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="39"/>
<p>asti cēyam । yasmādanēnēdaṁ bhavati tasmādanēnēdaṁ kuryāditi । siddhaṁ
tarhi bhavatītyasyārthasya siddhārthatvam । kathaṁ siddhasya bhavatīti vyapadēśaḥ ?
pramāṇāntarataḥ siddhiratrōpayujyatē nārthataḥ siddhiḥ । siddhamasiddhaṁ
vā pramāṇāntarapramitamarthāntarāvagatau nimittatāṁ pratipadyatē । tasmādēkārtha-
tvāt siddhaṁ prāmāṇyamatrāpi ।।</p>﻿<pb n="40"/>
<head>vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvacit ।।</head>
<p>nanu ca vidhyasambhavādēvādhastyē'dhikaraṇē pramāṇamātraparyavasāyitvaṁ-
muktamarthavādānām; iha tu pramēyatāstītyāśaṅkitaṁ, nirastaṁ ca । kimidamucyatē
<q>vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvaciditi ?</q> kvavā vidhērarthavattvē sambhavati kēvalaṁ pramāṇa-
tōktā yēnēdamucyatē 'vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvacit iti । tatsāmānyāditi ।
kimidaṁ tatsāmānyam ? vidhisambhavaḥ ēvātra pradarśitaḥ nāsambhavaḥ ।
ayathārthagrāhiṇa idaṁ cōdyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="41"/>
<p>atrāpi sādhyadvayamupanyasyatā vidhēyasya stutyarthatā nāvagamyata
ityuktam । yatra vidhēyāsambaddhā stutiravagamyatē na tatra stutyarthēnēti
śakyatē vaktum । tadidamucyatē—<q>vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvaciditi ।</q> na hi
vētasē vidhēyē āpaḥ śāntā iti stutirupapadyatē । na cāpsu jāyanta iti
vidhiḥ sambhavati, tathāpyēkārthāvagatēḥ nimittatvaṁ parikalpyatē ēvamatrāpi
bhavitumarhatīti । idaṁ tatsāmānyam । <q>prakaraṇē ca sambhavanniti ।﻿<pb n="42"/>
<p>kimanēnōpanyastam ? idamanēnōparanyastam—ēkavidhyarthatvē sambha-
vati nānēkavidhyarthatā yuktā kalpayitum; viniyōjakavirōdhāt ।﻿<pb n="43"/>
viniyōgamātrāpēkṣī viniyōjakaḥ sa na śakyatē viniyōgabhēdāt anyathā-
kartum, tadanyathātvē pauruṣēyī kalpanā prāpnōti । kiñca vidhyantaratōpi vākya-
bhēdaḥ prāpnōti । kiṁ jātam ? ēkārthāvagatērbādhaḥ । bādhyatām, na niyōgō
viniyōgaṁ bādhitumarhati । kāryatō hi bādhaṁ bādhavidō manyantē ।﻿<pb n="44"/>
tasmādvastutaḥ sādhyadvayāvagamēpi pramāṇataḥ siddhasādhyatayaiva hi ēkārthā-
vagatiriti sthitamēvaṁvidhēṣvapi pramāṇatvam ।</p>
<p><q>hēturvā syādarthavattvōpapattibhyām ।</q> kā punaratrāprāmāṇyaśaṅkā ?
yadi hētvarthaḥ karaṇaṁ yadi vā śūrpārthaḥ ubhayathāpi anvitapadārthakō vākyārthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="45"/>
ananvayini hi padārthē nimittatayā naimittikatayā vā pratibhā-
mātram । ataścāprāmāṇyaṁ na tvanvayini । tasmāt pramāṇalakṣaṇāntaḥ
pātitā kathamasyādhikaraṇasya ? । na cārthāntaraṁ yuktamatrārpayitum,
prasaṅgābhāvāt anaupōdghātikatvācca ।</p>
<p>nanu cāyamastyēva prasaṅgaḥ kimarthavādō nēti । satyamasti
niṣprayōjanastu saḥ । nanu cēdamasti prayōjanaṁ arthavādatvē śūrpēṇaiva hōmaḥ﻿<pb n="46"/>
itarathā hyaniyama iti । satyamastīdaṁ prayōjanaṁ tārtīyaṁ tvētat ।
na ca lakṣaṇāntaraprayuktaṁ prāsaṅgikaṁ bhavitumarhati । cintitaṁ
caitannivītaṁ manuṣyāṇāmityēvamādiṣu । tasmāt pramāṇalakṣaṇāntaḥ
pātitaivāsya vaktavyā ।</p>
<p>sēyamucyatē—hētupakṣē hi tannimittaṁ karaṇatvaṁ jñāyatē । yadi
vēdātsiddhaṁ tarhi vaidikatvam । satyaṁ siddham; sāpēkṣantu । sāpēkṣatvē
ca pramāṇāntaraṁ mr̥gyam । na ca tadastīti pratibhāmātram । tasmā-
ddhētutvamidānīṁ pratipadyatē । hēturayam kāryatvēnānvayasambhavāt । na
pramāṇamātraparyavasāyitā śakyatē vaktuṁm, kāryārthatvādanvayasya ।</p>﻿<pb n="47"/>
<p>nanu ca śūrpasyānnakaraṇatā na sambhavati । asādhakatamatvāt
vyāpr̥tasya cānyatrākaraṇatvāt । upapadyatē hi karaṇatvamāpēkṣikatayā । āpē-
kṣikī hi vivakṣā, vivakṣātaśca kārakāṇi bhavantīti kārakajñāḥ । vartamānakāla-
tāpyasya āpēkṣikyēvētyuktaṁ kālajñaiḥ । tasmādupapannō'yam-arthavattvōpapatti-
bhyamiti । avaśyaṁ cāyamāpēkṣikakaraṇabhāvō grahītavyaḥ; stutāvapi tulyatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>stutistu śabdapūrvatvādacōdanā ca tasya ।</q> atrōcyatē—nāyaṁ
hētuḥ । kasmāt ? śūrpahōmē hi hētuḥ pratīyatē । siddhaśca﻿<pb n="48"/>
hētuḥ na sādhyatayā'vagantuṁ śakyatē । hōmasya ca sādhyāvagatirvēdāt ।
na ca sādhyatvēnāvagamyamānō vēdāt sāpēkṣō bhavati । tasmāt hētuvadēvāyaṁ
na hētuḥ । ēvaṁ ca kr̥tvā avartamānō'pi vartamānatayā pratipattuṁ śakyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="49"/>
<p>nanu ca vartamāna ēva nāstītyuktam ? kēna cōktaṁ nāstīti । phala-
paryanta ārambhō vartamānavyapadēśaṁ bhajatīti sthitam । na punarvidhipakṣa
ētadupapadyatē । na hyarthāntarē prayōgaḥ śakyatē nirūpayitum ।
āpēkṣikatvaṁ ca karaṇasya madīya ēva pakṣē śakyatē nirūpayitum ।
vidhipakṣē hi kriyāntaratā kēna vāryatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="50"/>
<p>śūrpaśabdāditi cēt nivr̥ttāstarhi darvīpiṭharādayaḥ vyāhataśca
hētvarthō bhavati । ata ēvamuktam—yadi ca hēturavatiṣṭhēta
nirdēśācchūrpa ēvēti । hētvavyāghāta iti cēt—avyavasthā
tarhi । avyavasthāyā api sa ēva hēturvyāghātaḥ nivartyābhāvāt ।﻿<pb n="b051"/>
kārakasya hētōḥ nivartyābhāvēpyātmalābhō jñāpakasyēva । tasmāddhētuvanni-
gadānāmapi pramāṇatayaivāvasthānam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b052"/>
<p><q>tadarthaśāstrāt ।</q> yaduktaṁ <quote>‘dr̥ṣṭō hi tasyārthaḥ karmāvabōdhanaṁ
nāma’</quote> iti tadayuktam । avivakṣitārthatvaṁ svādhyāyasya mantrēṣu
dr̥śyatē kathamavivakṣitārthatvam ? tadarthaśāstravirōdhādibhiḥ navabhiḥ
pradarśyatē । nanu cāvivakṣitārthatvē tadarthaśāstrādayōpyavivakṣitārthā ēva ।</p>﻿<pb n="b053"/>
ōmityucyatē । kathaṁ tarhi tairavivakṣitārthatvam ? parasparavyāghātāda&mdash;
sambaddhārthataiva avivakṣāhētuḥ । yadi mantrā avivakṣitārthāḥ tadā tadartha-
śāstrāṇāmavivakṣitārthatvamiti parasparavyāghātaḥ । raśanābhidhānavivakṣāyāṁ﻿<pb n="b054"/>
<p><quote>‘aśvābhidhānīmādatta’</quote> ityasya tadarthaśāstrasya vyāghātaḥ । na ca
parisaṅkhayādibhiḥ śakyatē vyāghātaḥ parihartumiti pradarśitam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b055"/>﻿<pb n="b056"/>﻿<pb n="b057"/>
<p><q>aviśiṣṭastu vākyārthaḥ ।</q> atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;nāvivakṣitārthaḥ
svādhyāyaḥ । niyōgasambandhitayā svādhyāyasyārthavattā uk‍tā kāryē
prāmāṇyābhidhānāt kāryārthābhidhānatayā paraprayōgēpi ।</p>﻿<pb n="b058"/>
<p>kimidaṁ prayōga iti ? anuṣṭhānamityarthaḥ । anuṣṭhīyamānārthaupayi-
katayā vivakṣitārthatvamavagamyamānaṁ na śakyatē tadarthaśāstradibhirvihantum ।
prāptārthānuvādakānyapi vākyāni dr̥śyantē <quote>‘ya ēvaṁ vidvān paurṇaṁmāsīṁ yajata’</quote>﻿<pb n="b059"/>﻿<pb n="b060"/>﻿<pb n="b061"/>﻿<pb n="b062"/>
ityēvamādīni । na caitānyatadarthakāni iti pradarśitaṁ dēvatāvidhānādibhiḥ
viśēṣaiḥ । ēvaṁ pratisūtraṁ draṣṭavyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b063"/>
asya cārthasya nyāyyatvaṁ vaidikānyapi liṅgadarśanāni upō-
dvalayanti <quote>‘āgnēyyā āgnīdhramupatiṣṭhatē’</quote> ityēvamādīni ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ prathamādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b064"/>
<head>atha tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapēkṣaṁ syāt</q>&mdash;kimidamaprastutaṁ
cintyatē ? kimaprastutam ? acōdanārthavicāraḥ bravīti ca
dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapēkṣaṁ syāt iti । aśabdaścēnna
pratijñātaṁ; apratijñātacintā ca pratijñāṁ vihanti । pūrvāparavirōdhāccā-
﻿<pb n="b065"/>
buddhipūrvakatā prāpnōti । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;idamapi vēdavidbhiḥ
pramāṇatayā parigr̥hītam । tasmādidamapi vicāraṇīyamiti । tada-
yuk‍tam । pratyakṣādyapi taiḥ pramāṇatayā parigr̥hītaṁ tadapi vicāraṇīyaṁ
prāpnōti । <q>nanu ca</q> vicāritamētat । kva vicāritam ? satsaṁprayōgē
puruṣāṇāmityaṁtra pramāṇamiti । kiṁ pratyakṣaṁ pramāṇamapramāṇamityasya
saṁśayasya nirṇayāya tatsūtram ? dharmaṁ prati pramāṇaṁ na bhavatītyētatparaṁ
﻿<pb n="b066"/>
sūtraṁ, na tarhi pramāṇāntaraṁ pramāṇatayā cintitamasmin śās‍trē ।
tasmātpratijñātaṁ cintanīyaṁ nābhyupagataṁ apratijñātaṁ ca smr̥tiśāstram ।
atō'saṁbadvaivēyaṁ cintā ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē-pratijñātārthasya cintēyam । nanu ca svatantraśabda-
viṣayā sā pratijñā na cātra svātantryamasti । satyaṁ, svātantryaṁ nāsti
svatantraśabdaviṣayaivēyaṁ cintā । kimaṣṭakā kartavyēti svatantraśabdaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b067"/>
nāyaṁ svatantraśabdaḥ svatantraśabdasambandhastu । kēna svatantrēṇāsya
sambandhaḥ ? yāṁ janāḥ pratinandantīti । tataḥ kim ? sāpēkṣapara-
tantratvāt asyāpi sādhakatā prāpnōti tatsāmānyāccētarēṣāmapi । tadi-
damāha&mdash;<q>dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapēkṣaṁ syāt iti ।</q> apē-
kṣitaṁ caitat yāṁ janāḥ pratinandantītyēvamādibhiḥ । ata ēṣāmaśabdataivēti
﻿<pb n="b068"/>
sa ēva pratijñātārthaḥ punarākṣipyatē । na sāpēkṣānapēkṣayōḥ
ēkārthatvaṁ saṁbhavatītyuk‍taṁ viṣayabhēdāditi ।</p>
<p>nanu cātra viṣayabhēda ēva na saṁbhavati dvayōḥ kāryārthatvāt
tadēva hi na saṁbhavatītyucyatē । nanu ca kāryārthasyaiva anumānaṁ
bhaviṣyati । tatparityāgē kāraṇaṁ vak‍tavyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b069"/>
<p>nanu ca kāryāvagatirapi tyak‍taṁ na śakyatē tadānupūrvyasiddhamanu-
mānaṁ kēna vāryatē; satyaṁ na vāryatē yadyatra smaraṇābhimānō na syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b070"/>
smaraṇābhimānē kō dōṣaḥ ? smaraṇādanumānaṁ prāpnōti na kāryataḥ । kiṁ
tataḥ ? smaraṇaṁ hi pramāṇaviṣayaṁ nārthaviṣayaṁ; kimiti ? tatpurassaratvādartha-
saṁvidaḥ । siddhaṁ tarhi prāmāṇyaṁ; nēti brūmaḥ ayathārthatvēpi saṁbhavāt ।
﻿<pb n="b071"/>
tasmānna kāryatō'numānasiddhiḥ&mdash;asmākaṁ cēdamanumānam । na cāsmākaṁ
smaraṇavyavadhānādidamupapadyatē na kāryaṁ smaraṇasambandhi kāraṇasambandhi
tata । na ca vyavahitasya nirapēkṣaṁ tadastītyanapēkṣam । tasmādvandhyā&mdash;
sutasmaraṇatulyamidaṁ kāryam । nanu cānidaṁprathamatāpi tathātvē hēturdr̥ṣṭā-yathā
śabdārthāvagatau vēdō'yaṁ brāhmaṇō'yamiti । viṣama upanyāsaḥ
dr̥ṣṭē'rthē'nidaṁprathamatā yuktā । arthadarśanamēva hi tatra mūlatāṁ
﻿<pb n="b072"/>
pratipadyata iti । iha tu tasyābhāvaḥ । tasmānmr̥gyamatra pramāṇāntaraṁ
na ca tatpramāṇāntaramastītyuktam । tasmādacōdanālakṣaṇō dharmaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>api vā kartr̥sāmānyāt pramāṇamanumānaṁ syāt ।</q> nā-
pramāṇaṁ cōdanā, pramāṇasya hi tathātvē'vagatirēva kāraṇam । ayathārthatvē
punaḥ duṣṭakāraṇatā viparyayaśca । sēyaṁ tāvadavagatirasti na ca viparyayaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b073"/>
nanu ca kāraṇābhāvāt duṣṭakāraṇatānvayaḥ; kimabhāvaḥ kāraṇē śakyatē
vak‍tuṁ; kimiti na śakyatē ? vēdasaṁyōgasya saṁbhavāt; satyaṁ
kāraṇasyābhāvō na śakyatē vak‍tum । bhāvō'pi naiva ।</p>
<p>nanu kāryata ēvāvagamyatē kāraṇasya bhāvaḥ na, smaraṇavyavadhānādi&mdash;
tyuktam । kimidaṁ smaraṇavyavadhānāditi ? idaṁ tat, smaraṇaṁ hyatra pramāṇa-﻿<pb n="b074"/>
tayōpalabhyatē । tataḥ kiṁ ? tadgatamēva prāmāṇyamanumātuṁ śakyatē na
śabdagatam । upalabdhasya hi kāraṇasya śaktyanumānaṁ kāryataḥ nānupa-
labdhasya । nanu ca smaraṇamēva nōpapadyata iti kāraṇāntarānumānaṁ; kasya ?
kāryasya । maivaṁ vōcaḥ, na smaraṇaṁ kāraṇamityuktam । smaraṇasya tarhi
kāraṇāntarānumānam । kimāyātaṁ kāryasya ? । na hyanyakāraṇamanyasya
﻿<pb n="b075"/>
bhavitumarhati । nanu ca praṇāḍyā bhaviṣyati । kāraṇatastarhi kāryaṁ vijñēyaṁ
na kāryataḥ kāraṇaṁ; kāryaṁ hi kāraṇamātraparyavasāyi na tatastatpraṇāḍīmapēkṣatē ।
kāraṇaniṣpattirhi kāryōtpattau hētuḥ na tanniṣpādakamapi । asamba-
ndhasya cānumānē'vyavasthā prāpnōti । nanu ca niyatakāraṇakāraṇakaṁ hi
﻿<pb n="b076"/>
yatkāryaṁ tat kāraṇakāraṇamapyavagamayati; naivaṁ, tāvadēva hi tatra
kāraṇam । kimēvaṁ smr̥tēḥ śabdakāraṇakāraṇataivāsmin kāryē ?
ōmityucyatē, siddhaṁ tarhi caityavandanādīnāmapi prāmāṇyam ।
﻿<pb n="b077"/>
na, anabhyupagamāditi cēt, na tarhi kāryatō viśiṣṭakāraṇānu-
mānaṁ, tasmāt pramāṇāntaraṁ mr̥gyam । na ca tadastītyuktam ।
tadidaṁ vandhyāsutasmaraṇavadakāraṇaṁ na tatsmaraṇaṁ karaṇībhavitumarhati ।
﻿<pb n="b078"/>
tasmāt duṣṭakāraṇataivātra sthitā । tasmādaprāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p>ahō anavasitanayanītijñō bhavān । kimiti ? kāryata&mdash;
stāvat smaraṇē śaktirasti । smaraṇamidānīmakāraṇamityakāraṇatā
smaraṇē'dhyavasīyatē । na ca tadakāraṇatvaṁ smaraṇē'dhyavasātuṁ śakyatē
saṁbhavādvēdasaṁyōgasya, kāraṇāntarasya cāsaṁbhavāt asmin kāryē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b079"/>
﻿<pb n="b080"/>
caityavandanādiṣvasaṁbhavāt na punarasmadīyaṁ kāryatō'numānam । tasmāda-
tantramanupalabdhirgranthaviṣayā । vismaraṇōpapattēśca pratipat‍tuḥ । tasmā-
davyāhatamanapēkṣatvaṁ cōdanāyāḥ । yatpunaridamuk‍taṁ <quote>‘yāṁ janāḥ
pratinandanti’</quote> ityaṣṭakāliṅgā mantrā iti । tadanupapannaṁ; kutaḥ,
tadēkavākyatayaivāprāmāṇyamuktam । kathaṁ tadēva prāmāṇyahētutayōpanyasyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b081"/>
naivēdaṁ prāmāṇyahētutayōpanyastam, vēdasaṁyōgasya tu saṁbhavē liṅgam । kathaṁ
kr̥tvā talliṅgaṁ ? talliṅgāpēkṣaṁ dēvatābhidhānaṁ karmaṇi । tasmānmāntravarṇikīṁ
dēvatāṁ anuvadan vēdasaṁyōgamupōdvalayati । yatpunaridamuk‍taṁ yē dr̥ṣṭārthāstē
tata ēvēti, asadidamuktaṁ; kimatrāsaduktam ? bāḍhamatiśayēnāsaduktam ।
adhyayanavidhēḥ pramāṇāntarāpēkṣitōk‍tā bhavati । svarūpē vā kēna vāritama-﻿<pb n="b082"/>
vaghātādēriva dr̥ṣṭārthatvam । kathaṁ tarhi uparitanē'dhikaraṇē dr̥ṣṭārthatvāda-
prāmāṇyam ? tatraiva viśēṣaṁ vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>virōdhē tvanapēkṣaṁ syādasati hyanumānam ।</q> yadi saṁbhavati vēda-
saṁprayōgē'pratihataṁ kāryānumānaṁ smr̥tāviti prāmāṇyaṁ vēdasyāprāmāṇyamapi
﻿<pb n="b083"/>
anayaiva yuk‍tyā prasak‍tam । kathaṁ ? virōdhāt । virōdhō'pi ca
smr̥tyā saha vēda upalabhyatē । virōdhē cāprāmāṇyaṁ parasparavyāghātāt ।
yathā audumbaryāḥ sarvavēṣṭanaṁ sparśanēna । satyamēvaṁ yadyanyataḥ kāryānumāna-
vighātō na syāt । kutō'nyataḥ ? viruddhādēva vaidikādvacasaḥ,
﻿<pb n="b084"/>
sākṣādvēdapratipāditē hyarthē na tadvirōdhi sāpēkṣaṁ puṁvacaḥ prabhāṇaṁ bhavitumarhati ।
pramāṇāntarānavacchinnē pramāṇaṁ pramāṇaṁ bhavati na punaḥ tadavacchinnēpi । siddha-
sādhyavyavasthāyā hi bādhaṁ naiyāyikā manyantē । na siddhaṁ sādhyēna bādhyatē
siddhēna hi sādhyaṁ bādhyatē । siddhaścāyaṁ vaidikō'rthaḥ pratyakṣāvagamyakāraṇatvāt na
viruddhakāraṇaviṣayamanumānamātmānaṁ labhatē agnāviva śaityānumānam ।
﻿<pb n="b085"/>
tasmānna virōdhē prāmāṇyaṁ smr̥tēḥ । aprāmāṇyāccāvirōdhaḥ । avirōdhāccāvighātaḥ ।
avyāghātāccāvihataṁ prāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ । nanu ca kāryārthatvē śabdasya
kō virōdhaḥ ? kāryadvayaṁ hi pratīyamānaṁ ēkārthamapi vikalpēnānuṣṭhīyamānaṁ
﻿<pb n="b086"/>
na parasparaṁ vyāhantumutsahatē । satattvaṁ hi vastunaḥ siddhasya viruddhamavagamyamānaṁ
parasparavyāghātaṁ saṁvidaḥ upajanayati । kāryaṁ punarēkatayā pratipat‍tuṁ na śakyatē
anubandhādibhirbhēdēnaivāvagamāt । bhinnānubandhaṁ ca na svarūpē virōdhamāvahati
ēkakāryatvāc‍ca yugapadanuṣṭhānavirōdhamātraṁ, nirjñātasvarūpasya hi karmaṇō'nu-
ṣṭhānaṁ, anuṣṭhānavirīdhaśca vikalpēnaiva parihr̥taḥ prasaṅgāt kāryasiddhēḥ । tasmā-
dvirōdha ēvātra nāsti kāryārthatvācchabdasya । kimidamaprāmāṇyamāśaṅkayatē
nirākriyatē ca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b087"/>
<p>satyaṁ bhavēdētadēvaṁ yadyanuṣṭhānavirōdhē kāryavirōdhō na syāt । nanūk‍taṁ
vr̥hadrathantarādiṣu anuṣṭhānavirōdhē satyapi kāryavirōdhō na jāyata iti ।
anabhijñō bhavān vaikalpikānāṁ padārthānāṁ; anuṣṭhānamēva hi kāryamityucyatē ।
tadvirōdhē kāryavirōdhō nāstīti pralāpaḥ ।</p>
<p>kathaṁ tarhi punaḥ punaranuṣṭhānaṁ bahubhiśca । tathaivāvagamāt kāryasya ।
vyāghātastarhi vrīhibhiryajēta yavairyajētēti । bāḍham, kathaṁ tarhi prāmāṇyaṁ ?
uk‍tamanapēkṣatvāditi । kimanapēkṣatā vyāghātē [prāmāṇyē] kariṣyati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b088"/>
vyāghātō hi parasparaviparyayamāpādayati viparyayaśca mūrdhābhiṣik‍tamaprāmāṇyē ।
satyamēvam । iha tu viparyaya ēvātmānaṁ na labhatē ubhayōranapēkṣatvāt । na
tarhi vyāghātaḥ । kathaṁ na vyāghātaḥ ? ēkatvādanuṣṭhānasyaikaśabdāt । kimidaṁ
mahēndrajālōpamam ? idamidaṁ ēkatvācchāstrasya ; tataśca virōdhāvagatēstathaiva ।
﻿<pb n="b089"/>
tatsmr̥tistu na tathā । kutaḥ aprasiddhērēkatāyāḥ । ānumānikaṁ hi tatra
kāraṇaṁ anugatē ca pratyarthini nānumānamātmānaṁ labhatē ityuk‍tam ।
tasmāditarētarāśrayatātra vyāhatā siddhē nēti vaiṣamyam । tasmāt smr̥ti-
﻿<pb n="b090"/>
mukhamaprāmōṇyaṁ niṣiddhaṁ cōdanāyāḥ pramāṇāntarōpalabhyamānakāraṇatayā'numāna-
pratiṣēdhaḥ । taduk‍tam&mdash;</p>
<p><q>hētudarśanācca</q> iti । adhikaraṇāntaraṁ vēti kō'rthaḥ ?
ayamarthaḥ । pūrvayuk‍tinirapēkṣaṁ yuk‍tyabhidhānam । yuktyantarāpēkṣiṇī yuk‍tiḥ
pūrvamuk‍tā । iha punaḥ nirapēkṣatayā'bhidhīyamānā'dhikaraṇāntaramityucyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b091"/>
kathaṁ punaḥ yuk‍tyantaranirapēkṣaṁ kāryānumānavirōdhē hētudarśanaṁ ? hētu&mdash;
darśanādēva । na hi dr̥ṣṭē hētau hētvantarānumānaṁ kramatē । dr̥ṣṭō'tra
lōbha ēva hētuḥ । tasmāt dr̥ṣṭē hētau na vaidikānumānaṁ viruddhama-
viruddhaṁ vā bhavati । asati vēdānumānē dr̥ṣṭakāraṇānāṁ vaidikaprayōga-
grāhyatvaṁ kimasti । astu; kka tarhi aprāmāṇ‍yābhidhānamupayujyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b092"/>
adr̥ṣṭōpakāriṇō na gr̥hyantē dr̥ṣṭārthāstu gr̥hyanta iti viṣayabhēdaḥ tasmāda-
dr̥ṣṭārtham । dr̥ṣṭakāraṇamapramāṇamiti yuk‍tamaprāmāṇyābhidhānam । taduk‍taṁ
vaisarjanahōmīyasya vāsasō dr̥ṣṭārthaṁ dānam ।</p>
<p><q>śiṣṭākōpē'viruddhamiti cēt ।</q> virōdhāvirōdhaparihārēṇa sthitaṁ
prāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ । sa ēvāyaṁ virōdhaḥ kvāsti kva nāstīti
﻿<pb n="b093"/>
cintyatē hānōpādānārtham । viṣayavyāptidarśanaṁ kimarthaṁ ? nyāyasvarūpābhidhā-
na paraṁ hyētacchāstraṁ na lakṣyaniṣṭham । satyam yathā bhavānāha । nyāyasvarūpā-
bhidhānamēvēdaṁ viṣayavyāptyā pradarśyatē, svarūpē'bhihitēpi nyāyasya kasmiṁ-
ścidviṣayē'sadiva pratibhāti kāryadhiyām । ataḥ tadapanuttayē kr̥tadhībhirayaṁ
yat‍naḥ kr̥taḥ । yathā'sminnēvōdāharaṇē kramakālavirōdhaṁ manvānasya﻿<pb n="b094"/>
viruddhamācamanādi pratibhāti । kathaṁ ? yathāśrutasyārthasya vidhivitāna-
vaśādanuṣṭhānamiti sthitaṁ kramalakṣaṇē । pratyakṣavidhivitānavirōdhāt
virōdhaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b095"/>
<p>atrōcyatē śāstrārthavirōdhē virōdhaḥ । śāstraṁ ca kāryārthaṁ na
vidhivitānārthāmit‍yuk‍taṁ dvitīyē sūtrē । kāryamēva vitataṁ pratīyatē nityaṁ
kāryaparatantratvāt vitānasya, na svātantryēṇa pramēyatā kāryasya ca
kāryāntarēṇa virōdhaḥ, na padārthavaitatyēna tad‍guṇatvāt । kālē kathaṁ ?
kālō'pi hi pracayaḥ kāryāṇām । atastadapēkṣatvāt na viruddhayatē
<quote>“api ca prāptānāṁ padārthānāmuttarakālaṁ krama āpatati yadā padārthāḥ
prāp‍nuvanti tadā krama ēva nāsti”</quote>। kimanēnānabhihitamabhihitam ? sa
ēva hi guṇabhāvaḥ kamasya pratipāditaḥ। sa cōk‍tatvānna pratipādanīyaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b096"/>
<p>astyatrābhiprāyaḥ&mdash;na ca vitānapracayāvēva kramakālāviti
manyatē । kathaṁ ? paurṇamāsyāṁ paurṇamāsyā yajēta kaḥ pracayō'tra karmaṇāṁ ?
dvitīyādiṣbapi tulyatvāt na tatpracayasya paurṇamāsītvaṁ yuk‍tam ।
kāryatayā ca kramāvagatirddaṣṭā&mdash;yathā'dhvaryurgr̥hapatiṁ dīkṣayitvēti ।
tasmānna guṇatayā parihāra upapadyatē । kāryatvāt kāryatayā ca
virōdha iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b097"/>
<p>tadidaṁ parihriyatē&mdash;kiṁ prāptē dīkṣākāryē dīkṣāvitānamavagamyatē
adhvaryurgr̥hapatimityētasmin vāk‍yē uta tatprāptinirapēkṣa ēvāyaṁ svatantraḥ
kāryatayā'vagamyatē samidādivat । na hi kāryamantarēṇa kāryavita-
tiravagamyatē kāryasya cēdvitatiḥ na kāryāntaratayā śakyatē'vagantum ।
tasmādanavagatē kāryē vitānasyānavagamāt kēna virōdhaḥ ? kastarhi
adhvaryurgr̥hapatimityasya viṣayaḥ ? svāvasarē vakṣyāmaḥ । kālēpi cāyamēva
parihāraḥ । katha ? paurṇamāsīśabdavācyaṁ kimabhiprētamāyuṣ‍mataḥ tatrāpi kriyā-
pracitirēva saṁyōgavibhāgajā grahāṇām । iyāṁstu viśēṣaḥ cōditakāryapraciti-
﻿<pb n="b098"/>
rēkatrāṅgam । kiyāntarapracitiranyatra । tatra kriyāntarapracityā
tāvadavirōdhaḥ । cōditakāryapracitistu kāryōṁttarakālabhāvinī । tasmāt
kramavadavirōdhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q><quote>“na cācamanādayō</q> vyavadhānaṁ kurvanti”</quote> iti pratipadārthāṅgābhi-
prāyam । sāṅgasyaiva hi padārthasya padārthāntarēṇa kramāvagatiḥ । tasmādācama-
nādyanvitā ēva vaidikāḥ prayōgāḥ pratipattavyā iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b099"/>
<p><q>tēṣ‍vadarśanādvirōdhasya samā vipratipattiḥ syāt ।</q> śabdārtha-
vipratipattau satyāṁ kimaprāmāṇyaṁ vēdasya syāt । saṁśayādapratipattēḥ ।
nanu ca sandigdhēṣu vāk‍yaśēṣādityud‍dhr̥tamidamaprāmāṇ‍yam । satyamud‍dhr̥tam ।
yatrānēkārthatayaiva sarvatra nimittabhāvaḥ prasiddhaḥ yathā'kṣādiṣu । yatra
punaḥ vipratipattyaiva kvacit kasyacinnimittatvaṁ na tatra prayōgātsaṁśayō
﻿<pb n="b100"/>
bhavati । prayōgasya ca saṁśayaṁ vāk‍yaśēṣō vyāvartayati । nābhidhānē
saṁśayam । abhidhānē cāyaṁ saṁśayaḥ । abhidhānasaṁśayaśca vyavahāra&mdash;
vipratipattyā । śabdārthavyavahāramūlaṁ ca vēdārthajñānamityuk‍tam । tēna
vyavahāravadvēdārthēpi prāptā vipratipattiḥ । na cātra vēdārthasya virōdhāt śak‍yatē
nirākartum asau vipratipattiḥ । ubhayathōpapattērvāk‍yārthasya । tasmāt
nimittavipratipattyā'nadhyavasāyaḥ । anadhyavasāyāccāprāmāṇyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b101"/>
<p><q>śāstrasthā vā tannimittatvāt ।</q> satyaṁ yadyavirōdhaḥ syāt ।
api tu kāryata ēva virōdhō'vagamyata ēva । śrūyatē hi varāhaṁ gāvō'
nudhāvantītyēvamōdiṣu vākyaśēṣēṣu । tataḥ kiṁ ? viśiṣṭanimittakānva-
yō'vagamyatē । nanu tadēvēdamāpatitaṁ vākyaśēṣānnirṇaya iti । naivēdamā-
patitam sandigdhē hi nimittē tatra nirṇayaḥ । atra punarviparyaya ēva
nirākriyatē varāhādyēvautpattikaṁ na kr̥ṣṇaśakunādīti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b102"/>
<p>nanu ca vēdādēva nimittāvagamō'bhyupagatō bhavati । na
laukikādvayavahārāta yūpādīnāmiva । ēvaṁ sati kō dōṣaḥ ? na khalu
kaścidanyō dōṣaḥ । tadēva hi vaidikanimittatvaṁ na siddhayati ।
kutaḥ ? apratipannē laukikanimittabhāvē na vēdāt pratipat‍tuṁ
śakyatē । ata ēva vaidikatvaṁ na brūmaḥ kiṁ tarhi śiṣṭaprayōga
ēva valavānityucyatē vākyaśēṣānuguṇyāt । siddhē cāsyautpatti-
katvē prayāgasyānyatō naiva tadvirōdhinī pratipattirātmānaṁ labhatē । autpattika-
﻿<pb n="b103"/>
tayā gauṇēnāpi vyavahārōpapattēḥ । yadi hi vyavahārādēva dvayōrautpattikatva-
kalpanā syāt tatrētarētarāśrayāt kalpanāvyāghātaḥ । atra tvanyataḥ śāstrīyasya
prayōgasya siddhamautpattikatvamityuk‍tam । siddhē ca tasmin pratipakṣa-
vyāghātō'vagamyatē । anumānavirōdhāt । tasmādgauṇō nārthavyavahāraḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b104"/>
<p><q>cōditantu pratīyētāvirōdhāt pramāṇēna ।</q> yadyēvamanāryavyavahāraḥ
gauṇaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi yē śabdāḥ āryavyavahārē nimittatayā na prasiddhō
tēṣāmanimittataiva vaidikē vyavahārē yathā pikanēmasatatāmarasādīnām ।
mābhūditi cēt tadēvēdamaprāmāṇyaṁ prāpnōti । nigamaniruk‍tavyākaraṇādi-
vaśādbhavatvarthāvagatiriti cēt, na; tayōḥ prayōgamūlatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b105"/>
kathaṁ tarhi prakr̥tipratyayārthōhanaṁ ? viniyōgavaśāt । viniyuk‍tasya
mantrasya vākyaśēṣībhūtasya cārthavādasya vr̥ddhavyavahāraprasiddhanimittānuvarti
prakr̥tipratyayōhanaṁ na punarūhyapadanimittaṁ vidhyuddēśavākyaṁ bhavitumarhati ।
tasmādaprāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p>satyaṁ yadi sāmānyatō dr̥ṣṭaṁ kāryānumānavirōdhi syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b106"/>
atha tu yatraiva pratyarthī vidyatē tatraiva kāryānumōnavirōdhaḥ tadā vihatapratipakṣaṁ
kēna vāryatē । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ sāmānyatō dr̥ṣṭaṁ na bhavatīti sāmānyamēva
tanna syāt apratipakṣasiddhau । tasmādapratipakṣamlēcchavyavahārasiddhamapi
nimittamēva vēdārthāvagatau । atō virōdhāvirōdhanirastapratipakṣaṁ sthitamana&mdash;
pēkṣatvaṁ cōdanāyāḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b107"/>
<p><q>prayōgaśāstramiti cēt ।</q> kiṁ punaḥ karaṇaṁ siddhasya pauruṣē-
yatayā'napēkṣatvamāśaṅkayatē । kāryataḥ pramāṇataścāśaṅkayatē kāryaṁ
paṭhitasya pāṭhaḥ śākhāntaravat, pramāṇaṁ punaḥ ācāryavacaḥ pramāṇamiti ।
nanu vipratiṣiddhamidaṁ pauruṣēyatvamanapēkṣatvaṁ cēti । kimatra vipratiṣiddham ?
yathā'vagamyantē'rthāstathā bhavanti । dvayaṁ cātrāvagamyatē pauruṣēyatvamanapēkṣatvaṁ;
smaraṇāt pauruṣēyatvaṁ, kāryavacanābhyāmanapēkṣatvam । tasmād‍dvayamastu ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b108"/>
<p><q>na, asanniyamāt ।</q> naitadupapadyatē pauruṣēyatvamanapēkṣatvaṁ cēti ।
siddhaṁ cāsya pauruṣēyatvam । na kāṭhakādivat pravacanaparihāryam ।
kr̥tiśca pramāṇāntaradr̥ṣṭārthābhidhānamēvōcyatē na varṇādikāryatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b109"/>
tasmātsāpēkṣatvam । yatpunaḥ kāryamupanyastaṁ paṭhitasya pāṭhaḥ śākhāntaravaditi,
naitacchākhāntaratulyaṁ; prayōgābhyāsaḥ kāryagamyasyāvagamyatē svaravidhyarthavīda-
parityāgāt । tadānantaryapratipattau padārthānāmavyavadhānamāvahati ।
﻿<pb n="b110"/>
avyavahitāśca pratīyamānāḥ sukhamanuṣṭhīyanta iti paṭhitasya pāṭhaprayōjana-
mācāryāṇām । ata ēva prayōgaśāstramiti vyapadiśyatē, kalpaśabdā-
bhidhēyatā; kalpanā hyatra padārthānāṁ na vidhēyatvam । avagatasya klr̥pti-
rbhavati maṇēriva । yaduk‍tamācāryavacaḥ pramāṇamiti pramāṇādavagamyata
iti tanna । apramāṇatvādasya vacanasya । na hi svarūpē śabda-
﻿<pb n="b111"/>
syānapēkṣatvamastītyuk‍taṁ kintu kāryē । tasmādanyaśēṣatvādasya vākyasya
dr̥ṣṭānusārivyākhyānaṁ yuk‍tam । vēdō vā''cāryō'bhiprētaḥ ।</p>
<p>yadvā ācāryavacaḥ pramāṇam tadvadapēkṣya । kiṁ punaḥ prayōjanaṁ
cintaṣyāḥ ? vihitakalpanāparatvādasya śāstrasya na virōdhamavagacchāmaḥ ।
astyatra vihitavirōdhinī kalpanā sarvāsu tithiṣu darśapūrṇamāsādīnāṁ
kalpanā । sā ca kālaviśēṣaśravaṇādvirudhyatē viruddhaṁ cānapēkṣyam ।
anyathā hyādarē tēna vyāghātādaprāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b112"/>
<p><b>anumānavyavasthānāttatsaṁyuk‍taṁ pramāṇaṁ syāt ।</b> iha vyavasthita-
viṣayamavyavasthitaṁ cōdāharaṇam । kimidaṁ vyavasthitaviṣayamavyavasthitaṁ
cēti ? idamidaṁ prācyōdīcyadākṣiṇātyābhimāninaḥ kurvatē । hōlākādīnā-
mēvēyaṁ vyavasthā । na cābhimānasya niyāmakaṁ kiñcidastītyavyavasthā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b113"/>
<p><q>kathaṁ punarniyāmakaṁ nāsti ?</q> vidhistāvanna niyāmakaḥ niyōga-
mātraparyavasāyī hi saḥ । karmaśabdō'pi hōlākādirna niyāmakaḥ karma-
viśēṣābhidhānāta । na cānyatkiñcit guṇō jātiḥ saṁsthānaṁ dēśō vā tada-
bhāvāt । samākhyapi naiva । nanu yō yatra jātaḥ sa tēna dēśēna samākhyāyatē
prācyēdīcyadākṣiṇātyā iti । na janmamātrātsamākhyēyaṁ āgatādiṣvapi
﻿<pb n="b114"/>
tulyatvāt na niyāmikā samākhyā । lōhitākṣādayastu niyāma&mdash;
katvavyabhicaritāḥ । kiṁ punarasyāścintāyāḥ pramāṇalakṣaṇaupayi-
katvamasti ? kathaṁ vā nāsti; na, yadi niyāmakamasti yadi vā nāsti
kiṁ jātamanapēkṣatvasya । idamēva jātam । abhimānō vidyatē । na ca
tasya mūlamupalabhyata ityaprāmāṇyaṁ pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b115"/>
<p>rāddhāntē tu nābhimānaprabhavaṁ vacanamiti parihr̥tam । yadyabhimāna-
prabhavaṁ vaidikaṁ vacanaṁ tadā bhavēdaprāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ abhimānasya ca
mūlaṁ nāstīti bhavatvasāvayathārthōbhimānaḥ na punarayathārthatvaṁ cōdanāyāḥ śakyatē
vak‍tum ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b116"/>
﻿<pb n="b117"/>
<p><q>prayōgōtpattyaśāstratvāt śabdēṣu na vyavasthā syāt ।</q> kathaṁ puna-
rvyākaraṇāsmr̥tērnirmūlatvē sati <q>vēdasyāprāmāṇyamāśaṅkayatē ? yadi</q> gāvyādī-
nāmapyanādisattā syāt kiṁ jātaṁ <q>cōdanāyāḥ; ucyatē; aśvagōṇyādīnāṁ</q>
niyatārthatvaṁ smaranti vēdavidaḥ niyatārthatayā <q>ca vidavyākhyānamapi</q> kurvatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b118"/>
yadi ca vyākaraṇaṁ pramāṇaṁ tadidamupapannaṁ syāt । nirmūlatvē hi niyatārthatā
niṣpramāṇikā syāt । bhavatu kā nō bādhā । aniyatanimittakō vēdārthaḥ
prāpnōti । tataścānadhyavasāyādaprāmāṇyam । na ca śāstrasthanyāyō'tra śakyatē
﻿<pb n="b119"/>
vak‍tum । tasmādvayākaraṇanibandhana ēvātrādhyavasāya iti । atastadupapatti-
rvicāraṇīyā । tadidaṁ vicāryatē । kiṁ gaurityēvamādīnāmanāditvaṁ sās‍nādi-
mati gāvyādīnāṁ cādimattēti । kimiyaṁ smr̥tiḥ sambhavanmūlā nēti
vicāryatē । kiṁ tāvatprāptaṁ ? āstāṁ tāvanmūlacintā śabdānuśāsanaṁ
tāvadaniyatārtham ।</p>
<p>kēyamaniyatārthatā ? iyamaniyatārthatā prayōganiyamārthaṁ hīdaṁ
śāstram । na cāsau prayōgō niyantuṁ śakyatē । atha prayōgādēva niyamaḥ
siddhaṁ tarhi gāvyādīnāmapi sās‍nādimatyanāditvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b120"/>
<p>kathaṁ punaḥ prayōgō niyantuṁ na śakyatē ? itthaṁ na śakyatē
prathamaṁ tāvadidamanuśāsanaṁ, dhātōḥ parē pratyayā bhavantīti । tathā ca kēci-
tkartari, kēcitkarmaṇi, kēcit kartr̥varjitēṣu sarvakārakēṣu ; taccēdaṁ
sarvamanupapannam । kathamanupapannaṁ ? ēvamanupapannaṁ&mdash;dhātōrityucyatē; kō
nāmāyaṁ dhātuḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b121"/>
<p>nanu bhūvādayō dhātava iti kāṁścicchabdān kayā citparipāṭayā
paṭhitvā <quote>‘dhātava’</quote> iti saṁjñā kr̥tā । atastayā saṁjñayā yē saṁjñinō
lakṣyantē tēbhyaḥ parē pratyayā bhavantīti kiṁ nōpapadyatē ? gaṇḍatītyādīnāmapi
sādhutvaṁ prāpnōti; ghaṭaṁ bhūyata iti ca । sattādīnāmapi tārtīyapratyayaprasaṅgaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b122"/>
anārṣaḥ pāṭha iti cēt । bhavatvapyayaṁ parihāraḥ gaṇḍatyādīnāṁ
punaraprayōga ēva ।</p>
<p>atha kriyāvacanō dhāturityucyatē, na, bhavati tiṣṭhatītyādīnā-
maprayōgaḥ gaṇḍatēścānarthakaḥ pāṭhaḥ । akriyāpi k‍vacit pratīyata iti cēt
﻿<pb n="b123"/>
prayōgatastarhi niyamaḥ na kriyātaḥ prayōgaḥ । kriyāvagatibhātraṁ niyāmakamiti
cēt nādhyārōpānadhyārōpayōstulyatāvagatiḥ saṁbhavatītyuk‍tam । tasmādida-
mapi na niyāmakam । pāṭhakriyāvacanābhyāṁ niyama iti cēt
﻿<pb n="b124"/>
tatrāpi samuditaṁ vyastamiti vak‍tavyam । samuditapakṣē gaṇḍatibhavatyādīnāṁ
tathaiva vyudāsaḥ । pratyēkamiti cēt pacatyādīnāṁ pāṭhānarthakyam ।
āgamayatyādīnāṁ nivr̥ttyarthamiti cēt । ubhayaṁ tarhyāśritam । ēvaṁ
sati bhavatyādiṣu sa ēva dōṣaḥ । tasmāt punarapi prayōga ēva śaraṇam ।
﻿<pb n="b125"/>
tathā kārakaniyamāsiddhiḥ । dhruvamapāyē'pādānamiti dhruvatayā'pōdānamuk‍tam ।
dhruvasya kārakatvamēva nōpapadyatē, mēṣānmēṣō'pasarpati iti kārakam ।
mēṣāditi kasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ kārakamētat । yasya hi yasyāṁ kriyāyāṁ
vyāpārō vidyatē sa tasyāṁ kārakam । na ca dhruvasya vyāpāra upalabhyatē ।</p>
<p>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ sārthāddhīnaḥ rathāt patitaḥ iti sārtharathayōḥ
kriyōpalabhyata iti; nāsti kriyā sārthasya rathasya ca । api tu gamanarūpō
na ca kiyāntarē vyāpr̥taṁ kriyāntarē kārakaṁ bhavati । na ca gamēḥ
﻿<pb n="b126"/>
kartā pacatītyasyāvasīyatē । tasmānniṣkriyaṁ kārakamiti vadatō vyāpr̥tōdanyat
sarvaṁ sarvatra kārakaṁ syāt । pacatītyatra paṭhati dhāvati bhuṅkatē ityēva
mādyapādānaṁ syāt । ēvaṁ pacatyādiṣu kartā paṭhatyādyapādānaṁ syāt ।</p>
<p>ayamaparaḥ kārakaniyamaḥ । karmaṇā yamamipraiti sa saṁpradānamiti
karmaṇā cēdabhiprēyatē na kārakam । kartrā hi karmaṇā yō'bhiprēyatē
sa sampradānamityudāharaṇādvidmaḥ upādhyāyāya gāṁ dadāti iti । kartr̥vyā-
pārānunippādi vyāpāraṁ ca kārakam । yaḥ punarabhiprēyatē na tasyābhiprayaṇē
vyāpāraḥ tēna tam iti karmakaraṇanirdēśāt phalaṁ karma bhavati na kārakaṁ
yajēriva svargaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b127"/>
<p>nanu ca <quote>‘karmaṇā yamabhipraiti’</quote> iti kārakaṁ karma parigr̥hyatē;
sutarāmakārakatvam; na hi kārakasaṁbandhitayā kārakavyapadēśō bhavati,
karōtīti kārakaśabdavyutpādanāt । tasmānna śakyatē śāstrataḥ kārakaniyammē
'vagantum । kriyāsaṁbandhitayā ca [kārakatvē] viśēṣānuśāsanaṁ na siddhayati ।
ṣaṣṭhī ca sarvakārakāṇāṁ prāpnōti svargasya ca yāgakārakatvaprasaṅgaḥ prayā-
jādīnāṁ ca darśapūrṇamāsayōḥ । prayōgapratipattibhyāṁ niyama iti cēnna tarhi
śāstrataḥ । yadapi sādhakatamaṁ karaṇamityucyatē kiṁ tat sādhakatamamiti ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b128"/>
yasya vyāpārānantaraṁ kriyāniṣpattiriti, prāptaṁ tarhi taṇḍulairōdana&mdash;
miti । athānyēna hētunā sādhakatamatvaṁ; tadvak‍tavyam; prācuryāditi cēt,
yasya hi āphalaniṣpattēḥ punaḥ punaḥ vyāpāraḥ । kasya vā nāstīti । āstē
pak‍tā sthālyādisabhārasaṁbhr̥taḥ sajjaḥ । prasak‍taṁ tarhi kāṣṭhaiḥ pacatīti
sthālyāmudakēnēti । bhavatvēvamiti cēt, na tarhi kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyāmōdanaṁ
pacatīti prayōganiyamaḥ । prayōgāditi cēt namaḥ śāstrāya ।</p>
<p>ādhārō'dhikaraṇamiti cānuśāsanam । kasyādhāratvaṁ ? yatrādhīyatē
sa ādhāra iti । yadi tāvat kriyā sarvakārakāṇāmadhikaraṇatvaprasaṅgaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b129"/>
atha yatra karma tadadhikaraṇāmiti cēt, samē pacatīti na prāpnōti apsu
pacatīti prāpnōtīti । kaṭē bhuṅkatē iti cāpabhraṁśaḥ । karturhi tadadhikaraṇaṁ
na kriyāyāḥ, nāpi karmaṇaḥ । sarvakārakavyavasthānaṁ yatrēti cēt sthālyā-
mōdanaṁ pacatīti na prāpnōti । adhikaraṇasya vā kārakatvaprasaṅgaḥ । na
hyadhikaraṇaṁ adhikaraṇavyavasthitamiti śakyatē vak‍tum । saṁbandhitayā
sarvakārakādhikaraṇatā vā'dhikaraṇatvē hēturuk‍taḥ nirvyāpāratvaṁ ca kālādi-
ṣūk‍tam । yadapyucyatē karturīpsitatamaṁ karmēti, kō'yamātiśāyanikaḥ sarvaṁ
﻿<pb n="b130"/>
kriyārthamīpsitatamam । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yadarthā kriyā tat tamapā'bhi-
dhīyatē । prāptamakārakatvam । uk‍taṁ hi saṁpradānasūtrē । tathā yuk‍taṁ cānī-
psitam iti । kathaṁ yuk‍taṁ ? tamabarthēnēti cēt, na tarhyanīpsitamiti
śakyatē vak‍tuṁ anyasyātiśayinō'nupādānāt । tasmādandhapadamēvēdam ।</p>
<p>akacitaṁ ca kathitamēva । tasmāt prayōgādēva sarvamupapādanīyaṁ
na śāstrādityavagacchāmaḥ । tathā svatatraḥ kartēti kimidaṁ svātantryam ?
yadīcchātaḥ pravr̥ttiḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b131"/>
<p>jāyatē mriyatē kūlaṁ patatītyakartr̥tā prāpnōti । tataścāsādhutā-
prasaṅgaḥ śabdasya ।</p>
<p>atha tadvayāpārādhīnaṁ kārakāntaraṁ manyasē kēyaṁ tadadhīnatā yasmin
sati yō niṣpadyatē tat tadadhīnaṁ; prāptaṁ tarhi sarvakārakāṇaṁ kartr̥tvamitarēta-
rādhīnatvāt । na kēnacidvinā kasyacit niṣpattimupalabhāmahē । yasya
hi yēna vinā vyāpāraniṣpattiḥ na tēna tadapēkṣatē; parasparāpēkṣaśca kārakagrāmaḥ
tasmānna niyamaḥ ।</p>
<p>dhātūpāttavyāpāraḥ kartēti cēt । na vidmaḥ kasya dhātūpātta
iti sarvēṣāṁ saṁbandhitayā'vagamāt । tathā ca prayōgadarśanaṁ kāṣṭhāni
﻿<pb n="b132"/>
pacantīti । yasya vivakṣita iti cēta; vivakṣāyāḥ kāraṇaṁ vak‍tavyam । prayōga
iti cēt ; pramāṇaṁ tarhi śāstraṁ ; tasmānnirmūlēyaṁ śāstraniyamātkarturava-
cchittiḥ । tatprayōjakō hētuścēti prayōjyēnaiva vyākhyātam । yē cāpyarthōpapadō-
pādhayaḥ tē'pi kriyāviśēṣēṇa vā'rthaviśēṣēṇa vā niyāmakāḥ । tadyathā
rucyarthānāṁ prīyamāṇa iti saṁpradānē । bhītrārthānāṁ bhayahēturityapādānē । atrāpi
na vidmaḥ kimarthamapēkṣatē saṁpradānaniyamāya uta rucyarthōccāraṇamiti । kiñcātaḥ
﻿<pb n="b133"/>
yadi rucyarthōccāraṇaṁ dēvadattāya mōdakā dīyantāmiti na prāpnōti । kimiti
rucyarthā hi tē rucinimittatvāt । nanu ca rucyarthō dhātvarthaḥ parigr̥hyatē
kimasau nirviṣaya ēva ? na nirviṣayaḥ yadyasmai rōcatē tadviṣayō rucyarthaḥ ।
avagatastarhi, mōdakābhidhānāt dhātūccāraṇaṁ nibandhanamiti cēt dēvadattāya
mōdakāḥ kiṁ rōcanta iti praśnōttarānupapattiḥ । tadapēkṣayaiva prayuk‍tiriti cēt
na, praśnōttarānupapattēḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b134"/>
<p>praśnanirākaraṇārthamētaduccāraṇaṁ na caturthīprayōgasya sādhutvāya । tathā
apādānē'pi bhayahētutvaṁ bhītēḥ kārakamātrasyāpādānatāmāpādayati, sarvakāra-
kavyāpārādhīnatvādbhītēḥ । upapadādiṣu tu kārakataiva nāsti । anayaiva
diśā vibhak‍tividhānamapi pratyuk‍tam । viṣayanirūpaṇapūrvakatvāt vibhak‍ti-
vidhānasya । ēvaṁ vākyārthāvagamapūrvakasya niyamasya na vākyārthau-
payikatvaṁ tatsiddhēstadavagamāt । ēvaṁ kr̥tpratyayā api vyākhyā-
tāḥ । tiṅpratyayā api kālād‍yupādhayō na tadvacanāḥ ।
apratītaiśca niyamanirūpaṇamaśakyam । kēna cōk‍taṁ kālādayō
﻿<pb n="b135"/>
nōcyanta iti ? uk‍taṁ bhagavatā bhāṣyakārēṇa bhūtē dhātvartha iti ।
na ca dhātvarthēnaiva dhātvarthanirūpaṇaṁ śakyam । tathā liṅādayō'pi
vidhyādyarthānirūpaṇāt ।</p>
<p>kathaṁ punarvidhyādēranirūpaṇaṁ ? upapadārthavaśatvādbhēdasya । na
svatō bhēdaḥ śakyatē'vagantum । abhinnasvārthānāṁ ca niyamō durvacaḥ
aśvagōṇyādīnāmiva; tathā taddhitasamāsau samarthavacanā[ta] durnirūpau ।
kimidaṁ samarthavacanāditi ? samarthānāṁ prathamādvā samarthaḥ padavidhiḥ iti
cānuśāsanam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b136"/>
<p>ēkārthānvayitā ca sāmarthyam । tallakṣaṇatvārthaṁ ca
samāsaviśēṣābhidhānaṁ taddhitaviśēṣābhidhānaṁ ca । tēna ca tau lakṣyētē iti
itarētarāśrayaṁ taddhitaviśēṣavidhānam । tathā asamarthasamāsōpasaṅkhayānaṁ samarthācca
taddhitānutpattiḥ na prayōgāt r̥tē śakyatē'vagantum । tataścēt kr̥taṁ śās‍trēṇa ।
asamarthānāṁ tāvatsamāsō aśrāddhabhōjī dadhighaṭō gōratha iti । samarthāccānu-
tpattistaddhitasya aṅgulyā khanati vr̥kṣamūlādāgata iti । tasmāt prayōga-
śaraṇaṁ śīs‍traṁ na prayōganiyamāyālam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b137"/>
<p>tathā <quote>‘arthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikam’</quote> ityatrāpi kiṁ kāryamartha&mdash;
vattvaṁ utautpattikamiti vak‍tavyam । kō vā viśēṣaḥ ? yadi kāryamarthavattvaṁ
<quote>‘siddhē śabdārthasaṁbandhē’</quote> iti na ghaṭatē । athautpattikaṁ tatkathanōpāyatvācchāstrasya
na śās‍traupayikatvaṁ sētsyati । upāyatvēnēdaṁ śās‍traṁ upēyamūlaṁ cētītarēta-
rāśrayam । ēvaṁ ca tannibandhanaṁ svarakāryapratyayavidhānaṁ ca na siddhayati ।
adhāturapratyaya iti cāvayavātirēkaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b138"/>
<p>kimanēna nivartyatē ? dhātōrarthavattvēpi pratyayasya ca prātipadikasaṁjñā
mā bhūt ityēvamarthamuk‍tam । yadi prātisvikamarthavattvamāśritya
adhāturapratyaya ityuk‍tam vākyasya tarhi prātipadikasaṁjñā prāpnōti ।
samāsagrahaṇaṁ tannivr̥ttyarthamiti cēt; adhāturapratyaya ityanarthakam ।
tasyāpi samāsagrahaṇānnivr̥ttiḥ । ēkārthatvē sati nivartakaṁ nārthāntarē
﻿<pb n="b139"/>
iti cēt; tadayuk‍tam, samāsasyāpyarthāntarābhyupagamāt vāvacanānarthakyēna ।
atha arthavatsamudāyanirākaraṇatayā samāsagrahaṇam; kr̥ttaddhitagrahaṇaṁ tarhi na
kartavyam । tatrāpi kr̥dantāstaddhitāntāścēti samudāya ēvēṣyatē । tasmāt
prayōgasya tāvadabhyupāyatā durghaṭā । dughaṭēna cōpāyēna dūrāpētamupēyajñānam ।
﻿<pb n="b140"/>
uk‍tānuk‍taduruktanirūpaṇaṁ ca vyākhyātdr̥ṇāṁ lakṣaṇē prayōgata ēva
pratipattavyam । chandasi viśēṣābhidhānaṁ ca tadarthājñānānnōpapadyatē ।
tat jñānapūrvakamiti cēt, anarthakaṁ tarhi; vēdārthajñānāya hi aṅgāni
prayujyantē । nāṅgajñānāya vēdārthaḥ tasya kāryārthatvāt । ataḥ śabdasya
śāsaṁna anuśāsanamēva । tathā ca prātiśākhyādīnāṁ praṇētr̥bhiḥ paraspara-
viruddhārthapradarśanēna prakaṭīkr̥ta ēva śāstrādaniyamaḥ । yadapīdamaparaṁ
﻿<pb n="b141"/>
aprayōgānna bhavati iti vyākhyātr̥vacanaṁ, taddarśayati mūlāparijñānaṁ sūtra-
praṇētdr̥ṇām । aparijñātamūlasya tasya vacanānmūlaniyamō niyama
ēva । ākr̥tigaṇābhidhānaṁ ca śāstratō niyamasya mātr̥kā । bahulagrahaṇaṁ ca
śāstratō'niyamasya ḍiṇḍimaḥ । ēvamasyāḥ smr̥tēranāditvamabhyupagacchadbhiḥ
abhyupagatamajñatvam । tasmādanirṇītanimittādvēdārthajñānamiti vadadbhiḥ
sanmārgānusārī lōkō vyāmōhitaḥ । yadvā śraddhāvijr̥bhitamārjavāt । tadida-
muk‍taṁ <quote>‘prayōgōtpattyaśāstratvāt śabdēṣu na vyavasthā syāt’</quote> iti ।
nanu cēyamanupapattiḥ pāṇinīyasyōktā । anyasmānniyamaṁ vidmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b142"/>
na । anyasyāpyayamēvōpadēśōpāyaḥ । śabdē prayatnaniṣpattēraparādhasya bhāgitvaṁ
āstāṁ tāvadupadēśōpāyaḥ idamēva tāvadvicāryatē kimādimattayāpi śabdasya
vyavahāraḥ siddhayati nēti । kimiti na siddhayati ? ēvaṁ na siddhayati ।
vr̥ddhavyavahāraparaṁparayā śabdārthavyavahārasiddhiḥ avicchinnā ca sētyuk‍tam ।
avicchēdē ca kaḥ khalvavasarō'pabhraṁśasya । yaji paraṁ svavyavahārasiddhayarthaṁ kasya

﻿<pb n="b143"/>
cit saṁjñā paribhāṣā vā kr̥tā, tatra ca kartr̥smaraṇaṁ yathā'sminnēva
vyākaraṇē । na ca gāvyādīnāṁ ghaṭādīnāmiva saṁbandhasya kartā smaryatē ।
tasmāta ādimattāyā avasara ēva nāsti । satyaṁ yadyavasarō na;
asti tvasau, dr̥śyatē hi bālānāmanyaśabdōccāraṇēcchāyāmapi śabdāntarō-
ccāraṇam । yathā kartēcchāyāṁ kattēti viṣṇurviṇṇuriti । satyam ।
bālānāṁ anyathōccāraṇamupalabhyatē । tat‍tu tadvayavahārāvadhikamēva । yatpunaḥ
﻿<pb n="b144"/>
smaryamāṇaprabhavaṁ tadapyaśak‍tijamityaśak‍tijamēvābhidhānam । atrōcyatē
&mdash;satyaṁ yadyasak‍tijadarśanādaśak‍tijatvaṁ gāvyādērbrūmaḥ । vayaṁ tu
punaḥ smr̥tita upalabhya smr̥tērmūlōsaṁbhabamaśak‍tijadarśanēnōk‍tavantaḥ । nanu ca
tadēvēdamuk‍taṁ; na, tathōcyamānamanumānaṁ bhavati । tatra ca viruddhādēra-﻿<pb n="b145"/>
vasaraḥ । atra punaḥ smr̥tērmūlābhāvō na śakyatē vak‍tuṁ ityētāvatā aśak‍ti-
jadarśanam । saṁbhavamātranirasanaścābhāvō nāśak‍tijadarśanamapēkṣatē । atō'bhi-
yuk‍tasmaraṇamanyathēti na śakyatē vak‍tum । ēvaṁ tarhi smaraṇamēvēdaṁ na
niyamāyālaṁ bhavatītyuk‍tam; niyamāyālaṁ bhavati । kathaṁ punarna bhavatīti
jñātam ? tata ēva pūrvōk‍tavyāpakāvyāpakavyākhyānāt tadvayākhyānaṁ
kathaṁcitsamāhitaṁ vyākhyātr̥bhiḥ । yathā samāhitaṁ kathaṁcit tathaiva
parigr̥hyatām । tadapi hi smaraṇamēva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b146"/>
<p>ēvaṁ kr̥tvā sadr̥śānāṁ śabdānāmēkasminnarthē śak‍tibhēdō na
kalpitaḥ । dr̥śyatē hi adyatvēpyētacchabdasya śabdāntarasmaraṇa-
vyavahitamarthāvagamahētutvam yathā adritunna[ṅga]miti । ata ēva
vibhak‍tivyatyayaṁ śabdavidō'bhyupagacchanti । aśmakairāyāta ityuk‍tē
aśmakēbhya iti pratipadyatē । tasmādanēnāpi prakārēṇākṣēp‍tuṁ na śakyatē
prāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>prayōgacōdanābhāvādarthaikatvam ।</q> kiṁ ya ēva
﻿<pb n="b147"/>
laukikāḥ śabdāḥ ta ēva vaidikāḥ, kiṁ ta ēva caiṣāmarthāḥ ityasyāḥ
cintāyāḥ prayōjanam । nanu cākr̥tyadhikaraṇasyāyamupōd‍ghātaḥ । katha-
mupōd‍ghātaḥ ? yadi ta ēva śabdāḥ ta ēvārthāḥ tadā vyak‍tyābhidhāna-
mukhēna śakyatē prāmāṇyākṣēpaḥ kartuṁ; yadi tvanya ēva śabdā arthāścānya&mdash;
tvādēvāprāmāṇyaṁ kiṁ vyaktyabhidhānamukhēnāprāmāṇyōpanyāsēna ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b148"/>
<p>ata idamuk‍taṁ&mdash;<q>idaṁ tāvatparīkṣyamiti ।</q> kathamanyatvāśaṅkā;
vyapadēśabhēdāt ; laukikānāṁ vaidikānāṁ cētyabhiyuk‍tā vyapadiśanti ।
kr̥taṇatvamagniśabdaṁ paṭhanti । tathā dēvāsaḥ tmamētyēvamādēśca darśanāt । tathā
arthānyatvamapi vēdādēva pratibhāti । uttānā vai dēvagavā vahanti, hiraṇya-
parṇōḥ vanaspatiḥ । ghr̥taṁ madhviti ca । nanu caivaṁ vēdārthāvagamō nōpapadyatē
laukikaśabdārthapūrvakatvādvēdārthasya । sa ēva mābhūdityākṣiptam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b149"/>
<p>apratipādakastarhi vēdaḥ ? ōmityucyatē na prayōjanānuvarti
pramāṇaṁ bhavitumarhati । ēvaṁ tarhi pramāṇādēva prayōjanamavagacchāmaḥ ।
kiṁ tatpramāṇaṁ ? śabdārthayōrananyatvāvagatiḥ । bhēdō hi svarūpataḥ kāryatō
vā syāt svarūpaṁ tāvat tadēva varṇātmakaṁ gavādīnāṁ ; kāryamapi tadēva
sāsnādimatpratipattihētutvam । kēnānyatvamavagacchāmaḥ ? nanu ca ṇatvādibhiḥ,
﻿<pb n="b150"/>
varṇānyatvaṁ hi tat na padānyatvaṁ, arthapratipattihētutvaṁ, tasya
caikatvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b151"/>
<p>nanu cārthānyatvāt padānyatvaṁ; arthānyatvamēva hyasiddham ।
uttānā vahantītyasyārthasyāsiddhēḥ । na cāyamarthō'rthānyatvē
uttānaśabdāt pratipat‍tuṁ śakyatē । tasmāt dvayābhāvāt siddha-
mēkatvam । kathaṁ tarhi uttānā vai dēvagavā vahantīti ? । uk‍taṁ﻿<pb n="b152"/>
stutyarthatvēna prāmāṇyaṁ guṇavādēna vyakhyātam । kathaṁ tarhi
vyapadēśaḥ ? anuśāsanaviṣayānyatvāsiddhayarthaḥ । sāpēkṣānapēkṣatvēna
viṣayabhēdaḥ siddhayati ।</p>
<p><q>prayōgacōdanā ।</q> uktaṁ tad‍bhūtānāṁ kriyārthatvēna samāmnāya iti
tadidānīṁ vicāryatē । kimidaṁ bhūtānāmiti na vidmaḥ kimākr̥tau bhūtānāṁ
uta vyak‍tāviti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b153"/>
<p>nanu yadyasmāt pratīyatē sa tad‍bhūtaḥ । ubhayaṁ cāsmāt
pratīyatē । kathaṁ tarhi sāmānyēna pratyayāt vyak‍tau ca
kriyāsaṁbhavāditi । kiṁ cātra nōpapadyatē ? idaṁ cātra nōpapadyatē vyak‍tau
ca kriyāsaṁbhavāditi । kriyāsaṁbhavō hi vyak‍tau tad‍bhūtatvē hēturuk‍taḥ ।
vyak‍tau kimanēnāvagamō nirastaḥ ? ōmityucyatē; ākr̥tāvavagamā-
bhidhānāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b154"/>
<p>agranthajñō hi dēvānāṁ priyaḥ । kā'trāgranthajñatā ?
iyamatrāgranthajñatā । kriyārthēna samāmnāya ityuk‍tam । kiyārthatayā ca
tad‍bhūtatvaṁ nirūpitam । nāpratītaṁ kiyārthaṁ bhavatīti vyak‍tāvēva
tad‍bhūtatvam । sāmānyāvagatistarhi kathaṁ, astītyētāvacchakyatē vak‍tum ।
na punaḥ kriyārthatayā tad‍bhūtatvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b155"/>
<p>nanu ca sāmānyāvagatau satyāṁ vyaktyavagamō na prāpnōti । ahō
batānubhavēpyanavamarśaḥ ! kasya sāmānyasyāvagamaḥ ? sambandhitayā hyana-
vagamyamānaṁ sāmānyaṁ sāmānyamiti nāvagamyatē । sambandhyantarasāpēkṣā hi
sambandhini buddhirbhavati । viśēṣataścātra rūparūpitayā nāvagamyatē । na
hi rūpiśūnyā rūpabuddhirasti । yadi syāt rūpataiva na syāt । kimiti
﻿<pb n="b156"/>
tarhi bhēdēnōpanyāsaḥ ? kriyārthēna rūpasyānanvayapradarśanārtham । na
cānanvitasya śabdārthatvaṁ yuk‍tam pañjarasyēva siṁhamānayēti pañjarasthā-
vagatau । kimiti tarhyupanyāsaḥ ? amumēvārthaṁ pradarśayituma ।
kimartham ? ananvitanimittatayā aprāmāṇyābhidhānaṁ ākr̥ti-
vādinaḥ । vyak‍tēścānvayamicchanti vrīhin prōkṣatītyēvamādiṣu ।
﻿<pb n="b157"/>
vyak‍titad‍bhūtapakṣē vā kimanapēkṣatvaṁ siddhayati ? । śiddhayatu mā vā
apanyāyāśrayaṇaṁ tāvajjātivādinaḥ । vyaktipakṣē tu kāryānurūpā karaṇakalpanā
nyāyyā । nanu ca kathamayaṁ nyāyyaḥ pakṣaḥ yasmāt vr̥ddhavyavahāraparaṁparā
na vyutpattau kāraṇatāṁ pratipattuṁ śak‍nōti । kathaṁ na śak‍nōti ?
anvayavyatirēkāśrayō hi vr̥ddhavyavahāraḥ । anvayavyatirēkau ca sāmānya-
nibandhanau । na ca vr̥ddhavyavahārādanyadvayutpattau kāraṇamupalabhōmahē ।
karturasmaraṇādityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b158"/>
<p>nanu cākr̥tāvapi tad‍bhūtatvaṁ nirastam । āmnāyasya kriyārtha-
tvāditi । kiṁ punaranayōrbalīyaḥ ? kāryamiti brūmaḥ । taddhi kalpanābījaṁ
kāraṇacakrasya, vr̥ddhavyavahārādi saha tad‍bhūtatayā kāraṇaṁ kāryataścā-
sannataraṁ tadbhūtatvamavagamyatē tadanurūpā ca vyutpattiḥ kalpanīyā । sā
cēnna vr̥ddhavyavahārapūrvikā saṁbhavati kalpyatāṁ vā samayaḥ kr̥takatvaṁ vā vyā-
mōhō vā । nanu ca vr̥ddhavyavahārādēvāvagatirdr̥ṣṭā bālānāṁ; na hi dr̥ṣṭē'nupapannaṁ
nāmēti । upapannā tarhi ! satyaṁ jarśanata upapannā, nimittatastu nōpapadyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b159"/>
na ca samayaḥ kr̥takatvaṁ vōpalabhyatē । tasmānnimittakalpanā nayānnirastēva
lakṣyatē ।</p>
<p>yadi punaḥ sāmānyōpalakṣitaṁ vyaktidravyamēva nimittatāmāpadyatē vākyārtha-
pratipattau tataḥ kō dōṣaḥ ? naiva kāścit na khalu kaściddōṣaḥ, upalakṣaṇatvē
tu pramāṇaṁ vak‍tavyam । kāryapratipattiraivātra pramāṇam । na hi vyak‍tāva-
pratipannāyāṁ kāryapratipattirghaṭatē । na hi sāmānyēnānupalakṣitō vyaktiviśēṣaḥ
śakyatē pratipādayitumiti sarvamupapannam । atō vyaktyabhidhānaṁ manyatē
vyāḍiriti pradarśitam । ata ēva saṅkhayādīnāṁ viniyōjyōpādēyatvamupapannaṁ
﻿<pb n="b160"/>
bhavati । na hyanāśritō guṇānvayabhāgbhavati । anyatvavyapadēśaśca
na jātipakṣē upapadyatē । atō vyaktinimittataiva ca tad‍bhūtatēti
draṣṭavyam ।</p>
<p><q>ākr̥tistu kriyārthatvāt ।</q> atrōcyatē । siddhayatyapi
kadācidarya pakṣaḥ kāryāvagatirēva hyanaikāntikī, śyēnacitaṁ
﻿<pb n="b161"/>
cinvītēti nātra vyaktivacanatā[tad‍bhūtatā]śakyatē vak‍tum । na hyatra
vyaktigataṁ kāryaṁ pratīyatē । kimiti na pratīyatē ? nāyaṁ vākyārthaḥ
śyēnaiścitaṁ śyēnacitamiti । karmaṇyagnyākhyāyāmiti smaraṇāt ।
abhidhānasmaraṇaṁ ca yathārthamityuktam । ataḥ śyēnaśabdō'yaṁ citau vartatē ।
tasmāt dravyāntarasādhyāyāṁ citau śyēnaśabdaḥ upamārthē vr̥ttaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b162"/>
na hi vyaktisādr̥śyamupapādayituṁ śakyatē । tasmāt sāmānyānvayō
dr̥śyatē na vyak‍tēḥ । anghayinaśca padārthā ityuktam । tasmānnōpalakṣaṇa-
tayaiva sāmānyasyānvayō'vagamyatē । kintu kāryataḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b163"/>
kiñcōpamānōpasarjanārthānāmapyanvayitvamasti । bāḍhamasti pratipattau,
na kāryē । kiṁ kāryānanvayinō'pi anvayitā bhavati ? uk‍tamarthavādānāṁ
mantrapadānāṁ ca । ākr̥tēḥ tarhi kimiti nēṣyatē ? vrīhīn prōkṣatīti
kāryapratipattāvanaṅgatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b164"/>
<p>nanu cōpalakṣaṇatvē nāṅgaṁ bhavati; nōpalakṣaṇamaṅgaṁ vāsōva&mdash;
dviśēṣāvagatau । tasmātkvacidvayak‍tiranvayinī kvacitsāmānyamiti na
vidmaḥ ka tad‍bhūtatvaṁ nyāyyamiti । tasmādanavadhr̥ta[ti]nimittaṁ punara-
prāmāṇyaṁ prasaktam । atrōcyatē&mdash;na tad‍bhūtatayā vyak‍tēranvayō'vasī-
yatē । yadi hyanvayinī vyaktistadā vyaktimātrānvayaḥ ēkasyā vā vyak‍tēḥ
﻿<pb n="b165"/>
na cōbhayaṁ pratīyatē । anutsr̥ṣṭasāmānyapratyayō hi sarvatrānvaya upalabhyatē ।
nanu cōpalakṣaṇatayā sāmānyapratyayō'stītyuktam । tadēva tu nāvagamyatē ।
upalakṣaṇaṁ hi nāma nātmākāratayōpalakṣyamupalakṣayati yathā yatrāyaṁ kākaḥ
adō dēvadattasya gr̥gamiti, na kākākāraṁ gr̥hamavasīyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b166"/>
<p>yadapi cōk‍tam yēna pañjarasthaḥ siṁhō dr̥ṣṭaḥ tasya siṁhāvagamādēva
pañjarāvagamaḥ, tadbalādākr̥tēḥ vyaktyavagamādēvāvagama iti । tadapyayuktam ।
kutaḥ ? siṁhākārādākārāntaratayā pañjaramavagacchanti, naivaṁ gāmānayētyākārāntara-
mavagamyatē । tasmādapratīyamānākārāntaratayā vyaktiranvēti iti duśśakaṁ-
vak‍tum । nanu ca kāryārthatvādanvayasya ākāramātrasya ca tadanupapattēḥ
vyaktipurassaraiva sāmānyāvagatiḥ nimittānusārēṇa; satyaṁ yathāha
﻿<pb n="b167"/>
pitr̥mān । tathāpyākārāvagatiparyantaivānvayāvagatiḥ । athākāraḥ pañjarasthānīyaḥ
kalpyaḥ, tatō vyaktimātrānvayaḥ ēkavyaktyanvayō vā syāt । bhavatu kā
nō bādhā । anadhyavasāyī śabdaḥ syāt । kēna cōk‍taṁ nēti ? anadhya-
vasāyē hi kathamākr̥tērananvayaḥ śakyatē vak‍tum । yathā gāmānayētyaśvasya,
﻿<pb n="b168"/>
na punaranadhyavasitānvayē, yathā aktāḥ śarkarā iti ghr̥tasya ।
tasmādupalakṣaṇapakṣastāvadasambaddhaḥ । athēdamucyēta svābhāvikī śabdaśaktiḥ ।
kāryataścānvayaḥ । vyaktisthaṁ ca kāryam । na ca vyaktimātraṁ viśēṣō
vā'vasīyatē । gōtvasambaddha mēva dravyaṁ pratīyatē । pratipannaṁ tarhi gōtva-
sambaddhā vyaktayaḥ pratīyanta iti । maivaṁ vōcaḥ । kāryāvasāyī hyanvayaḥ na
punaḥ pratipattimātraparyavasāyī । yathā daṇḍinamānayēti na daṇḍasyānayanama-
﻿<pb n="b169"/>
vasīyatē vidyatē ca pratītiḥ ēvaṁ gavādērapi । avivēkajñō bhavān uk‍taṁ
vivēkaṁ na gr̥hītavānasi । kimuk‍tam ? idamuk‍tam । yatrākārāntara-
vivēkaḥ tatrākārāntaramupalakṣaṇam । yathā daṇḍītyēva daṇḍiviśēṣāvagatau
nānayanē daṇḍasyānvayaḥ । yatra punaḥ daṇḍitayaivāvagagyatē na viśēṣataḥ
﻿<pb n="b170"/>
tatra tathābhūtasyaivānvayaḥ śakyatē vak‍tum । viśēṣāvagatau tu daṇḍiśabdō
na daṇḍē vartatē । aviśēṣāvagatau vā kiṁ daṇḍiśabdō daṇḍē
vartatē ? satyam । na nimittatō vartatē । arthāntarasahitasyaiva
nimittatvasiddhērvyavahārāt । na punaḥ kāryatō vivēkāvagatiḥ । gavādīnāṁ
punaḥ nimittabhēdānavagamāt sambandhiṣu nimittatayā bhēdō na ghaṭatē kiṁ
punaḥ kāryataḥ । kathaṁ tarhi vrīhīn prōkṣatīti viśēṣāvagatiḥ
na cēnnimittatō bhēdaḥ ? kāryatō viśēṣāvagatiḥ kāryaṁ hi
﻿<pb n="b171"/>
prayōjanē paryavasyati tadvati vā tadvatsu vrīhiṣu । kathaṁ punaḥ tadvantō
vrīhayaḥ pratīyantē ? prakaraṇāt । tasmānna samō'yamupanyāsō daṇḍivaditi ।
atō'nanvitē sāmānyē kāryasyaivāparyavasānaṁ; na ca sambhavati paryavasānē'-
paryavasānaṁ śakyatē vak‍tum । nanu ca kāryaviṣayatvādaparyavasānamuktam ।
satyamuk‍tam yadyasambhavaḥ kāryasya । yathāsambhavaṁ hi kāryaviṣayatvaṁ na vikāra-
vattayaiva karaṇādīnāmiva । nanu ca tēṣāmapi svavyāpārē vikārō vidyata
﻿<pb n="b172"/>
ēva । gōtvādērapi tulyam । tadapi hi vyāpārasiddhau vyāpr̥tamēva ।
nanu ca na kiñcit prāgvyāpāraṁ nirvr̥ttyuttarakālaṁ ca karaṇādīnāmiva
vikāramupalabhāmahē sāmānyē । na vikāritā vyāpārasiddhau hētuḥ । kintu
sati tasmin bhāvaḥ । na ca sāmānyāvagamaśūnyā niyōgārthanirvr̥ttiri-
tyuk‍tam । yathāpratīyamānasyaivārthasya nirvr̥ttiḥ pratīyamānajñānā&mdash;
dupapadyatē । tasmādupapannaḥ sāmānyasya kāryānvayaḥ । anyatvābhidhēyatvaṁ tu
﻿<pb n="b173"/>
upādānataḥ siddhayati । tasmāṁt sāmānyapurassaraivānvayāvagatiḥ । uddēśyē tu
kāryata upalakṣaṇatvaṁ nātad‍bhūtatayā । ataḥ siddhaṁ yathāvagamyamānārthabhūtaiḥ
tad‍bhūtairiti । ētaccōk‍tamēva sāmānyākārēṇa śabdāt pratītiriti ।
atrākr̥tigrahaṇamupalakṣaṇatayōpanyastam । anākr̥tāvapi nāgr̥hītaviśēṣaṇā
viśiṣṭē buddhiriti । <quote>“atha vyaktyantarēpi prayujyatē na tarhi vyaktiḥ padārtha”</quote><note n="(1)"> p. 162.</note>
﻿<pb n="b174"/>
iti kō'bhiprāyaḥ । ayamabhiprāyaḥ । na hyēkaṁ dharmamanāśritya vastvantarē
jñātasambandhasya vastvantarasaṁbandhitā śakyatē'vagantum । na cāsaṁbandhinaḥ
prayōgaḥ । prayujyatē cēdāśritaṁ tarhi vyatiriktaṁ kiñcit । vyak‍tērasā-
dhāraṇataiva rūpaṁ sarvasāmānyaviśēṣaviyuktā hi vyaktiriti darśitam ।
﻿<pb n="b175"/>
<note n="(1)"> p. 162.</note><quote>“naiṣa dōṣaḥ”</quote> iti sarvasāmānyā tviyaṁ viyuktiriti । ēvaṁ tarhi
viyuktirvācyatayōk‍tā na vyak‍tiḥ tadidaṁ sāmānyamēvāpatitam । <quote>“nētyu-
cyatē yō'rthaḥ sāmānyaviśēṣāṇāṁ cāśrayaḥ sā vyaktiriti”</quote>। kasyēdamuttaraṁ
dīyatē ? । viyuktimātraṁ sāmānyamāpādayataḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ tasyēdamuttaraṁ ? na
kiñcidupalakṣaṇatvēna sāmānyaṁviśēṣaṁ vā gr̥hṇāti āśrayamātrābhidhānaṁ śabdasya ।
﻿<pb n="b176"/>
nanu cāśrayamātratāpi sāmānyaṁ; nētyucyatē; sāmānyaṁ hi ākā&mdash;
rāntaravatāmēkarūpatā । āśrayō nāma na cāśrayibhyaḥ ākārāntaram ।
tasmādananyatvāvagatēḥ prayōgaḥ siddhayatītyabhiprāyaḥ । yadyēvaṁ prayōgē
tarhi virōdhaḥ । nahyaśvavyak‍tau gōśabdaprayōgō dr̥śyatē, prāpnōti ca
yuṣmatkalpanāyām । nanu cādarśanaṁ bhavataivōktam । ēvaṁ tarhi prayōgadarśanaṁ
﻿<pb n="b177"/>
māśritam । ōmityucyatē । kathaṁ tarhyadyajātāyāṁ gavi prathama&mdash;
prayōgaḥ sidhyati ? dr̥śyatē ca । kiñca vyak‍tāvēva prayōgaḥ iti pratijñāna-
mātrāmidaṁ, yadi vyaktāvēva prayōgaḥ syāt vyaktyantaranirapēkṣādvayavahārā-
d‏vyutpattiḥ syāt tatō vyaktyantarē vyutpattyantaraṁ prāpnōti । tadbhēdē ca iyaṁ
vā gauḥ iyaṁ vā gauḥityuk‍taṁ syāt । yathā ayaṁ vā akṣō' iti ।
na punaḥ ēkavyutpattinibandhanaṁ <quote>‘iyaṁ gauḥ iyamapi gauḥ iyamapi’</quote> iti syāt ।
tasmānna vyaktyabhidhānapakṣaḥ sambhavati vyutpattyantarānavagamāt ।
﻿<pb n="b178"/>
ubhayaṁ tarhi bhavatu guṇapradhānabhāvastu kāryatō nirṇēyaḥ । tathā ca pradhānapakṣē
laukikaṁ vaidikaṁ vēti sandihyatē । upādānapakṣē punaḥ sāmānyamēva ।
tadidamuktaṁ ubhayaṁ bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ iti । nāyamapi pakṣaḥ saṁbhavati ।
kāryatō hyupādānalakṣaṇatvaṁ na punaḥ pratipattitaḥ । pratipattiśca sāmānya-
nibandhanā । kutaḥ ? anvayavyātirēkābhyāṁ, vrīhīn prōkṣati
iti vyak‍tiniṣṭhē'pi prayōgē sāmānyākāratayaiva hyabhidhānamabhidhattē ।
﻿<pb n="b179"/>
vyak‍titō'vasīyata iti cēnna । vyaktyantaragatatvēnānavagatēḥ । sāmānya-
niṣṭhē punaḥ prayōgē ēkākāratayaiva dravyamavasīyata ityuk‍tam । tadi-
damāha&mdash;<q>mānasādapacārāditi ।</q> tasmānnānadhyavasāyaḥ sāmānyapratyayā-
dadhyavasāyyēva śābdam ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ prathamādhyāyasya
tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b180"/>
<head>br̥hatī</head>
<head>prathamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>uktaṁ samāmnāyaidamarthya tasmātyarvaṁ tadarthaṁ syāt ।</q> nanu cēdaṁ
pramāṇalakṣaṇaṁ; vakṣyati ca dvitīyādau&mdash;uk‍taṁ pramāṇalakṣaṇamiti;
kimidamupanyastaṁ kimudbhidādayō guṇavidhayaḥ āhōsvit karmanāma-
dhēyānīti । kiṁ vā pramāṇalakṣaṇē'yamupanyāsō na ghaṭatē ? bāḍham, sthitē
prāmāṇyē'rthaviśēṣāvadhāraṇacintōpapadyatē । aprāmāṇyē panaḥ arthābhāvāt
﻿<pb n="b181"/> 
kēyaṁ viśēṣacintā । uk‍taṁ samāmnāyaidamarthyamiti ca yat
guṇavidhānōpapattitayā vyākhyātaṁ tadapi nōpapadyatē । na hi mantrārtha&mdash;
vādatvāsaṁbhavō guṇavidhitvē hētuḥ । kiṁ tarhi ? kriyāprāptirguṇa-
vidhānatvē hētuḥ । tathā ca svayamuditam&mdash;avihitē karmaṇi guṇa-
vidhānamanarthakamiti । yadi ca mantrārthavādatvāsambhavō guṇavidhitvē hētuḥ
svargakāmō yajētētyapi guṇavidhiḥ syāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b182"/> 
<p>yadap‍yuktam&mdash;prakr̥tau jyōtiṣṭōmē guṇavidhānamarthavadbhavip‍yati
iti । tadap‍yayuk‍taṁ, tatrāpi guṇapadaṁ śrūyata ēva jyōtiṣṭōmēnēti । atha
tatra viśiṣṭavidhānaṁ bhaviṣ‍yatītyabhiprāyaḥ iha kasmānna bhavatīti । athai-
kasmin siddhē karmaṇi itarattatraiva guṇavidhānamiti, iha siddhē tada‍guṇavidhānaṁ﻿<pb n="b183"/> 
kimiti na bhavati । na ca niyamē hētuṁ paś‍yāmaḥ । viśiṣṭavidhānaṁ ca
viśiṣṭakarmōtpattau pratīyatē । na hi viśiṣṭa utpannē karmaṇi guṇāntara&mdash;
vidhānaṁ yuktam; <quote>“guṇaścāpūrvasaṁyōgē vāk‍yayōḥ samatvāt”</quote> iti nyāyā-
bhidhānāt । tasmānna lakṣaṇāntargatatvaṁ nāpi nyāyābhidhānam । atrōcyatē
&mdash;pramāṇalakṣaṇamēvēdam । nanu pramāṇalakṣaṇē'rthaviśēṣāvadhāraṇacintā
nōpapadyata ityuktam । naivēdamarthaviśēṣāvadhāraṇamupanyastam । kiṁ tarhi,
karmavidhānamatra sambhavati uta guṇavidhānamātramēvēti । guṇavidhai ca
saṁbhavati na karmavidhānaṁ nyāy‍yam guṇaparatvādvāk‍yasya rak‍tapaṭavat ।﻿<pb n="b184"/> 
tasmāt karmavidhānāsambhavāt aprāmāṇ‍yam । guṇavidhipakṣē kathaṁ ? laukika-
karmāśrayaṇāt । avaś‍yaṁ hi guṇavidhiparē vāk‍yē laukikaṁ karmāśrayaṇīyam ।
vaidikē vā kō dōṣaḥ ? na khalu kaścit । kintu asambhavaḥ vaidikasya ।
kathamasambhavaḥ ? sarvatrōpapadaśrutēḥ । ēvamapi kimityaprāmāṇyaṁ, dhātvarthē'nyataḥ
pravr̥ttirmr̥g‍yā । anyataścēt sāpēkṣatvaprasaṅgaḥ sāpēkṣatvāccāprāmāṇ‍yaṁ prasak‍tam ।
yadi punaḥ stryupagamādiṣ‍viva niyamavidhānānnirapēkṣatvaṁ tadā kathamaprāmāṇyaṁ
syāt ? syādētadēvaṁ yadi sarvatra puruṣārthā ēva vidhayaḥ syuḥ । karmārthā api﻿<pb n="b185"/>
vaidikē vā[kō] dōṣaḥ ? na khalu kaścit । kintu asaṁbhavaḥ vaidikasya ।
kathamasambhavaḥ ? sarvatrōpapadaśrutēḥ । ēvamapi kimityaprāmāṇ‍yaṁ ? dhātvarthā-
nyataḥ pravr̥ttirmr̥g‍yā, anyataścēt sāpēkṣatvaprasaṅgaḥ । sāpēkṣatvāccāprāmāṇ‍yaṁ
prasaktam । yadi punarabhyupagamādiṣviva niyamavidhānānnirapēkṣatvaṁ kathama&mdash;
prāmāṇ‍yaṁ syāt । syādētadēvaṁ yadi sarvatra puruṣārthā ēva vidhayaḥ syuḥ
karmārthā api tu kēcit vidhayaḥ pratīyantē । na tatra niyamaḥ sambhavati ।
kiṁ ca svargakāmō yajēta iti kiṁ niyamyatē ? nanu ca kartā, yathaitatkartr̥-
viśēṣaṇaṁ na ghaṭatē tathā pradarśitamēkādaśē । phalasya tvavidhēyatvādēva
niyamāsambhavaḥ । phalē karma niyamyata iti cēt; uk‍tama-
vidhēyatvaṁ karmaṇāṁ padārthāntaraparatvādvāk‍yānā, tasmātpramāṇāntaraṁ mr̥g‍yaṁ
andhapratibhā vēti pratipattavyam । guṇavat‍karmavidhānaṁ kimiti
na daṇ‍ḍinamānayēti । anavagamāt । na hyatra tr̥tīyādi-
bhirmat‍varthaḥ bhavati yathā pratipādyatē । mat‍vantānāmēva hi sō'rthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b186"/>
 lakṣaṇayā parigr̥hyata iti cēt । prāptaṁ tarhi sāpēkṣatvan । na śrutitō hi
lakṣaṇā śak‍yā'vagantum । tasmāt pramāṇāntaramēyatā ।</p>
<p>yaduk‍taṁ&mdash;uk‍taṁ samāmnāyaidamarthyaṁ tasmāt sarvaṁ tadarthaṁ syāt
iti na guṇavidhau hēturiti । bhavati hi nāmanirākaraṇatayā hētuḥ । kathaṁ
punaranēna nāma nirākiyatē । aidamarthyāsambhavāta । kathamaidamarthyaṁ
na saṁbhavati ? niyōgārthatayā vidh‍yuddēśamantrārthavādānāmarthattōktā ।
taccaitat avidhēyatvānnāmnō na saṁbhavatīti । nanu avidhēyānāṁ
hi śrut‍yā vā'rthavattōktā । tacca dvayamasya na saṁbhavati । tasmāt﻿<pb n="b187"/> 
vidhēyat‍vam । vidhēyaścēd‍guṇaḥ । tasmād‍guṇavidhiḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ <quote>‘sōmēna
yajēta’</quote> iti vidh‍yuddēśa udāharaṇaṁ ?। kathaṁ vā na saṁbhavati ? tatrāpi 
yāgasyāvidhānāt । mābhūdyāgasya vidhānaṁ guṇastāvadvidhīyatē ।</p>
<p>nanu ca guvidhirapi naiva saṁbhavati nāmatayā prasiddhēḥ । vr̥ddhavyavahārē
hi prasiddhiḥ prasiddhirit‍yucyatē । nanu yājñikavyavahārō'pi vr̥ddhavyavahāra ēva ।
na, laukikavyavahārapūrvakatvāt yājñikavyavahārasya na ca lōkē nāmatayā
prasiddhirudbhidaḥ arthāntarābhidhānatayā prasiddhēḥ । tasmād‍guṇavidhiḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b188"/> 
<p><q>ēvamapi prakr̥tau j‍yōtiṣṭōmē guṇavidhānamarthavadbhaviṣ‍yatīti ।</q>
ayuk‍tamēvēdaṁ bhāṣ‍yaṁ pratibhāti । kimiti ? j‍yōtiṣṭōmēpi j‍yōtiṣṭōmapadaṁ
vidhāyakamēva । tatrāpi yaj‍yarthō mr̥g‍yaḥ । kēna vōk‍taṁ nēti ?
yadyēvaṁ tatra vidhānaṁ nōpapadyatē guṇavidhiprakr̥titā tatra lakṣitā ।
ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati&mdash;sōmēna yajētēti guṇaṁ vidadhatā pratipannā'&mdash;
nyatō yāgasiddhiḥ । pratipannā cēt tatraivēdamap‍yupapannaṁ bhaviṣyati ।﻿<pb n="b189"/>
tasmājjyōtiṣṭōmaśabdō'bhyupagataprakr̥t‍yupalakṣaṇārthaḥ viśiṣṭavidhānāsaṁbhava-
ścōktaḥ । nāmadhēyapakṣē punaḥ niyōgārthatā na saṁbhavati yajinōpāttatvādvidhēyasya
samarpitavidhēyā nāmatā ca na vidhērupakarōti vidh‍yarthaupayikatayā ca
prāmāṇ‍yam । atastvadīyēpi pakṣē prāmāṇ‍yaṁ pramāṇāntaramr̥g‍yamēva ।
as‍madīyē punaḥ pakṣē padārthō'pi tāvad‍vr̥ddhavyavahāraprasiddhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>api vā nāmadhēyam ।</q> atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;guṇaparamētadvāk‍yamiti
yaduk‍taṁ sat‍yamētat viniyōgē tu tat । na ca viniyōgāpēkṣā kartavyā ।﻿<pb n="b190"/>
kiṁ tarhi ? bhāvāpēkṣā bhāvaścāyaṁ yajētēti । tasmāttadviṣayō niyōgaḥ । na caivaṁ
viśēṣaviṣayō niyōgaḥ pramāṇāntarasiddhō'sti । <quote>“j‍yōtiṣṭōmāt‍karmāntaraṁ”</quote>
iti । ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati&mdash;siddhaṁ laukikādvaudikaṁ karmāntaramiti । darśayiṣyati
ca <quote>‘tēbhyaḥ kriyā pratīyēta’</quote> iti । kathaṁ tarhi guṇārthēna punaḥ śrutiriti ?
kartavyatāprāp‍tyabhiprāyaṁ ca tat na viniyōgābhiprāyam । kiṁ vā na
yathāviniyōgaṁ niyōgaḥ । ēṣā tāvatprakriyā sūtrakārasya bhāvārthāḥ karma-﻿<pb n="b191"/>
śabdāḥ tēbh‍yaḥ kriyā pratīyētēti paṭhataḥ । kimidaṁ yathā
viniyōgaṁ niyōgapratyarthībhūtaṁ sūtraṁ, ? bāḍham । anyathā hi rak‍paṭanyāyēna
ś‍yēnādividhānaṁ prāpnōti । nirākr̥taṁ caitat abhāvārthatayā । kiṁ punarasyāḥ
prakriyāyā mūlam ? avagatiriti brūmaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu viniyōgē'p‍yavagatirēva। kēna cōk‍taṁ nēti ? kin‍tu kartav‍yatā
bhāvaviṣayā avagamyata ityuk‍tamasmābhiḥ kāryasvabhāvatvādbhāvasya । viniyō-
gāvagamaḥ idānīṁ kimarthaḥ ? bhāvārtha iti brūmaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi guṇaparatōcyatē ?﻿<pb n="b192"/>
prāptau sat‍yāṁ bhāvasya । nanu cōpapadaśravaṇē sati kēvalasya bhāvasya
viṣayataiva nāvagamyatē yathā raktaḥ paṭō bhavatīti । na kēvalaṁ
paṭabhavanamēvāvasīyata iti pradarśitam । kēna cōk‍taṁ kēvalō bhāvō
viṣayatāmāpadyata iti । sa tu viṣayōniyōgasyētyuktam । na cāsau
padāntarasaṁbandhaṁ niruṇaddhi rak‍tapaṭavadviśiṣṭa ēvāvasīyatē । kathaṁ puna-﻿<pb n="b193"/>
rudbhidādayō guṇāḥ santō viśēṣaṇatāṁ pratipadyantē । kiṁ guṇatayaiva viśēṣaṇa-
viśēṣ‍yabhāvaḥ ? nāmnōpi hi dr̥śyatē ḍit‍thō'yaṁ brāhmaṇaḥ ḍabit‍thō'yaṁ kṣatriya
iti । kathaṁ punaratra nāmatvam ? sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yāvagatēḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ
sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yamavasīyatē ? tr̥tīyānirdēśāt । asti hi yāgē
tr̥tīyārthaḥ sa tasyānēna siddhayatīti kathitaḥ । tr̥tīyā cōdbhidādiṣu
śrūyatē । tasmādudbhidā yāgēnēt‍yavagamyatē ।</p>
<p>tadidamayuktam&mdash;na hyēkavibhak‍tinibandhanaṁ sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yaṁ;
kiṁ tarhi ? ēkārthāvagatinibandhanam yadyēkavibhak‍tinibandhanaṁ
﻿<pb n="b194"/>
syāt aruṇayaikahāyanyēti dravyaguṇayōḥ kriyāsaṁbandhō na syāt parasparasaṁba-
ndhaniṣṭhataiva syāt nīlōtpalavat । ata ēva gauraśvaḥ puruṣō hastīti
na sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yamēkavibhaktitvēpi pratīyatē । ēkārthatayā cāyaṁ dēvadatta
iti pratīyatē । tasmānna vibhak‍tiḥ kāraṇaṁ sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yasya ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē&mdash;uktaṁ bhāvārthatvāt yajyarthē kartavyatā na punarnāmārthē ।
avagamyatē ca saṁbandhaḥ । yadi guṇanimittakaḥ parigr̥hyatē tadā
luptamatup‏pratyayanirdēśaḥ kal‍panīyaḥ । atha tu nāmadhēyaṁ tadā﻿<pb n="b195"/>
akal‍pitaśabdāntaranimittakaḥ saṁbandhō bhavati । upapadyatē cāsau samāna-
vibhaktiyōgāt । yattvaruṇayēti pradarśitaṁ tatra bhāvasaṁbandhitā dvayōḥ ।
iha tvarthāntarāśravaṇāt kasya sambandhināṁ tr̥tīyā kathayati anyadatō bhāvava-
canāt । tasmānnirdēśamātraphalaivēyaṁ tr̥tīyā । nanu ca nirdēśamātrē
prathamayā bhavitavyam । prātipadikārthāvyatirēkānuśāsanaṁ tat; na
padārthāvyatirēkasya । tathā ca ḍit‍thēna brāhmaṇēna bhuk‍tamiti nidarśitam ।</p>
<p>nanu caikārthāvagatērabhāvāt kiṁ vibhaktiḥ kariṣyati ।﻿<pb n="b196"/>
matub‍lōpa ēvātra varam । dvayōrvā niyōgārthatā । dvayōstāvat niyōgārthatvaṁ
nāsti kāryaviṣayatvānniyōgasyētyuktam । na ca kāryābhidhāyi nāmētyuktam ।
bhavatvavayavayōgāt kāryābhidhāyitā nāmnaḥ, satyaṁ, bhavatyarvyatirik‍tapakṣē ।
padārthāntaratayā tu saṁbandhāt kaḥ siddhārthatāmapaharati । siddhārthaścāniyōga-
viṣaya ityuk‍tam । tasmādavayavayōgānugatēḥ siddhamavyatiriktārthatvaṁ
nāmnaḥ । avyatiriktatvācca parihr̥tō vidhyasaṁsparśaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b197"/>
<p>nanu ca yāvadēvōk‍taṁ yajētēti tāvadudbhidā yajētēti syāt ।
syādayaṁ dōṣaḥ yadi prayōjanānuvarti pramāṇaṁ; pramāṇānuvarti tu
prayōjanam । dr̥śyatē ca vāk‍yāntarārthōpayikatvaṁ nāmnām । tasmā&mdash;
tsiddhamanapēkṣatvaṁ cōdanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>yasmin guṇōpadēśaḥ pradhānatō'bhisaṁbandhaḥ ।</q> uk‍taṁ nāmadhēya-
mapi guṇaphalasaṁbandhēnārthavadbhaviṣ‍yatīti । tadayuk‍taṁ manvānasya viṣaya&mdash;
viśēṣē kvacida‍‏yuk‍tatā pratipādyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="b198"/>
<p>yathā tāvadayuk‍taṁ tathōcyatē&mdash;guṇōpabandhārthaṁ tāvat pañca-
daśānyājyānīti । phalōpabandhārthaṁ citrayā yajēta paśukāma iti ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yuk‍taṁ tāvat udbhidā yējētētyēva&mdash;
mādīnāṁ nāmadhēyatvaṁ yajyarthasāmānādhikaraṇyāt । tathā āj‍yādīnāma-
pyājyaiḥ stuvata iti stutyarthasāmānādhikaraṇyāt । yatra punaḥ bhāvārtha-
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṁ na pratīyatē pañcadaśānyājyānīti tatra nāmāvagatirnāsti﻿<pb n="b199"/>
anugatārthatvēpi sāmānādhikaraṇyaṁ na pratīyatē pañcadaśānyājyānīti tatra
nāmāvagatirnāsti । anugatārthatvēpi sāmānādhikaraṇyānnāmatā uk‍tā । na
tadihāsti । tasmānna guṇōpabandhēna nāmnaḥ śak‍yatē'rthavattā vak‍tum ।
yuk‍taṁ tāvat guṇōpabandhē । phalōpabandhē punaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasaṁbhavāt
kimiti nārthavattā citrayā yajēta paśukāma iti ।</p>
<p>ucyatē&mdash;nārthavattā yajēta paśukāma ityēva siddhēḥ । tatra hi
sannidhānādēva yāgaviśēṣō labhyatē na nāmataḥ । mā bhūdviśēṣaḥ nāmatā tāvannā﻿<pb n="b200"/>
nirākartaṁ śak‍yatē । kēna cōk‍taṁ nāmatvaṁ nirākriyata iti । prayōjanaṁ nāstī-
tyētāvatā''kṣēpaḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ guṇavidhānaṁ citrayā yajēta paśukāma iti ।
ēvaṁ guṇavidhānaṁ-atra nirjñātō yāgaviśēṣaḥ phalāya cōdyatē nirjñātē hi
viśēṣē padāntarāvagatiḥ na viśēṣāyōpapadyatē । kutaḥ । nirjñātatvādēva । yatra
hi vidhēyō'rthaḥ svavāk‍yānvitapadāvagamya ēva bhavati tatra tata ēva viśēṣā-﻿<pb n="201"/>
vagamaḥ vākyāntaranirjñātastu nātmaparijñānāya svavākyē padānvayamapēkṣatē ।
anapēkṣitasya sāmānādhikaraṇyamaśābdam । tasmāccitrāpadaṁ vidhēyatayā'va-
gantavyam । yatra tarhi upapadādēva viśēṣāvagatiḥ vihitasyāprakr̥tatvāt
bhavatu tatra prayōjanam । iha tāvadēkāntatō nāstītyudāhr̥tam । aprakr̥tēpi
ca naiva nāmadhēyatayōpakarōti । aprakr̥tē hi karmāntara(mēva ।)taiva ।
tatra ca padadvayārthavidhānaṁ pradarśitam । agnihōtraṁ juhōti iti
kuṇḍapāyināmayanē । tasmānnōtpannasyōtpadyamānasya vā phalōpabandhē-
nā'rthavattā । tasmāccitrayēti yatrōpapadyatē tatra vidhiḥ kalpanīyaḥ﻿<pb n="202"/>
yajēta paśukāma ityēnānākāṅkitatvāt । tasmāt guṇaphalōpabandhēnārtha-
vadityayuktam ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē । naitadayuktam—yatrāparō guṇaścōdyatē tatra pūrvaprati-
pannakarmanāmadhēyataiva pratīyatē । na hyakarmaṇi guṇō vidhātuṁ śakyatē āśri-
tatvātprayōgasyēti nyāyābhidhānāt । sāmānādhikaraṇyācca sthitē nāmadhēyatvē
śaknōtyēva nāminaṁ pratipādayitum । tasmādupapannaṁ guṇōpabandhēnārthavāditi ।
yuktamājyādiṣu; citrayēti tu kathaṁ ? tatra hi prakr̥tatvādēva viśēṣāvaga-﻿<pb n="203"/>
mānnārthavattā śakyatē vaktum । bāḍhaṁ, śakyatē tatrāpi yadi na nāma
syāt nōtpannasya phalē vidhānamupapadyatē guṇaśrutēḥ vyāghātāt; phalārthamidaṁ
na guṇārthamiti viśēṣānavagamāt । anavagamē cānadhyavasāyaḥ । anadhya-
vasāyāccāprāmāṇyam । tannāmatayā parihr̥tamiti phalōpabandhēnārthavaditi
yuktam । <quote>na cāmī yaugikā</quote> iti yaugikatvanirākaraṇaṁ kvōpa—
yujyatē ? । ayamabhiprāyaḥ—yaugikatvē hi prakr̥tayāgābhidhānasiddhiḥ
syāt; yathā pācakāya vētanaṁ dēhīti sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvēpi
prakr̥tapācakābhidhānasiddhiḥ । tasmānna cāmī yaugikā ityuktam ।
jātyabhidhānē tvatra vidhēyataiva । vyaktyābhidhānaṁ hi viśēṣā﻿<pb n="204"/>
pēkṣaṁ bhavati । na cāyaugikō vyaktyabhidhāyī bhavati । ēvaṁ citrayēti guṇa-
mātrābhidhānāt jātyabhidhāyibhistulyatā । <quote>citrayā yajētēti ca yāgānuvādō
nirjñātatvānna yāgavidhiḥ</quote> ityanēna kiṁ pradarśitam ? anākāṅkṣitatvaṁ citrā-
padasya anākāṅkṣitatvē ca sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvaḥ, tadabhāvānna nāmatēti ।
tasmāt phalavidhau na nāmatayōpakāritā'vagamyata iti । <quote>guṇaphalakalpanāyāṁ
yajatēravivakṣā</quote> iti kimanēnāśaṅkitam ? yatō guṇaphalasambandhēpi naiva
