nāmnō'rthavattāsti । pratyuta rāddhāntinaitannirākaraṇīyaṁ nāmnō'rthavattāṁ vadatā ।
tasmādasambaddhamēvēdaṁ bhāṣyakhaṇḍalakaṁ manasi viparivartatē । atrōcyatē ।﻿<pb n="205"/>
<p>guṇaphalakalpanāyāṁ na nāma śakyatē nivartayitum । kutaḥ ?
yasmādyajatēravivakṣā । avivakṣāyāṁ cānāśritō guṇō na śakyatē phalāya
vidhātuṁ ca । anyataḥ pravr̥ttirhi karmaṇō guṇaphalasambandhasya nimittam ।
na ca ṣaśukāmavidhānādr̥tē yajyarthasya pravartakamasti । tasmāt
paśukāmasambandhāparityāgē citrāpadasya nāmataivāvaśiṣyatē । tasmā-
dubhayēnānākāṅkṣitatvāt kvacidguṇānurūpō guṇavidhiḥ pratipattavyaḥ ।﻿<pb n="206"/>
guṇavidhikalpanāyapi na lakṣaṇēti<note n="(1)">P. <dn>199</dn></note> ।</q> lakṣaṇāśrayaṇē hi pramā-
ṇāntarapramēyā dōṣa uktaḥ । asāvapyatra samānādhikaraṇasambandhā-
bhāvānnāstīti siddhō guṇavidhiḥ । ataḥ siddhaṁ guṇaphalōpabandhē-
nārthavannāmēti । ucyatē । nātra guṇavidhiḥ sambhavati, nāmārthavidhānē
hi siddhasyārthasya kriyānupravēśitayā vidhānaṁ na punaḥ svārthasya kāryatayā
tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tatō bhavati । yatrāyaṁ guṇaḥ siddhaḥ san 
karmaupayikatāṁ pratipadyatē tatra vidhātavyam । ataḥ paśāvasya vidhānaṁ
tatra ca vidhīyamānē asyāparō guṇō vidhātavyaḥ strītvaṁ; yadi punaḥ﻿<pb n="207"/>
sārasvatyāṁ vidhānaṁ tatrāpi paśukāmasambandhō'vagamyamānaḥ tyaktavyō
bhaviṣyati । agnīṣōmīyaguṇaprāptiśca sārasvatyāṁ bādhanīyā bhavati ।
ataḥ sarvaprāṇidravyakāṇāṁ yāgānāṁ prakr̥tibhūtē'gnīṣōmīyē vidhānamasya
svavākyānvayanirastasya । tatra ca dvayamidamaprāptaṁ punarvidhātavyaṁ bhavati ।
tasmānna guṇavidhiḥ saṁbhavati । ataḥ pratīyamānānvayanimittatā'sya
kalpayituṁ nyāyyā । sā cātra nāmnō na saṁbhavatītyuktam । tasmāt
siddhaṁ nāmadhēyatvam । phalōpabandhēnārthavadityētadapi pradarśitam । tathā
pañcadaśānyājyānīti guṇavidhipakṣē guṇadvayavidhānaṁ; tacca na saṁbhavati ।
ata ēkamatra lakṣaṇatayā grahītavyam । tacca karmaṇaḥ tasmādvākyāntarē﻿<pb n="208"/>
nirjñātasya karmaṇō vācakasyājyaśabdasyaiva lakṣaṇatvamupapadyatē । ēvaṁ paraṁparā-
saṁbandhāvagatirna parityaktā bhavati । pañcadaśānyājyānīti । yadapyuktaṁ
guṇavidhipakṣē nātra lakṣaṇēti । tadapyayuktam । kasmāt ? ājyāni
bhavanti iti yatra ājyāni vidhīyantē sa bhavatinā vaktavyaḥ । atō'trā
pyājyavanti bhavantīti saiva lakṣaṇā ।</p>
<p>yattvaprasiddhaṁ karmaṇō nāmadhēyatvamukta tata karmaṇō lakṣaṇatvāt siddha-
miti, pravr̥ttinimittasya ca sarvatra vidyamānatvāt <quote>yadājimīyu</quote> ityēva—
mādēḥ । atha kasmāt na pañcadaśasaṅkhyāviśiṣṭānyājyāni stōtrēṣu vidhīyanta﻿<pb n="209"/>
iti kimanēnānirākr̥tamupanyastam ? padadvayārthō'nyatra vidhīyatē । kimēvaṁ
bhaviṣyati ? anāvr̥ttirvākyasyētyabhiprāyaḥ । siddhyatyēvaṁ yadi
prāgvidhānādanayōḥ saṁbandhaḥ siddhaḥ syāt agnayē pāvakāyētivat ।﻿<pb n="210"/>
na tvasāvasti । tasmādvidhyuddēśanimitta ēvānayōḥ saṁbandha iti na
padadvayārthasya vidhēyatā saṁbhavati ।</p>
<p>atha kasmādagniprajāpatyōrivāsaṁbandhayōrapi vidhānaṁ na
saṁbhavati ? parasparasambandhāvagamāt । sa ca pramāṇāntarasiddhō nāstīti
vidhyuddēśanimittaka ēva grahītavyaḥ । tasmāt siddhamidamapi
nāmadhēyami[damapīti]ti ।</p>﻿<pb n="211"/>
<p><q>tatprakhyaṁ cānyaśāstram ।</q> kēna punarviśēṣēṇātra guṇavidhyā-
śaṅkā matvarthalakṣaṇābhāvāt guṇavidhānēnāpi sāmānādhikaraṇyōpapaptiḥ । tathā
ca darśitaṁ agnayē hōtramasminniti samāsō'yaṁ hōmavacanaḥ । upasarjanārtha-
vidhānēnāpi guṇavidhirbhavatyēva yathā hiraṇyastraja r̥tvijō bhavanti' iti ।
yuktaṁ tāvat agnihōtraṁ juhōtīti । āghāramāghārayatīti tu﻿<pb n="212"/>
kathaṁ ? naivātra sāmānādhikaraṇyēna prayōjanaṁ, karmavacanataivātra na pratīyata
iti guṇavidhiḥ yatrāghāryaṁ dravyaṁ tatraivēdamāghāraṇaṁ vidhīyatē ।</p>
<p>nanu cāghāryadravyakō yāgaḥ āhavanīyasādhyatvāt prāptāghāraka ēva
kimāghāravidhānēna; hōmāghārādāghārāntaramidaṁ dravyasaṁskārārthamityabhiprāyaḥ
karmasādhanamāghārē śabdaṁ manvānasya । ata ēvōpāṁśuyāja iti
pradarśitam । tasmādakarmavacanatayaivāsmin udāharaṇē pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
agnihōtrē tu karmavacanatvēpi guṇavidhiraviruddha ityuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="213"/>
<p>atrōcyatē—nātra guṇavidhiḥ saṁbhavati । kutaḥ ? prāptatvāt
guṇānāṁ, yē guṇā vidhēyatvēnōpanyastāḥ tē anyata ēva prāptāḥ । agnistāvat
yadagnayē ca prajāpatayē cētyasmāt । āghāraṇamapi <quote>santatamāghārayati</quote>
<quote>r̥jumāghārayati</quote> ityēvamādibhyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="214"/>
kimidamasambaddhamucyatē ? kimidamasaṁbaddhaṁ ? darvihōmē guṇavidhiruktaḥ ।
na ca darvihōma ēvaitadvidhānaṁ yadagnayē ca prajāpatayē cēti । tathō—
pāṁśuyājē āghāraṇamityuktam । na ca santatādayaḥ upāṁ-﻿<pb n="215"/>
śuyājē guṇavidhayaḥ tadidaṁ viyatpadamiva pratibhāti ।</p>
<p>atra vadāmaḥ । guṇavidhipakṣē darvihōma ēvaitadvidhānaṁ upāṁśuyājē
ca gatam । na tarhi tatprakhyatā rāddhāntahētuḥ । bāḍhaṁ rāddhāntahētuḥ
kathaṁ ? tatprakhyatāpi hi darvihōma ēva viṣayāntarāpēkṣitvāt ।﻿<pb n="216"/>
'agnihōtra juhōti' itivat । ēvaṁ santatamāghārayatītyupāṁśuyāja ēva
prayōjanavaddravyāpēkṣitvāt āghāramāghārayatītivat । nāmatāpi hi tarhi
tēṣāmēvōpāṁśuyājasya ca । aprāptijñō dēvānāṁ priyaḥ । anyatō guṇavidhāna-
siddhēḥ । nāmnaścāvidhēyatvāt agnihōtraṁ juhōtītyākhyātārthavidhānāt ।
kimanyadasmādvākyāt pratīyatē vihitē cākhyātārthē yadagnayē ca
prajāpatayēcētyētadviṣayamēva prakaraṇāt । ataḥ siddhamasyaivēdaṁ nāmēti । ēva-
māghārayatītyāpi niṣiddhē guṇavidhānē kimanyadākhyātārthādvidhātum । sa ca﻿<pb n="217"/>
dravyadēvatōpasaṁbandhāddharativadyajatiḥ । ataḥ santatādayō'pi tannaiva ।
tasmādidamapi tasyaiva nāmēti sthitaṁ santatamāghāraṁ nirvartayatītyarthaḥ । kathaṁ
punaratra na vākyabhēdaḥ, yadagnayē ca prajāpatayē cētyanēkaguṇavidhānāt ।
naikakārakaviśēṣaṇavidhānē anēkaguṇavidhānākhyō vākyabhēdaḥ । saṁbandhya-
ntaravidhānaṁ hi anēkaguṇatōcyatē na dravyāntaravidhānam ।</p>﻿<pb n="218"/>
<p><q>tadvyapadēśaṁ ca ।</q> iha rūḍhiśabdā udāharaṇaṁ śyēnājyapr̥ṣṭhādayaḥ ।
kaḥ punaratrōdbhidadhikaraṇēna viśēṣaḥ ? ayamasau; pravr̥tti-
nimittānurōdhī yōgaḥ, rūḍhiḥ punaḥ na yōgamanuvartatē । nanu ca﻿<pb n="219"/>
nāmadhēyatvapakṣēpi śyēnēnēti naiva yōgānuvartitvaṁ kalpayitavyam । kiṁ tarhi ?
gauṇamabhidhānam । na rūḍhiḥ gauṇatāṁ vihanti । rūḍhimūlatvādgauṇā-
bhidhānasya । tasmāta matublōpō niṣpramāṇaka iti varaṁ gauṇataivāśritā ।
idamēvājñānamapanētuṁ bhagavatā bhāṣyakārēṇēdamudāhr̥tam । yuktaṁ matu-
blōpabhayāt yōgāśrayaṇānnāmadhēyamiti vaktumudbhidādiṣu । na puna—﻿<pb n="220"/>
rlōpabhayāllōpāntarāśrayaṇaṁ śyēnē । luptavatikā hi gauṇānāṁ vr̥ttiḥ ।
tasmādvaraṁ matublōpa ēvāśritaḥ śrautārthānvayabhāvitvāditi punaḥ pūrva-
pakṣitam । ucyatē; rūḍhāvapi nāmadhēyataiva nyāyyā । nanu na
rūḍhiryōgamanuvartata ityuktam । yōgō'pi hi naiva rūḍhimanuvartatē ।
nanu cātra pūrvapratītā rūḍhiḥ yōgamapaharati । satyam । yadi nimittā-
vagamapūrvakō vākyārthaḥ । atha tu kāryāvagamapūrvakaṁ nimittatvaṁ tadā﻿<pb n="221"/>
naiva, bhāvārthagatā ca pratipattiḥ । atastadānuguṇyādyōga ēva prathama-
taramavasīyata ityaparigr̥hītā rūḍhiriti pradarśitaṁ vākyaśēṣē yadājimī-
yurityēvamādau । yuktamājyādiṣu; śyēnē tu kathaṁ ? sāmānādhikaraṇyāt
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṁ hi gauṇābhidhānēpyabādhitaṁ, vatyarthasya vidhēyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="222"/>
matublōpē punaḥ bhinnādhikaraṇatā'parihāryaiva vidhēyatvānmatvarthasya । tasmā-
dvatērlōpō na matupa iti siddhaṁ nāmadhēyatvam ।</p>
<p><q>nāmadhēyē guṇaśrutēḥ ।</q> kimarthamidamadhikaraṇaṁ ? yōgika-
prāptārtharūḍhīnāṁ nāmadhēyatvaṁ pratipāditam । śakyatē ca vājapēyē
tatprakhyatā vaktum । surāgrahavidhānāt । sarvanāmākṣēpakabhidamadhikaraṇaṁ﻿<pb n="223"/>
yajēḥ tantrābhidhānōpanyāsāt । tantrābhidhānapakṣē guṇavidhānēpyanapēkṣataiva
śabdasyēti na śakyaṁ nāmābhidhānam । tasmāt tantrābhidhānanirāsāyēda-
madhikaraṇamārabhyatē ।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ tarhi udbhidādayōpyatrōdāharaṇam; bāḍham । kimiti tarhi
vājapēyēna svārājyakāmō yajētētyudāhr̥tam ? śiṁśipācōdyamētat
udbhidādāvapyudāhr̥tē kimityudbhidudāhriyētēti śakyatē vaktum ।﻿<pb n="224"/>
tasmādacōdyamētaccōdyāmahē । śakyatē cātra viśēṣā'pi kaścidvaktum ।
'tulyatvātkriyayōrna' iti । vājapēyagatamētaddarśanam tadapi sarvārthamēva । ata
idamucyatē guṇavidhipakṣaḥ śrēyān iti । kutaḥ ? ēvaṁ hi kāryānvayyu-
dbhidādiḥ padārthō bhavati । nāmadhēyapakṣē punaḥ pravr̥ttinimittamātraṁ padārthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="225"/>
yasmādvihitasyōdbhittvaṁ nōdbhidādividhānaṁ tasmādapravr̥ttyarthaṁ nimittōpādānaṁ
pravr̥ttyarthaṁ vākyamiti kāryanimittayōrasāmañcasyaṁ syāt ।</p>
<p>nanu ca matvarthalakṣaṇā aśabdārthabhūtā''śrayaṇīyētyuktam । saiva
nāstītyucyatē । kathaṁ nāsti ? ākhyātārthō hi kāryakāraṇasaṁbandhēpyē-
karūpō'vagamyatē । sādhyamāna ēva hi sādhanam । ubhayōravagatau kimiti
matvarthalakṣaṇā । tasmādupapannō'yamarthaḥ vājapēyēna yāgaṁ yāgēna svārājyamiti ।﻿<pb n="226"/>
darśanatō'nyathābhidhānaṁ; na punaḥ śabdārthāvagatau ।</p>
<p>nanu vastudharmō'yaṁ na śabdadharmaḥ śabdō hi anyathā vidhēyatayā'vaga-
mayati । anyathā cōddēśyatayā । satyam । sa tūbhayarūpatvāt tathā'bhidhēyatā
ca, ubhayābhidhānēpi yajētēti śabdaḥ saṁbandhinōḥ samarpayituṁ kṣamaḥ । kṣamaścēt
siddhō guṇavidhiḥ prāmāṇyaṁ ca । maivam; tau tvakṣamau tayōścēt sāmarthyaṁ nāsti﻿<pb n="227"/>
kimabhidhānasāmarthyaṁ kariṣyati । tasmāt dvayōrarthayōrvidhānāt kārya-
dvayamidaṁ prāpnōti-yajēta svārājyakāmaḥ vājapēyēna yajēta iti ca
parasparāsambaddham । kiṁ jātaṁ ? parasparaṁ sambandhāvagatiratyaktā bhavati ।
anavagamyamānārthaḥ kalpitō bhavati । tadēvēdaṁ sāpēkṣatvam ।
viruddhā ca matvarthalakṣaṇā । tasmāt uktābhiryuktibhiḥ nāmadhēyapakṣa ēva
samañcasaḥ । yatpunaḥ kāryanimittayōrasāmañcasyamuktaṁ; na, avighātāt ।
vighātē cāsāmañjasyaṁ nānaupayikatvē । tasmādadōṣaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="228"/>
tadguṇāstu vidhīyēran ।</q> kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamārabhyatē ? kō'yaṁ praśnaḥ ?
nanu cāgnēyādayō guṇavidhayaḥ na nāmadhēyānīti jñātuṁ; yuktam yaugika-﻿<pb n="229"/>
prāptārtharūḍhīnāṁ nāmatvam । na ca 'āgnēyō'ṣṭākapāla' ityatra
nāmadhēyatvaṁ saṁbhavati । ākhyātārthasāmānādhikaraṇyāddhi nāmatōktā
na cātra bhavatītyākhyātamavidhēyārthatvāt bhāvārthaṁm na cāsau vidhēyaḥ
na cōktāddhētōḥ hētvantaraṁ nāmadhēyē'stīti praśnaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="230"/>
<p>atrōcyatē—punarapi sāpēkṣataivātra śaṅkyatē, kathaṁ ? yathaivātra
nāmadhēyatvaṁ na saṁbhavati bhāvārthasāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvāt tathā guṇavidhānamapi
vidhēyabhāvārthāśravaṇāt ।</p>
<p>nanvāgnēya iti dravyadēvatāsaṁyōgaśravaṇāt yajyarthō bhāvārthaḥ, satyaṁ yadi
dravyadēvatāsaṁyōgaḥ śrūyatē । nanu cāgnēya iti śrūyatē; satyam, yadyaṣṭā-﻿<pb n="231"/>
kapālaviṣayō na syāt । yadyaṣṭākapālaviṣayaḥ tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tatō
bhavati । avihitaivāṣṭākapālatā pratipattavyā । na cāvihitō'ṣṭāka-
pālō'sti ।</p>
<p>nanu aṣṭasu kapālēṣu śrr̥tō yaḥ sō'ṣṭākapālō laukikaḥ;
vācanikō vā, kapālēṣu śrayayatīti vacanādvā । vācanikastāvanna
sambhavati aṣṭasaṅkhyāśravaṇāt । saṅkhyā vidhīyata iti cainna;
itarētarāśrayaprasaṅgāt āgnēyē saṅkhyā saṅkhyāyāmāgnēya iti ।﻿<pb n="232"/>
tasmānna guṇavidhiḥ sambhavati । na ca nāmētyuktam । kathaṁ tarhi
nāmadhēyamityuktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa ? kva vōktam ? upanyāsē kiṁ nāmadhēyaṁ
uta guṇavidhiriti । guṇavidhipratiṣēdhaṁ ca kurvatā nāmadhēyamityuktaṁ bhavati
satyamuktaṁ na tu vidhēyasya । atō nāmagrahaṇāt prasiddhārthatā darśitā ।
prasiddhiśca pramāṇāntarādr̥tē na bhavatīti sāpēkṣatvaṁ prayōgasya darśitam ।
atrōcyatē । syādētadēvaṁ yadi saṅkhyāsambandhē dēvatāsambandhē cētarētarā-
śrayaḥ syāt । na tvasāvasti । aṣṭākapālasya dēvatāvidhiḥ । nanu cāsāva-﻿<pb n="233"/>
prasiddha ityuktam । kimabhidhēyatayāpi ? na, kāryatayā । iṣṭamēvaitata,
ata ēva vidhīyatē । tasmādabhidhānāprasiddhiḥ vidhānaṁ vihanti ।
na punaḥ kāryatayāpyaprasiddhiḥ tasmādyajyarthasyēva siddhamaṣṭāka-
pālārthasya vidhānam । prasiddhābhidhānaṁ caitat pradarśitaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa
'nānyēna śrapitaṁ gr̥hṇāti' iti । tasmādyajyarthavat taddhitārthō'yamapi
prasiddhaḥ । atō na sāpēkṣatvaprasaṅgaḥ । na ca prāptārthatā'gnihōtravatsambhavati ।﻿<pb n="234"/>
<p><q>barhirājyayōrasaṁskārē ।</q> prāsaṅgikamidamadhikaraṇam । kaḥ punaḥ
prasaṅgaḥ ? vidhēyēnāpyarthēna nāmārthānvayō dr̥ṣṭaḥ । ayamapi cājyaśabdaḥ
karmanimitta ēva lōkē dr̥ṣṭaḥ । tasmādayamapi kāryānvayī saṁskārēṇājyaṁ kuryā-
diti । nanu cākarmanimittakō'pi kvacit dr̥ṣṭaḥ <quote> ājyaṁ krayyaṁ</quote> 'barhirādāya
gāvō gatāḥ' iti । sārvabhaumō hi prayōgaḥ śrautō bhavitumarhati naikadēśa﻿<pb n="235"/>
prabhavaḥ । kasmāt ? prasiddhasya śrautē'rthē gauṇatā saṁbhavati ।
na cāyaṁ sarvatra ghr̥tavacanatayā prasiddhaḥ । aprasiddhasya ghr̥tē gauṇatvaṁ
nōpapadyatē । karmaṇā sādhanē yatra punarēkadēśē prayujyatē tatra karmanimitta-
kēpi prayōgātsiddhō ghr̥tē gauṇaḥ । tasmātkāryārthataiva yuktā</p>﻿<pb n="236"/>
<p>atrōcyatē । na kāryārthatayānvayō ghaṭatē itarētarāśrayatvaprasaṅgāt
barhiṣaḥ prōkṣaṇaṁ prōkṣaṇēna ca barhiriti । kathaṁ tarhi aṣṭākapālē na ?
na, abhidhānataḥ prasiddhērityuktam ? iha punaḥ kāryata ēvābhidhānamiti
vaiṣamyam । yūpē katham ? anyataḥ prasiddhyabhāvādagatikā gatiriyam ।
kēyamagatikā gatiḥ ? kiṁ na śāstrādavagamyatē ? satyāṁ prasiddhau
nāvagamyatē ? aprasiddhē punaḥ padārthē apratihatatvādvidhyarthasya kalpyatē ।﻿<pb n="237"/>
<p>yaduktaṁ sārvabhaumō gauṇō na saṁbhavati śrautasyāprasiddhēḥ; ēka-
dēśasthastu saṁbhavatīti; nāvaśyaṁ prasiddhaścautārthamēva gauṇaṁ prayuñjatē
laukikāḥ rājaśabdamiva kṣatriyēpi । tatrāpi tulyō dōṣaḥ sādr̥śyaprati-
pattyarthaṁ hi gauṇaṁ prayuñjatē । atadbuddhyāpi gauṇaṁ prayuñjata iti
haṭhō'yam । atrābhidhīyatē । na prayōkturvivakṣāmapēkṣatē śabdārthasambandhaḥ ।
saṁbandhāpēkṣā hi vivakṣā ।</p>﻿<pb n="238"/>
<p>uktaṁ hi gōpōtalikādiṣu aśaktijatvāparijñānādanādimiva prayuñjata
iti sa ēvamatrāpi vivakṣāparijñānāt kasyacit prayōkturvivakṣāśūnyamarthāntarē
prayuñjatē । kathaṁ punaridamavagamyatē ? lōkē vēdē ca vyavahāradarśanāt । vēdē
tāvadājyaṁ vidhāya ghr̥taśabdēna stauti । lōkēpi vā ājyaṁ krayyamiti kriyā-
sādhananirapēkṣaḥ prayōgaḥ । nanu ca tatrāpyajñātavivakṣā(rtha)tvaṁ śakyatē vaktum ।</p>﻿<pb n="239"/>
<p>uktō vaitasādiṣu parihāraḥ । vaidikavyavahārasāmyāt vipratipattau
nirṇaya iti । kiṁ punaḥ prāsaṅgikasya prayōjanam ? anavadhyavasāya ēva ।
nanu ca bhāṣyakārēṇa karmaṇyēva viśēṣaḥ pradarśitaḥ ata ēvānadhyavasāyaḥ
prayōjanam । nirṇayē tvadhyavasānāt sthitamēva prayōjanam ।</p>﻿<pb n="240"/>
<p><q>prōkṣaṇīṣvarthasaṁyōgāt ।</q> kimarthamidaṁ pr̥thagadhikaraṇaṁ ? sārva-
bhaumaikadēśaprabhavayōḥ smr̥titō'pavādaḥ kathyatē । kathaṁ punaḥ prayōgasya
smr̥titō'pavādaḥ kathyatē ? sambhavati smr̥tyānuguṇyaṁ prayōgasya । yasmāt
dvayōravayavayōgaḥ saṁbhavati 'prōkṣaṇīrāsādayati' 'prōkṣaṇībhirudvējitāḥ smaḥ'
iti । tasmāt smr̥titō nirṇaya iti । śēṣamuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="241"/>
<p><q>tathā nirmanthyē ।</q> kimatrātiricyatē ? idamatrātiricyatē । smr̥ti-
rapyativyāpikā aciranirmathitē darśanāt । ataḥ smr̥titō'pi na nirṇaya﻿<pb n="242"/>
iti manyatē । aviśēṣavidhānāt smr̥tērna viśēṣaprayōgō vihantuṁ
kṣamaḥ । vihantyaviśēṣajñānamiti cēt, na vihanti viśēṣaparisamāptē—
raviśēṣasya । tasmāt pūrvavadidamapi । tēna tathētyuktam ।</p>
<p><q>vaiśvadēvē vikalpa iti cēt ।</q> kathaṁ punaḥ guṇavidhi-
nāmadhēyatayātra saṁśayaḥ ? guṇavidhipakṣa ēvātra sāmānādhikaraṇya-﻿<pb n="243"/>
mupapannataram । pratyayārthatvāt bhāvasya । kimiti tarhi nāmadhēya-
tayōpanyāsaḥ ? viṣayābhāvādvidhānasya । kimiti viṣayābhāvaḥ ?
agnyādibhiḥ śrutyāvaruddhatvāt prakr̥tānāṁ karmaṇām । karmāntaraṁ
kimiti na bhavati ? tadapi nādhyavasīyatē prakr̥tatvādāmikṣāyāḥ ।﻿<pb n="244"/>
tasmānna nāmatō nāpi guṇatō'napēkṣatvaṁ śakyatē'vagantumiti । cēnmanyasē
anapēkṣatvādhyavasānaṁ na śakyatē kartumiti bhavatu guṇavidhānēna
adhyavasānam tathā'vagamānnāmākhyātārthasambandhasya । nanu cōktō viṣayā-
bhāvaḥ, duruktō hi saḥ । kathaṁ duruktaḥ ? śrutāddhi kāryakalpanā, na kāryataḥ
śrutam । kimidaṁ ? idamidaṁ, utpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarōdhō hyanavagamē hētuḥ ।
na punaravagatasya vighātē । vaiśvadēvaśabdaścāyaṁ ākhyātārtha ēva vartatē ।
nāgnyādayaḥ saṁbandhinamākhyātārthaṁ vaiśvadēvaśabdābhidhētayā nivārayituṁ﻿<pb n="245"/>
kṣamāḥ । sambandhyantaraviṣayatāṁ nivārayanti nābhidhēyatām । tataḥ
kim ? idaṁ tatō bhavati abhidhēyōpapattyarthaṁ sambandhyantaraprāptiḥ nōtpatti-
saṁbandhinō'gnyādayaḥ vighnanti । tathā saṁskāryatayā''kṣiptaṁ phalacamasasya
yāgasādhanabhāvaṁ sōmaḥ । tasmādvikalpēnādhyavasānam । na prakaraṇāt
pratyakṣavidhānācca । na hi prakaraṇaṁ dravyasya ।</p>
<p>yadyēvaṁ nāmadhēyataivāstu; abhidhānōpapattyarthaṁ hi guṇāntarasaṁbandhaḥ﻿<pb n="246"/>
kalpyatē । atulyapramāṇaśiṣṭānāṁ tvavikalpaḥ tattu nāmadhēyatayai-
vōpapadyatē ।</p>
<p>nanu cāvayavārthō'vagamyamānaḥ kāryānanvayī syāt । nānvita-
syānvayō nyāyyaḥ anvitaścāmikṣāyāmarthaḥ । tasmāt kāryānanvayō nābhidhānaṁ
vārayitumutsahatē । tasmānna vikalpaḥ kalpayituṁ śakyatē । nāpyāvr̥ttiḥ
karmaṇaḥ ataḥ nāmatayaivādhyavasānaṁ nyāyyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="247"/>
<p>kathaṁ punaravaiśvadēvē vaiśvadēvābhidhānam । guṇavidhau punarvidhānataḥ
siddhyati । satyamēvaṁ yadyēkāntatō vidhānataḥ siddhyati । āmikṣāyāṁ
hi anabhidhānaprasaṅgāt । tulyaṁ ca prakr̥tatvam । kataratpunaranayōḥ
balīyaḥ ? na vidhēyasyāvidhēyābhidhānaṁ siddhyati । bhavati ca tulyayōgināṁ
lakṣaṇābhidhānaṁ nāmapakṣē daṇḍinō gacchantīti ca । tasmājjyāyānayaṁ
pakṣaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="248"/>
<p><q>pūrvavantō'vavidhānārthāḥ । uktaṁ vidhyuddēśārthavādamantravidhibhiḥ
prāmāṇyam । iha punaḥ aṣṭākapālē mantratvaṁ nāsti । ataścōdakatvāt
nāmadhēyamapi na sambhavati sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvāt aṣṭākapālādiṣu ।
arthavādaguṇavidhānatvaṁ tu sandihyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="249"/>
<p>tatra guṇavidhānaṁ tāvanna sandihyatē, viṣayābhāvāt । kathamabhāvaḥ ?
guṇāntarōtpattinirōdhāt । purōḍāśakapālē tu abhāvārthatvādēvāviṣayaḥ ।
tathā'rthavādō'pi dvādaśasaṅkhyā saṅkhyāntaranirōdhāt na tatsambandhitayā
stutiḥ 'āpaḥ śāntā' itivat । tasmāt pratibhāmātratvāt punarapyana-
pēkṣatvākṣēpaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="250"/>
<p>ēvaṁ sthitē kaścit guṇavidhānēna prāmāṇyaṁ manyatē kō'bhiprāyaḥ ?
kimutpattinirōdhaṁ na paśyati ? na na paśyati sahavākyabhramāt
sarvasaṅkhyāyuktaṁ nirvapatiṁ manyatē । ēkavākyatvāt । ataścāvr̥ttiḥ
karmaṇō vikalpō vā guṇānāmityabhiprāyaḥ । vaiśvānaraṁ dvādaśakapālamiti
dēvatārthamupakramaṁ manyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="251"/>
<p>atrōcyatē । na guṇavidhānāt prāmāṇyaṁ śakyatē
vaktuṁ viṣayābhāvāt । nanu vaiśvānaradēvatākaṁ karma viṣaya
ityuktam । na tat, dvādaśakapālavirōdhāt । <quote>'yadaṣṭākapāla'</quote>
ityēvamādinā saṅkhyāvidhānamiti yaduktaṁ duruktaṁ tat । kathaṁ ?﻿<pb n="252"/>
vaiśvānaraśabdasya vyatiriktārthavibhaktivacanatvāt । dvādaśakapālaśabdasya
ca sāmānādhikaraṇyaṁ śrautam । yadaṣṭākapāla ityēvamādīnāṁ brahmavarcasapunāti
padasaṁbandhānna vaiśvānarapadārthādhikaraṇatā'vagamyatē । punātistutyanyathānu-
papattyā tu kalpanīyaḥ sambandhaḥ । na ca kalpanā klr̥ptau upapadyata ityuktam ।﻿<pb n="253"/>
ēvaṁ tarhi pratibhaiva, na, stutyarthatayaivōpapattēḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ stutyarthatōpapadyatē ?
nirastatvāt saṅkhyāyāḥ saṅkhyāntarēṇētyuktam । abhidhānatō hi nirāsaḥ,
nāsadbhāvataḥ sadbhāvanimittaśca saṁbandhō, nābhidhānimittaḥ sadbhāvē satya-
vayuttyābhidhānamupapadyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="254"/>
<p>nanvavayōjitasya saṁbandhānavagamaḥ prāpnōti abhidhānārthamēvā-
vayōjanaṁ śakyatē na punaḥ saṁbandhitāpyavayōjayituṁ śakyatē । vivakṣāhya-
bhidhānamanuvartatē na vastu । tasmāta āpaḥ śāntā itivadupapannā
stutiḥ । tathā ca darśitaṁ śōbhanamasya cakrasya nēmitumbāramiti﻿<pb n="255"/>
guṇaphalasaṁbandhavidhānamapyētasmādēva na saṁbhavati । kasmāt ētasmāt ?
stutyarthatvēnaikavākyatāvagamāt । taddarśitamupakramōpasaṁhārābhyām । ataḥ
stutyarthatayōpapattēḥ siddhamanapēkṣatvam ।</p>
<p>tatsiddhiḥ । uktamavayutyābhidhānataḥ saṁbandhēna stutirupapadyata
iti । yatra punaḥ saṁbandhitaiva nāvagamyatē । na ca guṇavidhānaṁ sambhavati
yathā 'yajamāna ēkapālaḥ' 'yajamānaḥ prastara' iti tatra kathaṁ prāmāṇyam ?﻿<pb n="256"/>
<p>nanu ca gauṇamukhyādhikaraṇē sthitaṁ yathā gauṇaḥ saṁbandhō'rthāntara-
vācināmapi bhavatīti । tadēvēdaṁ na mr̥ṣyatē । kasmāt ? naiva gauṇatā
sambhavati arthāntarasaṁbandhitayā । kathaṁ punarna saṁbhavati ? gauṇē hyabhidhānē
guṇānāmēva vācyatvaṁ yuktam । anyathā śauryamēva siṁhaśabdō dēvadattē prati-
pādayati, jvalanaśabdaśca māṇavakē piṅgalatāmiti nōpapadyatē । siṁhajāti-﻿<pb n="257"/>
mukhēna siṁhaśabdō guṇān pratipādayan yāvantō jātyabhisambandhā
guṇāstān pratipādayēt, aviśēṣāt ।</p>
<p>atha manyasē tāvanmātravivakṣāyāṁ sa ēva pratīyata iti ।
vivakṣānuvartī tarhi śabdaḥ nābhidhēyānuvartī । tataḥ kiṁ ?
adhyārōpitatadbhāvō gauṇaḥ । adhyārōpē ca nārthāntarasambandhaḥ ।
kimiti ? adhyārōpō hi adhigatārthaviṣaya ēva nānadhigataṁ
vastu spr̥śati । sa ēvēti gr̥hyatē na tatsadr̥śa iti ।﻿<pb n="258"/>
tasmāt prastaraikakapālayōḥ yajamānaśabdō nālaṁ stutau । guṇavidhistarhi
bhavatu । asāvapyasaṁbhavānnaiva bhavati । guṇō vidhīyamānaḥ kāryārthē'tra
vidhīyatē । sa cōbhayathāpi nōpapadyatē । tadētaddarśitaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa ।
tasmātsaivēyaṁ pratibhāśaṅkā ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē । satyaṁ guṇavidhirna saṁbhavati arthavādastu na 
nivārayituṁ śakyatē । nanu cārthāsambandhānnārthavāda ityuktam ।
ayuktamuktam । kathaṁ ? saṁbhavati svārthasaṁbandhitayaiva gauṇamabhidhānam ।</p>﻿<pb n="259"/>
<p>nanu svārthasaṁbandhiguṇamātrānavagamānnētyuktam । vivakṣātō
viśēṣa ityēvadapyuktam । satyamuktam । vivakṣāyāṁ hi nābhi-
dhēyasaṁbandhō'stītyapyuktam । tataśca stutyanupapattiḥ । kiṁ kēna saṁbadhyatē ।
atrōcyatē—na, aniyamajñaḥ khalvasi । abhidhēyāvivakṣāyāṁ siṁha-﻿<pb n="260"/>
śabdōccāraṇamanibandhanam । na ca śabdāntarēṇādhyārōpābhidhānaṁ nōpa-
padyatē । manda maivaṁ, adhyārōpaviṣayatayā hi siṁhārthō vivakṣyatē,
na guṇasaṁbandhitayā । na cāsau siṁhaśabdādr̥tē saṁbhavati
tasmānnanibandhanaṁ siṁhaśabdōccāraṇam । nanu cāsmābhiridamuktam ।﻿<pb n="261"/>
kimiti siṁhārthō dēvadēttē adhyārōpyata iti । tadguṇadarśanāditi
cēt; prāptaṁ tarhi mukhyārthasaṁbandhitayā pratipādanam । kathaṁ viśēṣā-
vagatiḥ iti cēt । pramāṇāntaradarśanāt tatpūrvakatvācca gauṇasya ।﻿<pb n="262"/>
mukhyō'pi tāvadarthaḥ pramāṇāntaradarśanādviśēṣē vyavasthāsyāti gauṇō
nēti kā yuktiḥ ? kathaṁ tarhi khapuṣpamiti ? yathaiva khapuṣpamiti ।
tasmātsiddhō'rthavādaḥ । kiṁ prayōjanaṁ kathaṁ cēti darśitaṁ bhāṣyē ।</p>
<p>jātiḥ । jātyādiṣvapyēvamēva yōjyam । pr̥thagadhikaraṇāni tu parihārānyatva-﻿<pb n="263"/>
pradarśanārthāni । tasmāt gauṇārthānāmarthavādatayā sthitaṁ prāmāṇyam ।
lākṣaṇikārthānāṁ ca । kathaṁ punaḥ sr̥ṣṭyādiṣu lakṣaṇānāmapi
lakṣyatvam ? lakṣyaiḥ sahaikakriyāyōgāt । tasmāllakṣaṇatvē nimitta-
tvāt । atō lakṣyalakṣaṇatēti na virōdhaḥ । aśvādiṣu kathaṁ paśuśabdō﻿<pb n="264"/>
lakṣaṇayā । pratiṣēdhapūrvakatvāt prayōgasya । pratiṣiddhō hi
tajjātīyēṣu jātiśabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ tajjātīyāntarēṣu gauṇatayaiva
prayōgaṁ labhatē । kasmāt ? jātiśabdō hi tajjātīyē pratiṣidhyamānaḥ
samavētasya guṇasya pratiṣēdhyatayaiva pratiṣēdhaviṣayō bhavati । guṇapratiṣēdhācca
tajjātīyēṣvēva prayujyamānō gauṇārtha ēva pratīyatē । tasmājjātiśabdō
gauṇa ityavirōdhaḥ । ataḥ siddhamanapēkṣatvam ।</p>﻿<pb n="265"/>
﻿<pb n="266"/>﻿<pb n="267"/>
<p><q>sandigdhēṣu vākyaśēṣāt ।</q> nanu ca yavavarāhādiṣu vākyaśēṣāt
sandēhāpanayaḥ kr̥taḥ ? satyaṁ, padārthaviṣayastu saḥ, autpattikānautpattikatayā
sandihyamānaḥ padārthō nirṇītaḥ । asti vā padasyārthaḥ ? bāḍhamasti ।﻿<pb n="268"/>
kathaṁ tarhi vākyavākyārthayōrautpattikatvaṁ vr̥ddhavyavahārāt । satyaṁ, sa
tvavayavaśa ityuktaṁ tadbhūtānāmityatra । tasmāt tadbhūtē tatra sandēhaḥ ।
iha tu kriyārthē । sō'yaṁ padārthavākyārthayōḥ viśēṣaḥ । pratipāditaścāyaṁ
vistarēṇa । ataḥ kriyārthasaṁśayādapyaprāmāṇyam । ēvaṁ sthitē kaści-
dupakramavaśādupasaṁhāranirṇayō yukta iti manyatē, avirōdhāt । sāmānyaṁ hi
svātmani viśēṣē ca vartatē । sr̥ṣṭyarthavat । atrōcyatē । syādētadēvaṁ yadi﻿<pb n="269"/>
vākyāntaravihitaṁ sāmānyaṁ syāt । iha punaḥ viśēṣaparyantaivānvayāvagatiḥ
ēkavākyatvāt । tasmādvākyaśēṣāpēkṣaṁ kriyārthatvamiti siddham ।</p>
<p>arthādvā kalpanaikadēśatvāt । yatrāpyanuṣṭhānē saṁśayaḥ tatrāpi
śāstramēva sandigdhaṁ manyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="270"/>
<p>nanu caitadayuktam anuṣṭhānasandēhātśāstramēva sandigdhamiti śāstra-
pūrvakatvōdanumānasya । satyaṁ yathā bhavānāha siddhānuśāsanē । kāryānu-
śāsanē tvāskandatyanuṣṭhānasaṁśayō'pi śāstram । kimanuṣṭhānaṁ na śāstrapūrvakaṁ ?
satyamanubandhē śāstrapūrvakam । niyōgārthaṁ tvanuṣṭhānam । tasmādupapannāṁ
niyōgārthasaṁśayaḥ । sa punaḥ sāmarthyatō nirṇētavyaḥ anuṣṭhānasyāsaṁbhāvyāt ।
sāmarthyasādhyatvāccānuṣṭhāsya । tasmānmāṁsādiṣu darśitā vyavasthā bhāṣyakārēṇa﻿<pb n="271"/>
atō vidhyarthavādamantrasmr̥tināmadhēyānuṣṭhānatō'pēkṣatākṣēpaṁ kr̥tvā sthāpitaṁ
prāmāṇyaṁ cōdanāyāḥ । iti pramāṇalakṣaṇam ।
iti śrīmatprabhākaramiśraviracitāyāṁ
śavarabhāṣyaṭīkāyāṁ br̥hatyāṁ
prathamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ
pādaḥ samāptaḥ﻿<pb n="272"/>
<head>atha dvitīyō'dhyāyaḥ</head>
<p><quote>prathamē'dhyāyē pramāṇalakṣaṇaṁ vr̥tta</quote>iti । yathā pramāṇaṁ śabdaḥ
tathōktamityarthaḥ । kutaḥ <quote>yasmādvidhyarthavādamantrasmr̥tayaḥ tattvatō nirṇītāḥ ।﻿<pb n="273"/>
guṇavidhirnāmadhēyaṁ ca parīkṣitam । sandigdhānāmarthānāṁ vākyaśēṣā-
darthāccādhyavasānamuktam</quote> । ētē cākṣēpahētravō'nyathāgr̥hyamāṇāḥ । tattvatastu
parijñātā na prāmāṇyaṁ vighnanti । atastattvatō nirṇītā yasmāt
tasmāt—'uktaṁ pramāṇalakṣaṇaṁ' ityuktam ।</p>
<p><quote>tanna prasmartavyaṁ</quote> ityanapēkṣatvasavyapēkṣaṁ bhēdābhēdakathanam ।
kasmāt ? kāryasya hi bhēdābhēdaḥ kathyatē । sa cānapēkṣatvanibandhanaḥ ।
anyasavyapēkṣē hi śabdē śabdādēva kāryavibhāgō na śakyatē vaktum ।
tasmādanapēkṣatvādityēvaṁ na prasmartavyamityuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="274"/>
<p>anantaramiti kasmāt ? anyadapi hi lakṣaṇaṁ śēṣādi ana-
pēkṣatvasavyapēkṣamēva śabdānnirṇētuṁ śakyatē । satyaṁ śakyaṁ na punarana-
ntaram । idamēva tvanantaramityabhiprāyēṇōkmam । kasmātpunaridamēvā-
nantaraṁ na śēṣalakṣaṇādi ? kāryabhēdapūrvakatvāta sarvasthōparitanasya,﻿<pb n="275"/>
<quote>pradhānāpradhānāni parākṣyantē । bhinnānyabhinnāni cēti</quote> । kimidaṁ pradhānā-
pradhānānīti ? yadi tāvat parīkṣiṣyanta iti saṁbadhyatē anyat pratijñātaṁ
anyatparīkṣitaṁ syāt । bhēdābhēdaparīkṣā hyanantaraṁ dr̥śyatē, na punaḥ
pradhānāpradhānaparīkṣā ।</p>
<p>nanu cētarattadarthaṁ—yaimtudravyaṁ cikīrṣyata iti pradhānā-
pradhānaparīkṣāpyanantaraṁ dr̥śyata ēva । naitadēvam । tr̥tīyasiddhaṁ hi
tat । saṁvyavahārārthamihānītaṁ kāryabhēdaprasiddhyē । tathā ca bhāṣyakārēṇa
svayamēvōktam <quote>yaistudravyaṁ cikīrṣyatē guṇastatra pratīyētēti ।
tatrāpūrvārthatā vyāvartitā dr̥ṣṭapraṁyōjanānāmākhyātārthānām । iha
tu sarvēṣāmēva śēṣāṇāṁ lakṣaṇamucyata</quote> iti । tasmātpradhānāpradhānā-﻿<pb n="276"/>
nītyasaṁbaddham । ucyatē । pradhānāpradhānānīti sādhyānubandhā abhidhīyantē ।
atastāni pradhānāpradhānānīti parīkṣiṣyantē bhinnānyabhinnāni cēti ।
anubandhabhēdastāvat—yajati dadāti juhōtīti । anubandhābhēdōpi ya
ēvaṁ vidvān paurṇamāsīṁ yajata iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="277"/>
<p>āgnēyō'ṣṭākapāla iti । tasmātsūktam—<quote>pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣiṣyantē
bhinnānyabhinnāni</quote> cēti । <quote>ēṣa ēvārthō varṇanīyō nānya</quote> ityanantara-
śabdavyākhyānam । <quote>ēṣa cādhyāyasaṁbandha</quote> ityānantaryasya hētvabhidhānaṁ
tathā pradarśitamasmābhiḥ ।</p>
<p><quote>tadiha ṣaṅvidhaḥ karmabhēdō vakṣyatē-śabdāntaramabhyāsaḥ saṅkhyā
guṇaḥ prakriyā nāmadhēyamiti । kathaṁ karmabhēdaḥ śabdāntaraṁ ?﻿<pb n="278"/>
bhidyatē'nē nēti bhēdaḥ tacca karma tasmāt karmabhēda ityuktam ।
vakṣyamāṇakramānapēkṣaṁ śabdāntarādīnāṁ vyutkramēṇōccāraṇaṁ kramasyānaupayikatva-
pradarśanārtham । vakṣyamāṇamanusaṅkīrtyata iti kimarthaṁ ? hētvabhidhānakāla ēva
pratijñābhidhānaṁ nyāyyaṁ naiyāyikā manyantē ।</p>﻿<pb n="279"/>
<p>satyaṁ, sādhyē sukhagrahaṇārthaṁ caitat, śrōtr̥buddhisamādhānāt । <quote>tadē
tannānākarmalakṣaṇaṁ</quote> iti pūrvācāryābhidhānaprasiddhiṁ darśayati anāditāṁ
nyāyasya kathayitum । <quote>atōnyadupōdghātāt prasaktānuprasaktaṁ ca</quote>
iti—apratijñātārthacintādōṣaparihārārtham । prathamaṁ tāvadidaṁ
cintyatē prathamē'dhyāyē idamuktam cōdanālakṣaṇō'rthō dharma iti
cōdanēti kriyāyā abhidhāyakaṁ vākyam । vākyē ca padānāmarthaḥ﻿<pb n="280"/>
tatra kiṁ padēna padēna dharmaḥ ucyatē-uta sarvairēka iti sambandhaḥ ।
prathamē'dhyāyē idamuktamityasya kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ kēna vā sambadhyatē
atō na vidmaḥ kathamidaṁ vyākhyēyamiti ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē—kiṁ padēna padēnēti prakriyāvirōdhaṁ manvānaḥ
vākyavākyārthayōrautpattikatvābhidhānāt । tasyēdamuttaram । satyaṁ
prathamē'dhyāyē idamuktam—cōdanālakṣaṇō'rthō dharma iti । cōdanā ca
vākyaṁ vākyē ca padānāmartha ityuktam tadbhūtānāmiti ।﻿<pb n="281"/>
tatō yuktamēvēdaṁ kiṁ padēna padēna dharma ucyatē uta sarvairēka iti । ētaduktaṁ
bhavati-kiṁ padēna padēnābhihitārthasya kāryayōgitā, uta parasparasambandhasavya-
pēkṣasyēti । kathaṁ punaḥ parasparasambandhitayā'vagamyamānasyārthasyāsambandhina
ēva kāryayōgitā । dr̥ṣṭā hi aruṇādiṣu dravyaguṇayōḥ । nanu tatrāvagatirēva
nāstītyuktam । satyamēvam । aidamarthyēna nāstītyuktam, na guṇaguṇitayā;
anyathā niyama ēva hi na syāt । ēvamatrāpi nāmākhyātayōḥ, kriyākāraka-
sambandhanirapēkṣa ēva niyōgasambandhaḥ utājahatkriyākārakasaṁbandha ēvētyupapannaḥ﻿<pb n="282"/>
saṁśayaḥ । kiṁ tāvatprāptaṁ ? asmin saṁśayē kiṁ tāvadyuktamityarthaḥ ।
pratipadaṁ dharmā iti yuktam । kasmāt ? niyōgārthatvāduccāraṇasya sarva-
padānām । nanu ca kriyākārakasaṁbandhō'pyatrāvagamyatē । satyamavagamyatē,
na tu kriyārthatvē kārakāṇāṁ pramāṇamasti । niyōgārthasya sādhyatvēnā-
vagamāt । kathaṁ punaḥ nirvyāpāramēva kārakaṁ niyōgārthamabhiniṣpādayati,
karma vā'kriyamāṇaṁ ? bhavatvarthādayaṁ dravyaguṇayōriva sambandhaḥ tādarthyaṁ tu
niyōgāyaiva ।</p>﻿<pb n="283"/>
<p>tasmāt pratipadaṁ dharmaḥ । atrōcyatē—naitadupapadyatē, yadi
hyajahatāṁ pratītamarthaṁ niyōgārthatā na syāt syāt pratipadaṁ dharmaḥ ।
yatra punarapēkṣitaiva saṁbandhāvagatirānuguṇyēna tatra tattyāgē śrutahāna-
mēva syāt । na caitadyuktam । tasmādanyatarānugr̥hītō'nyaparō vidhyartha
iti । <quote>ēvaṁ cādr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅkalpanā laghīyasī bhaviṣyati</quote> । kā﻿<pb n="284"/>
punaratrādr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā ? śabdādapi hi dr̥ṣṭaṁ dr̥ṣṭamēva ।
satyaṁ yathā bhavānāha । pratipadaṁ kalpanāyāmāśrayāśrayi(bhāva)prasaṅgē niya-
mānumānamadr̥ṣṭamapramāṇakaṁ prāpnōtītyarthaḥ । tatra bahvadr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā
kathaṁ ? ēvaṁ tāvadāśrayatvaṁ kārakāṇāṁ, āśrayitvaṁ karmaṇāṁ, punaśca tatsiddhayē
sādhyasādhanatvaṁ viśēṣaniyamaścēti । anyatarānugr̥hītapakṣē punaḥ
alpīyasyadr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā bhaviṣyatīti ।</p>
<p>kimidaṁ adr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅkalpanēti ? adr̥ṣṭamanumānaṁ yasyāsau
adr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅgaḥ tasya kalpanā adr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā alpīyasī﻿<pb n="285"/>
bhaviṣyati । nanu ca naiva bhavati । kimalpīyasī bhavatītyucyatē ।
anyatarānugr̥hītapakṣēpi vidhyarthasyaiva vidyatē kalpanā । nanu ca
śābdamēvēdaṁ kimatra kalpyatē ? kāryatō'vagamaṁ navamē vakṣyāmaḥ ।
śabdāvagatakāryamūlatvācca śābdam । tasmātsādhūktam—ēvamalpīyasya-
dr̥ṣṭānumānakalpanēti । <quote>tasmādēkamapūrvamiti</quote> kimidamēkama-
pūrvamiti ? nanvidamēva । naivamēkasmādapūrvamiti prakramāt ।
atrābhidhīyatē । yadā pratipadaṁ dharmaḥ tadā pratipadaṁ niyōgabhēdēna
bhavitavyam । pratipadamanubandhabhēdāt । amumēva kāryabhēdaṁ darśayituṁ﻿<pb n="286"/>
bhagavatā bhāṣyakārēṇa phalēnōpasaṁhr̥tam। tasmādēkamapūrvamiti ।।</p>
<p><quote>yadā ēkamapūrvaṁ tadā sandēhaḥ-kiṁ bhāvaśabdēbhyaḥ uta dravyaguṇa-
śabdēbhya iti</quote> ।। bhāvaśabdagrahaṇēna kasya grahaṇaṁ ? ākhyātānāmēva ।
ēvaṁ tarhi nāmaśabdēbhyaḥ utākhyātaśabdēbhya iti vaktavyam । kimida-
mucyatē । kiṁ bhāvaśabdēbhyaḥ uta dravyaguṇaśabdēbhya iti ।﻿<pb n="287"/>
kiṁ vātrātiricyatē ? dviruccaritō nāmaśabdaḥ । anabhiprāyajñō bhavān ।
yadi hi kimākhyātaśabdēbhyaḥ uta nāmaśabdēbhya ityucyatē tataśca nirṇīyatē
ākhyātaśabdēbhya iti tadā āgnēyō'ṣṭākapāla ityakriyārthaḥ syāt;
nāmatvāt, bhavatīti ca kriyārthaḥ syāt ākhyātatvāt । aniṣṭaṁ caitat
bhavatyarthasyāvidhēyatvāt । dravyadēvatāsaṁbandhasya ca vidhēyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="288"/>
tasmānnāmākhyātagrahaṇaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa na kr̥tam । kiṁ tarhi,
yēnaiva svabhāvēnākhyātasya vidhyarthatā saṁbhavati yēna ca nāmnō na saṁbhavati
tēnaiva svabhāvēnōpanyāsaḥ kr̥taḥ । kēna punaḥ svabhāvēnākhyātasya vidhyarthatā ?
kēna ca nāmnō na bhavati ? bhāvārthatayā''khyātasya vidhyarthatā ।
dravyaguṇābhadhānatayā ca na nāmnaḥ । <quote>kaḥ punarayamākhyātārthavyatiriktō
bhāvō nāma</quote> ? kaścākhyātaśabdādanyō bhāvaśabdō nāma ? prativacanaṁ tu
<quote>yajati dadāti juhōtīti</quote> ।</p>
<p>nanu sa ēvāyamākhyātārthaḥ ta ēvāmī ākhyātaśabdā ityākṣēpaḥ । samā-
dhānaṁ tu, nākhyātārthamātraṁ yajati dadāti juhōtīti, kintarhi anyōtpāda-﻿<pb n="289"/>
katvamapi gamyatē na kēvalaṁ pūrvāparībhāvaḥ yathā bhavatīti ।
tadidamuktam <quote>yajyarthaścātō'vagamyatē bhāvayēditi ca</quote> । kimuktaṁ
bhavati ? pūrvāparībhāvaścātō'vagamyatē, anyōtpādakatvaṁ cēti । punaścā-
yamabhiprāyaḥ prakaṭīkr̥taḥ tathā yatēta, yathā yatkiṁñcidbhavatīti । tēnaitē
ākhyātaśabdā api bhāvaśabdā ityucyantē । atō dravyaguṇaśabdagrahaṇamapi﻿<pb n="290"/>
dravyaguṇapratyayōtpādakatvāt akriyārthatvaṁ, na nāmatvāta । <quote>kiṁ tāvatprāptaṁ ?
aviśēṣēṇēti</quote> kā'bhiprāyaḥ ? dravyaṁ vā bhavatu kriyārthaṁ; kriyā vā
bhavatu dravyārthā । sarvathā tāvadaparityaktakriyākārakasaṁbandha ēva kārya-
sambandha iti siddham । atrōcyatē । naivaṁ sidhyatīti । yadā hi dravyārthā
kriyā tadā kriyākārakasaṁbandhaḥ tyakta ēva bhavati । kasmāt ? dravyaṁ
hi tadā karmabhūtaṁ kriyāyām । na ca karma kārakaṁ kārakasthā hyatpattiḥ
karmēti vakṣyāmaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi karmaṇi kārakē dvitīyētyāgamaḥ । karturīpsita-﻿<pb n="291"/>
tamaṁ karmēti ca kārakādhikārē । yatra kiyāphalamabhinippadyatē tatkarmēti
sūtrārthaḥ । anyathā hīpsitatamagrahaṇamanarthakaṁ syāt । tasmāt karmaṇi dvitī-
yētyapi siddham । tasmāt kriyārthaṁ yadā''khyātaṁ bhavati tadaiva dravyaguṇayōḥ
kārakatvasiddhiḥ । ata āha-<quote>yē yē bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdāstēbhyaḥ kriyāpratīyēta
yajētētyēvamādibhyaḥ</quote> । kutaḥ ? iti praśnaḥ kimanyathā bhāvārthatvaṁ hīyēta ?﻿<pb n="292"/>
bāḍhaṁ hīyatē । pūrvāparībhāvē hi bhāvārthatvaṁ bhavati । sa pūrvāparībhāvaḥ
dravyaguṇayōstadarthatvē sati । anyathā hi gādōhanēna paśukāmasya
praṇayēditivat āśrayamātrāvagatiḥ syāt । na ca gōdōhanasādhyaṁ
praṇayanamavasīyatē । nanu ca gōdōhanēna praṇayēditi pūrvāparībhūtamēva
praṇayanaṁ pratīyatē gōdōhanaṁ ca karaṇamēva । satyaṁ pratīyatē । na tu
gōdōhanēna paśukāmasya praṇayēdityētadvākyārthatayā . tasmādaniyamapakṣē
na niyamēna kiyākāraka(saṁbandha)bhāvamajahatō vidhyarthatvaṁ vākyasya pratīyatē ।
ata idamuktaṁ bhāvārthatvādēvēti ।</p>﻿<pb n="293"/>
<p>ētaduktaṁ bhavati । ēvamēva saṁbandhāvagamāditi । tadidānīṁ pūrvāparī-
bhūtabhāvavyatirēkiṇamarthaṁ bhāvaśabdavācyaṁ prapañcayati <quote>ya āhuḥ kimapi
bhāvayēditi tē svargakāmapadasaṁbandhāta svargaṁ bhāvayēditi brūyuḥ</quote> iti ।
kimidaṁ svargakāmapadasaṁbandhāt svargaṁ bhāvayēditi । svargakāmaṁ bhāvayēditi
yuktaṁ vaktum । padārthasya hi padārthāntarēṇa saṁbandhaḥ svargakāmaścātra
padārthaḥ na svargaḥ, atō'sadēvēdaṁ pratibhāti । atrōcyatē ।
satyaṁ svargakāmaḥ padārthaḥ । sa ēva padārthāntarēṇa saṁbadhyatē ।﻿<pb n="294"/>
svargaparastvasau saṁbandhaḥ ityaidaṁparyamatra darśitaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa, dhātvarthasya karaṇa-
tvapradarśanārtham । vakṣyāti ca <quote>sthita ētasminnadhikaraṇē guṇavidhirnāma-
dhēyamiti vicārō bhaviṣyati</quote> iti । kathaṁ punaḥ svargaṁ bhāvayēdityēvaṁ paratā
vākyasya ? yathaivaṁparatā tathā'dhikāralakṣaṇē vakṣyāmaḥ । <quote>tasmāttēbhyaḥ
kriyāpratīyata</quote> iti nigamitaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa । kā punaratra kiyā ?﻿<pb n="295"/>
vidhyarthaḥ nanu ca phalasya karaṇaṁ kriyētyuktam । phalasya ca yāgaḥkaraṇaṁ
na vidhyarthaḥ ucyatē । yathā vidhyarthaḥ karaṇaṁ tathō'dhikāralakṣaṇē vakṣyāmaḥ ।
ihāpi ca bhāṣyakārēṇa <quote>tē ca yāgadānasaṁbaddhāḥ svargasyōtpattiṁ vadantī</quote>ti
vadatā vidhyarthasyaiva karaṇatōktā । tatsaṁbandhāddhi yāgādēḥ । <quote>kuta*</quote> iti praśnō-
'yam । kathaṁ punarniyōgārthasya karaṇatā'vagamyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । uttaravādī tu﻿<pb n="296"/>
<quote>ēṣahyarthō vidhīyatē tathā yāgādinā svargakāma</quote> ityādhikāralakṣaṇasiddhamarthaṁ
darśayati । <quote>kēna sādhayēt svarga yāgādinē</quote>ti । kimanēna granthēna pradarśitaṁ ?
saivādhikārikī yuktiḥ । svargaṁ sādhayatō'dhikāra iti sthāsyati । <quote>yasya ca
śabdasyārthēna phalaṁ sādhyatē tēnāpūrvaṁ kr̥tvā nānyathēti tatō'pūrvaṁ gamyata</quote> iti
pūrvāparavirōdhaparihārō'yam । pūrvaṁ hi niyōgāt phalamityuktam idānīṁ yāgā
tphalamiti । tēnāpūrvaṁ kr̥tvētyavirōdhaḥ । tatō'pūrvamēva phalasādhanamiti gamyatē ।﻿<pb n="297"/>
<quote>atō yastasya vācaka iti</quote> nigamanamētat । yasmādapūrvaṁ sādhayan
bhāvārthaḥ phalaṁ niṣpādayati nānyathā, kṣaṇikatvāt tēna tadviṣayō vidhyarthō
liṅādibhiḥ pratyāyyatē । tasya ca viṣayādhīnapratipattitvāt, bhāvārthānāṁ
ca viṣayabōdhakatvāt tatō'pūrvaṁ pratīyata ityucyatē, na punastasyāmī vācakā
iti । <quote>na tu kaścit sākṣādapūrvasya vācakō'sti</quote>iti bhāvārthābhiprāyamētat ।﻿<pb n="298"/>
na punarliṅādiśabdō'pi niyōgaṁ nācaṣṭē । kathaṁ punarbhāvārthē vācaka-
tvāśaṅkā ? kēvalasyāprayōgāt niyōgaśabdasya, tiṅantasyaiva prayōgāt;
tēna yāvatprayōgānuvartinyēva vācakatēti bhrāntānāmarthāvagamaṁ muktvā prayōgē-
yattā na sidhyatīti tannirākartumavācaka ityuktam ।</p>
<p>nanu ca na yuktam nirākartum kiṁ vā prayōgēyattā
anyathā siddhyati ? arthāvagamō vā vibhāgādavagamyamānaḥ kimapahnōtuṁ﻿<pb n="299"/>
śakyatē ? kiṁ tarhi prayōganiyamē kāraṇaṁ ? prayōga ēva । vācaka-
tvasyēva prayōgasyāpyanāditōktā । tasmātsūktaṁ na bhāvaśabdēna niyōgō'rthō-
'bhidhīyata iti । <quote>bhāvārthaiḥ kimapi bhāvayitavyaṁ</quote> ityavaibhaktika-
saṁbandhaṁ phalaniyōgabhāvārthānāṁ darśayati ।</p>
<p>atō nāyaṁ vainiyōgikaḥ saṁbandha iti siddham । anyathā﻿<pb n="300"/>
viniyōgābhāvādasambandhaṁ bādaririva vibhaktividhānānusārī manyatē ।
ataśca sthita ētasminnadhikaraṇē guṇavidhirnāmadhēyamiti vicārō bhaviṣyatīti
na śakyatē vaktum । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ na viniyōgalakṣaṇasaṁbandhō'yaṁ ?
viniyōjakānāṁ śrutyādīnāmabhāvāt । kathamabhāvaḥ ? saṁbandhasyānavagamāt ।
nanu cāyamasti saṁbandhaḥ yajēta svargakāma iti । bāḍhamasti na puna-
radaimarthyalakṣaṇaḥ । kiṁ lakṣaṇastarhi ? adhikāralakṣaṇaḥ । aida-
marthyaṁ ca viniyōgāvagamyamityuktaṁ śēṣaḥ parārthatvādityatra । tatra ca
śrutyādīni viniyōgē kāraṇānīti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b301"/>
<p>kathaṁ tarhi <quote>“karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt”</quote> iti ? na
dravyaguṇasaṁskārēṣvēva pārārthyaṁ phalayāgapuruṣēṣvapīti bādaripakṣaṁ nirasyatā
pārārthyalakṣaṇaḥ saṁbandhō'trāstītyabhyupagatam। satyamabhyupagataṁ na puna-
stacchabdēdaṁparatayā। tathāca darśitaṁ naṣṭāśvadagdharathavaditi <quote>“nanu ca
bhāvārthaiḥ kimapi bhāvayitavyaṁ svargakāmasya ca kēnāpi”</quote> iti guṇa-
pradhānabhāvaṁ darśayati। sa ca pārārthyē satīti punaraidaṁparyamēva prāpnōti।
nētyucyatē। bhāvasvabhāvō hyayamiti kathyatē nēdaṁparatāśabdasya। ata
ēva ca dravyaśabdēbhyaḥ tr̥tīyāyuktēbhyō'pi na vidhyarthatā'bhyupagatā।</p>
﻿e<pb n="b302"/>
tasmānna viniyōgādyāgasvargayōḥ saṁbandhaḥ। kathaṁ tarhi, bhāvārthatvā-
dēvētyuktam। ata ēva cākhyātaṁ na saṁbandhē smarati pāṇiniḥ।
nanu ca kartari karmaṇi bhāva iti smarati। satyaṁ smarati
na tēṣāmanyasaṁbandhitām। yathā prātipadikādavagatasyārthasya
saṁbandhapratipādinyō vibhaktayaḥ na tathā'' khyātāttasyārthasya। nanu ca
tr̥tīyādibhiḥ dviṣṭhatvātsaṁbandhasya dvayōrapi sambandhitā uktā bhavatīti।
satyaṁ dviṣṭhaḥ saṁbandhaḥ। sambandhitā punarnāmārthasyaiva tr̥tīyādibhiḥ।
yathā pumān sadvitīyō dvivacanasyaukārāntasya na punardvitīyōpyarthaḥ।

﻿<pb n="b303"/>
ata ēva cākhyātārthē kartr̥karmagatā saṅkhayaivōcyatē vacanaiḥ na
punaḥ kartrādayaḥ, pramāṇāntarāvagamyā hi tē niyōgataḥ pratyakṣādi-
bhirvā। ata ēva tu niyōgaḥ kāryēpyarthē na bhaviṣyantamartha---
mavagamayati। kārakavyāpārō hi kālatrayāvacchēdyō nādhikāraḥ। kathaṁ
tarhi prayājādērviniyōjyatvaṁ ? nākhyātātpārārthyamavasīyata ityuktam।

﻿<pb n="b304"/>
<quote>“kimētāvantyēva pramāṇāni ityatra parihāraṁ vakṣyāmaḥ। <quote>“naivaṁ dravyaguṇa-
śabdā”</quote> iti। kiṁ naivaṁ ?”</quote> naivamadhikāralakṣaṇasambandhamarhantītyarthaḥ।
sarvathā hi viniyōgapramāṇaviṣayā ēvaitē। ataḥ siddhaṁ bhāvārthatvādēva
viniyōgasaṁbandhitāṁ pratipadyata iti।
kathaṁ tarhi svargakāma iti। viṣayamaṅgīkr̥tyaitaduktam na punarvi-
niyōjyatām। yathā caitadēvaṁ tathā svargakāmāghikaraṇē nipuṇatara---
﻿<pb n="b305"/>
mupapādayiṣyāmaḥ। <quote>“bhavanti kēcitkarmaśabdā na bhāvārthāḥ yathā śyēnaikātri-
kādayaḥ kēcit bhāvārthā na karmaśabdāḥ yathā bhāvō bhavanaṁ bhūtiriti”</quote>
bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti padadvayābhidhānē bhāvārthasya kiṁ prayōjanam ? yadi
karmaśabdēbhyaḥ kriyētyucyatē śyēnaikatrikādibhyō'pyapūrvasyōtpattirityuktaṁ
syāt। ētē'pi hi karmaśabdāḥ। ētēbhyō'pi kimiti na bhavati ? dravya-
guṇaśabdanivr̥ttyarthaṁ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā ityuktam। na karmaśabda-
nivr̥ttyartham। tasmādabhidhīyamānē viśēṣaṇē naiva śyēnādīnāṁ
nivr̥ttiḥ। ētē'pi bhāvārthasyaiva karmaṇō vācakā yāgādēḥ।
﻿<pb n="b306"/>
idamaparaṁ kharparaṁ <q><quote>“sthita ētasminnadhikaraṇē nāmadhēyaṁ”</quote></q> na punarasyāṁ
cintāyāṁ karmavacanatvaṁ śyēnādērupapadyatē। yadā''khyātārthēna vidhiḥ sādhyata
iti sthitaṁ tadā lakṣaṇābhayannāmadhēyatvābhityuktam। ataḥ śyēnādini-
vr̥ttyarthamabhidhānadvayaṁ śakyam। atrābhidhīyatē। nēdaṁ śakyaṁ yadi karma-
śabdēbhya ityucyatē idamēvādhikaraṇaṁ sthitiṁ na labhatē। sthāpyamānaṁ hyētajjyō-
tiṣṭōmādēḥ karmaśabdatāmāvahati। ataśca na nāmākhyātayōḥ viśēṣō labhyatē।
﻿<pb n="b307"/>
bhāvaśabdābhidhānē punaḥ siddhavatkarmābhidhānāt jyōtiṣṭōmādērnivr̥ttiḥ।
sakarmakē pūrvāparībhūtē bhāvaśabdō vartata iti।</p>
<p>ēvaṁ tarhi bhāvaśabdā ityēvāstu karmaśabdnagrahaṇamatiricyatē। ida-
mēva hi na labhyatē pūrvāparībhūtē sakarmakē bhāvaśabdō vartata iti।
anyatrāpi darśanāt bhāvō bhavanaṁ bhūtiriti bhāvaśabdasya। kiṁ punarudāharaṇaṁ ?
﻿<pb n="b308"/>
<p>yadi śyēnaikātrikādayō'pi karmaśabdā naivaṁ dravyaguṇaśabdānāṁ nivr̥ttyartha-
midaṁ sūtramupapadyatē। sarvatrādhikāracōdanāsu nāmaivōpapadamupalabhyatē।
tasmānnirviṣayaṁ sūtraṁ manvānaḥ kiṁ punarihōdāharaṇamiti pr̥cchati।</p>
﻿<pb n="r309"/>
kā vārtā ētasyaiva rēvatīṣvityēvamādiṣu ?। yathākhyātādr̥tē nānyasya
vidhyarthatā saṁbhavati tathā tatraiva vakṣyāmaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi nāmōpapadānyē-
vātrōdāharaṇāni ? । anēnaiva sūtraiṇa nāmākhyātayōḥ vidhyarthatvē
vivēkaḥ । avivēkē hi nāmataiva na syāta dravyaguṇaśabdataiva
syāt । tasmātsiddhaṁ dravyaguṇanivr̥ttyarthamudāharaṇam । ākhyā-
tikyō vibhaktayaḥ pūrvāparībhāvaṁ pratipādayantītyupariṣṭādvakṣyati ।
visadr̥śavibhaktiyōgācca jyōtiṣṭōmādēḥ na pūrvāparībhūtapratipādana---﻿<pb n="b310"/>
<q>nasāmarthyamastīti</q> na nāmadhēyānāṁ vidhyarthatā। kintu ākhyātānāmēvēti
<q>siddhō vivēkaḥ</q>। <q>atra kēciccōdayanti</q>। <q>nanu karmaśabdamātrāt mābhūdapūrvōtpattirityupa-
padyata ēvaitatsūtram</q>। <q>ēnañca kimihōdāharaṇamityēvamādēgrēnthasyābhiprāyavarṇanamanarthakama</q>।
asyārthaḥ। yadi tāvat dravyaguṇaśabdā adhikāracōdanāsu bhavanti tadā labdhamudāharaṇa-
miti nōdāharaṇābhāvābhiprāyēṇōdāharaṇapraśnōṣapattiḥ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b311"/>
<p>kathaṁ tarhi śyēnaikatrikādayō nirasyantē ? anākhyātārthatvādēva।
bhāvārthagrahaṇaṁ kimartham ? karmaśabdatvē'pi abhāvārthatvēna anākhyātārtha-
taivēti। tasmātsūktamētat kimihōdāharaṇamityēvamādērgrantha-
syōpanyāsaḥ।</p>
<p><q>sarvēṣāṁ bhāvō'rtha iti cēt</q>। kimanēna pūrvōktamākṣiptam ?
yatpūrvōktaṁ tadēvākṣiptam। bhāvārthēbhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata iti। sarvēṣāṁ bhāvō'rtha
﻿<pb n="b312"/>
iti vadatā kathamidamākṣiptaṁ bhavati ? yadi hyabhāvārthānāmapūrvārthatāṁ vadēt
tadā''kṣēpaḥ saṁbhavati। sarvēṣāṁ bhāvō'rtha iti vadatō naiva dravyaguṇa-
śabdāḥ santītyabhiprāyō gamyatē। na punardravyaguṇaśabdāḥ api
bhāvārthā iti śakyatē pratipat‍tum। karmaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyācca
viśēṣataḥ। ayamabhiprāyaścōdakasya। dravyaguṇaśabdā api bhāva-
rūpāpannā ēva vidhyarthā bhavanti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b313"/>
taccēdaṁ dadhnā juhātītyatra pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ। ēvañcēt sarvēṣāṁ bhāvō'rthaḥ dravya-
guṇāvagatistu nāntarīyakyēva। tasmādabhidhānavanna svarūpataḥ kriyānvayō
dravyaguṇānām। tasmādbhāvārthā iti sūtraṁ na viśēṣāvagatāvalam।</p>
<p><q>yēṣāmutpattau</q>। satyaṁ sarvēṣāṁ bhāvārthatā, kintvēkasya svataḥ
anyasya tadyōgāt। kimidaṁ tadyōgāditi ? tadarthānupravēśādityarthaḥ।</p>

﻿<pb n="b314"/>
kathaṁ punaridamavagamyatē---ēkasya svataḥ, anyasya tadyōgādanupravēśāditi ?
tatsvabhāvāt, ēkasya hi siddha ēva svabhāvaḥ, anyasya sādhyaḥ tatra na
sādhyatāmanyatō'pēkṣatē। siddhiḥ punaḥ na sādhyayōgāddatē sādhyatayā pratipat‍tuṁ
śakyatē। kiṁ jahatsvabhāvā sādhyānvayitā siddhasya ? bhavatu, kō dōṣaḥ ?
ayamēva dōṣaḥ siddhataiva nāvagamyatē। ananvitānāñcāyaṁ vivēkaḥ sūtrakārēṇa
pradarśitaḥ। tasmānnamaḥ śabdavidbhayō yairayaṁ vivēkō niścīyatē।</p>
﻿<pb n="b315"/>
yathāhācāryavān। kintu nimittagataiṣā kathā। nimittataśca kāryama-
kāryaṁvēti parīkṣakaiḥ vaktavyam। tathā cēyaṁ yēṣāmutpattāviti bhagavatā
sūtrakārēṇa nimittāvasthōpavarṇitā utpattiśabdaṁ prayuñjānēna। yēṣāmutpattau
nimittāvasthāyāmityarthaḥ। nimittatō hyakāṅkṣā cākhyātārthasyaivēti darśitam।﻿<pb n="b316"/>
kāryē punaḥ kiṁ siddhasādhyavivēkō nāsti ? asti tāvat
<q>āśritatvātprayōgasyēti</q>। kimidamāśritatvātprayōgarayēti ? ucyatē।
bhāvārthānāmēva prayōgaḥ puruṣēṇāśrita iti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b317"/>
<p>kimidaṁ bhāvārthānāmēva prayōgaḥ puruṣēṇāśrita iti ? yāvatā
dravyaguṇānāmapi kimiti nāśrita iti ? nimittāśritattvātkāryasya,
yathānimittamavabhāsatē। tadidaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa <note n="1">p. 316</note>kiñcētyuk‍tvā kāryā-
dapyēvaṁbhūtanimittataivēti pratipāditam, sākṣēpanirapēkṣatvātkāryāvagataḥ﻿<pb n="b318"/>
kva sāpēkṣatvaṁ kva vā nirapēkṣatvamuktam ? siddhasādhyayōḥ sādhyasyānapēkṣatvaṁ
vidhyarthē sādhyaviṣayatvāt niyōgasya। sādhyāpēkṣitā ca siddharayēti
guṇavidhau darśayiṣyāma ityuktam। ēṣa vinigamanāyāṁ hētuḥ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b319"/>
<q>cōdanā। kathaṁ punaridamavagamyatē asti tadapūrvamiti</q> ?
nanu cāyaṁ praśnō nōpapadyatē, apūrva hi vidhyarthaḥ। vidhitaśca prāmāṇya-
mityuktam। kathaṁ tadākṣēpa upapadyatē। atrōcyatē। ayamabhi-
prāyaścōdakasya। niyōgō hi karmaṇi puruṣaṁ niyuṅktē na svārthē।</p>
﻿<pb n="b320"/>
karma cānityam। na ca svargādyanantaramupalabhyatē। tasmādyāgasya varaṁ
nityatvaṁ kalpayitavyam। ātmanō vā saṁskāraḥ kaścita, dēvatāprasādō vā
na punastēnāpūrvaṁ kr̥tvētyētatsuktamiva pratibhāti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b321"/>
atrābhidhīyatē---niyōgaḥ karmāṇi puruṣaṁ niyuṅkta iti
na samyagavadhr̥taṁ bhavatā। ārambhē hi puruṣaṁ niyuṅktē na
karmaṇi। ārambhaviṣayaṁ hi karma। sa cārambhō vidhyarthaḥ।
﻿<pb n="b322"/>
svargakāmasya cāsāvityārambhāt svarga iti। brūmaḥ। karmaṇāñcā---
rambhaḥ। karmādinityatvaparikalpanā punaḥ pramāṇāntaraviruddhaiva;
animittā ca ārambhē pratyārthini। kathaṁ punaḥ pramāṇāntaravirōdhaḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b323"/>
bhaṅgitvaṁ hi karmaṇāṁ prasiddhamēva। kṣaṇāntarānupalambhācca। ātmanaśca
niṣkriyatvaṁ sarvagatatvādātmanaḥ। purōḍāśādēśca karmavadvināśadarśanāt।
saukṣmyādēśca viśēṣasya ārambhē pratyarthini nāsti kalpanētyuktam।
darśitaṁ tadbhāṣyakārēṇa sāmānyakalpanāyāṁ pramāṇaṁ na viśēṣakalpanā---
yāmiti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b324"/>
<p><q>tāni dvaidham। avagatamētadbhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇō bācakā iti</q>।
kva punaridamavagatam ? bhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇō vācakā iti
bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā ityētatsamadhigatam। karmaṇaḥ pūrvāparībhūtasya
﻿<pb n="b325"/>
vācakā iti। na punaḥ prādhānyaṁ kacinnirdiṣṭam। athāyamabhiprāyaḥ
itarattadarthamiti vadatā nāmarthaṁ pratyākhyātārthasya prādhānyamuktamiti।
tadayuktam। svargakāmapadārthaṁ prati guṇabhāvadarśanāt। tathōcōktam
---tē svargakāmapadasaṁbandhāt svargaṁ bhāvayēditi brūyuriti। tasmānna vidmaḥ
kimidaṁ <quote>‘avagatamētadbhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇō vācakā’</quote> iti। atrā-
bhidhīyatē---prādhānyaṁ hi niyōgaviṣayatvamabhiprētam। kutaḥ ? viṣayatvādēva।
﻿<pb n="b326"/>
viṣayatayā hi yāgādayaḥ pratīyantē niyōgārthasya। na kasyaci-
dutpattyādyarthatayā। taduktaṁ <quote>“adhikāralakṣaṇē vakṣyāmaḥ”</quote> iti।
tasmāda‍yuktamuktamētadavagatamiti। cintā cōpapadyatē---kiṁ sarvāṇyēva
niyōgaviṣayatayā pratīyantē ? utōtpattyādyarthatayāpi kēciditi।
﻿<pb n="b327"/>
yuktaṁ tāvata kēṣāñcidutpattyādyarthatā kalpayitum yadyaivaṁbhūtānāmapi
niyōgasaṁsparśitēpapadyatē; na tu tadadyāpi nirṇīyatē। atha tu
nirṇayahēturasti tatō na sarvasyāpūrvārthatā nyāyyā। <quote>“ēvamalpīyasya-
dr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā nyāyyā”</quote> iti bhāṣyam। tatpunarasaṅgatārtha-
miti pratibhāti। niyōgārthatvēpi hi naivādr̥ṣṭakalpanā। ucyatē।
﻿<pb n="b328"/>
parihr̥tamētat ēvamalpōyasyadr̥ṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanētyatra। nanu yuktaṁ
tatra pramāṇāntaradr̥ṣṭakriyāniṣpattiparityāgēna nāmārthānāṁ śabdatō niyōgasya
niṣpādakatvam। ēvamapyupapadyamānē na yuktamiti। atrāpi tulyaṁ kriyāntara-
sādhanōtpādyarthatayā sambhavati śabdē na niyōgasādhanatā yuktā। nanu ca
niyōgaśūnyānāṁ niyōgaviṣayasādhanōtpattyādyarthataiva nāvasīyatē। na cāvihi-
tamaṅgaṁ bhavatīti vakṣyati। satyaṁ niyōgādr̥tē nāṅgatā। astyēvātra niyōgaḥ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b329"/>
na ca niyōgārthatēti tr̥tīyē vakṣyāmaḥ। kē punarastē bhāvārthāḥ ?
ya ēva lōkē cikīrṣitōtpattyādyarthatayā prasiddhā darśitā bhāṣyakārēṇa।
prayōjanamapyuktam।</p>
<p><q>dharmamātrē tu karma syādanirvr̥ttēḥ prayājavat</q>। uktamajahātkriyā-
kārakasambandha ēva niyōgasambandhaḥ। kārakāṇāṁ bhāvārthānāñca
cikīrṣitārthānām। ihēdānīṁ yatra dr̥ṣṭaḥ saṁskārō nōpa-
labhyatē cikīrṣitapratipādikā ca vibhaktirasti tatrāpi kimajahatkriyā-
﻿<pb n="b330"/>
kārakasambandhaiva niyōgārthatā, uta yāgādēriva niyōgaviṣayataiva dhātvartha-
syēti। kiṁ punaratra yuktam ? dr̥ṣṭasyābhāvānniyōgasiddhirēvāvaśiṣyatē।
tasmāt prayājādivanniyōgārthataiva sammārgādēḥ।</p>
<p>nanu ca cikīrṣitārthapratipādikā dvitīyāvibhaktiravivakṣitā bhavati।
na cēyamaikāntikī। balbajān śikhaṇḍakān kurvityēvamādiṣu vyabhicārāt।
﻿<pb n="b331"/>
vēdē'pi sak‍tūn juhōtīti। tasmāt karaṇārthēpi asyāḥ prayōgō
dr̥ṣṭaḥ। tulyaśrutitvāccētaraiḥ sarvadharmaḥ syāt। ucyatē। yattāvallōkē
vyabhicāradarśanamupanyastam---tadayuktam। lōkē hi vivakṣātaḥ kārakāṇi
bhavanti। vivakṣā ca puruṣavaśānuvartinīṁ। ataḥ cikīrṣitavibhaktidarśa-
nāt tathaiva vivakṣēti yuktaṁ prativak‍tum। vēdē tu katham ? uktamasmābhiḥ
﻿<pb n="b332">
kāryarthatayā prāmāṇyam। iha cikīrṣitārthāparityāgēna niyōga-
saṁsparśitā na śakyatē vak‍tum। kriyāntarasādhanatvēnāśravaṇāt
sak‍tūnām। na ca saktavō niyōgauk‍yēnētikartavyatābhāvaṁ pratipat‍tuṁ
kṣamāḥ। kimiti niyōgauk‍yaṁ na bhavati। abhāvārthatvāt sak‍tūnām।
﻿<pb n="b333">
kāryārthasya hi karaṇāṁśōpanipātitā, kimityaṁśōpanipātitā vā।
atō nānubandhabhāvaḥ। bhinnānubandhānāñca kimityaṁśabhāva ēvaik‍yam।
bhidyatē cātra kimityaṁśabhāvaḥ। atō naik‍yaṁ vidhēḥ। anēkatvācca nēti---
kartavyatā saktavaḥ। tasmādalaukikō'yaṁ cikīrṣitārthasaṁyōgaḥ, cikīrṣita-
tvēna sak‍tūnāmanavagamāt। na caitāvatā vyabhicāritā śak‍yatē vak‍tuṁ
﻿<pb n="b334">
dvitīyāyāḥ। yāvaddarśanabhāvī hi chāndasaḥ prayōgaḥ। tathā ca vyākhyā-
tārō dr̥ṣṭānuvidhiśchandasītyupadiśanti। ata ēva ca bhagavatā sūtrakārēṇa
tr̥tīyā ca hōśchandasi iti tr̥tīyārthē chandasi dvitīyā dr̥ṣṭētyuktam।
﻿<pb n="b335">
ata ēvōpapadavibhaktitulyaiṣā। tasmādajahatsvārthavr̥ttitvānniyōgārthasya
cikīrṣitārthaivēyaṁ <quote>“grahaṁ sammārṣṭi”</quote> <quote>“vrīhīn prōkṣatī”</quote>ti dvitīyā।
nanu ca dr̥ṣṭō'rthō nāstītyuktam। niyōgārthasya sādhyatvaṁ na cikīrṣi-
﻿<pb n="b336">
tārthēṣu sambhavatītyapyuktam। na cānyat pramāṇamasti yēna kāryakalpanā
syāt। cikīrṣitārthābhidhānāt। niyōgārthasaṁraparśitvācca siddhamadr̥ṣṭa-
kāryatvaṁ lōkavat kāryāntarasaṁyōgāt। lōkē'pi kāryāntarayōgitvāt
ha/?/styādīnāṁ siddhaṁ nīrājanādēradr̥ṣṭārthatvaṁ prayōjanam। varuṇapradhāsēṣu śrūyatē
---śamīmayyaḥ srucō bhavanti hiraṇmayyō vēti। prakr̥tau nānāvr̥kṣīya-
﻿<pb n="b337"/>
sruk‍sammārgavyaḍagyamapūrvamiti nānāvr̥kṣīyāḥ sruva utpādayitavyāḥ
sammārgārthēna yathā pūrvapakṣaḥ। yathā tarhi siddhāntaḥ śamīmayya ēva
hiraṇmayyō vā sammārjayitavyāḥ। tathā paridhyādiṣu।</p>
<p>nanu ca pūrvapakṣē'pyaṅgapradhānārthamētadvidhānaṁ bhaviṣyati barhirvat।
naivam। yatra hyaṅgapradhānārtha ēvōpadēśavidhiḥ kāryavidhirapi tathaiva tatra।
﻿<pb n="b338"/>
yatra punarupadēśē vidhibhēdaḥ kāryavidhirapi tatra prakaraṇāt pradhānasyaiva
darśitam---<quote>‘ānarthakyāttadaṅgēṣu’</quote> iti। yatra hi pradhānasya tatkāryaṁ
na bhavati tatrānarthakyāttadaṅgānām। yatra punaḥ sambhavati tatra
﻿<pb n="b339"/>
pradhānārtha ēva iti prakr̥tatvādityuktam। yathā sahasradakṣiṇādayaḥ pradhānada-
kṣiṇāsu। nōdāharaṇamādaraṇīyaṁ madhvaśanādiṣu darśanāt।</p>
﻿<pb n="b340"/>
<p><q>stutaśastrayōḥ</q>।। atrāpi sa ēva saṁśayaḥ। kintu stuta-
śastrayōḥ cikīrṣitārthatvamuta vidhiviṣayataivēti। nanu cikīrṣitārthatvē stutya-
rthō'pi hīyatē stauti śaṁsatīti ca tadarthābhidhānam। tasmāt nātra saṁśayaṁ
﻿<pb n="b341"/>
paśyāmaḥ। ajahatsvārthē tr̥ṣṇayā hi cikīrṣitārthatvaṁ gr̥hyatē। viparī-
tañca tadatra। athāyamabhiprāyaḥ paśupurōḍāśavat; yāgasya satō
dēvatārthatvam। dēvatārthatvē ca cīkīrṣitārthatvam। na ca yajyarthō-
'pauti। tasmādatrāpi stutērēva dēvatāsmaraṇaṁ yajēriva prayōjanaṁ bhaviṣya-
tīti। viṣama upanyāsaḥ। tatra hi dēvatāsādhanakō yāgaḥ।
atō'jahatsvārthavr̥ttitvaṁ yujyatē yajēḥ। na dēvatāsaṁskāratvē kaścidvirōdhaḥ।
iha punaḥ stutiḥ stutyamapēkṣatē na dēvatām। ēvañca dēvatārthatvē
hīyēta stutyarthaḥ। nanu stutibhājō'pi dēvā iti dēvatāvidaḥ
﻿<pb n="b342"/>
dēvatā cētsāmyaṁ paśupurōḍāśēna। maivaṁ vōcaḥ। ghōṭārūḍhasya vismr̥tō
ghōṭa iti। stutibhājaśca dēvatā iti bravīṣi। havirbhājaśca saṁskāraṁ
manyasē। purōḍāśē tvavibhāgād‍yuktam। tasmānnātra pūrvapakṣaṁ paśyāmaḥ। aya-
﻿<pb n="b343"/>
mēvātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ। stautiḥ stutyārthēti, na cācikīrṣitaḥ stutyaḥ।
yāgasambandhitvēnābhidhēyābhēdāt। na punaḥ purōḍāśavaddēvatābhēdā-
diti brūmaḥ। tatra dēvatāpratyabhijñānamēvābhiprētam। tacca tatraiva
pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ। atra tvabhidhānābhēdamātrēṇaivājahatsvārthavr̥ttimupapadyata
iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē।</p>﻿<pb n="b344"/>
<p>itarastu cōdayati yadyēvaṁ māhēndrasya grahr̥yajēḥ sannidhau
aindrīstutistatraikābhidhānābhāvāt na cikīrṣitārthā syāt। utkarṣō
vā kalpanīyaḥ। ucyatē। nōtkarṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ। indra ēva
hi mahēndraḥ abhinnārthābhidhānaṁ hi sāmānādhikaraṇyamucyatē।</p>
<p>nanu ca nīlōtpalamiti bhinnārthāvagatēḥ kathamabhinnārthābhidhānam;
bhinnārthābhidhānē vā kathaṁ sāmānādhikaraṇyam ? utpalagata-
﻿<pb n="b345"/>
guṇābhidhānāditi brūmaḥ। āgatō'si tarhi madīyaṁ panthānam।
tatra prayuktaḥ tada‍‍guṇābhidhānasamarthō bhavati। yatra ca śabdaḥ
prayujyatē tamācaṣṭē। ata ēva ca guṇamabhidhāya guṇini pravartantē
yē guṇaśabdāsta iha gr̥hyantē guṇavacanatayēti samāsapratiṣēdha
uktaḥ। tasmātsiddhamēkābhidhānam। guṇāvagatirhi sāmānādhikaraṇyē
﻿<pb n="b346"/>
vājinasthānīyā। ataścikīrṣitārthatvaṁ stutēraindryāḥ। tadidamayuktam।
nirastō'yamarthaḥ ananvitō'pyavasīyata iti। kāryē tu kadācidanvēti
kadācinnēti। avagatau punaḥ na taṭasthaṁ padārthāvabōdhanamityuk‍tam।</p>
﻿<pb n="b347"/>
mābhūttadarthāvagatau। kāryē punaruttarapadārthapradhānatvāt samāsasya indra ēva
kāryabhāk anyathā hyanupapannaiva śabdavidāṁ vāgiyaṁ <quote>“uttarapadārthapradhānō'yaṁ
samāsaḥ ayaṁ pūrvapadārthapradhāna”</quote> iti। kiñcijjñō dēvānāṁ priyaḥ। samāsō
hi nāma parasparānugamapūrvakaṁ padārthāntarānugamanam, tatrāpi kadācit
﻿<pb n="b348"/>
pūrvaṁ padaṁ uttaramanvēti। kadāciduttaraṁ pūrvam। kimidamanvētīti ?
idamidaṁ idamāśrityāyaṁ padārthō'rthāntarānvayībhavatīti। tataḥ kim ?
idaṁ tatō bhavati। nānabhidhānataiva sthāsyati saguṇasyānvayāt।
atha mataṁ arthāntarasaṁbandhaḥ punaḥ arthāntarēṇa saṁbadhyata iti।﻿<pb n="b349"/>
uk‍taṁ parasparānvayē samāsaḥ। tatō'rthāntarānvayaḥ। tasmānnārthāntarākṣēpasya
samāsaḥ। na ca samastasya kēvalasyārthāntarasaṁbandhaḥ। ataḥ saguṇadēvatā
na kēvalēnābhadhātuṁ śak‍yatē। bhavati vai pradhānasya sāpēkṣasyāpi samāsa iti
samāsavidāṁ giraḥ śrūyantē। pradhānaṁ cēndrārthaḥ। atō dravyasaṁbandhasyāpi
﻿<pb n="b350"/>
mahatvamupapadyatē। na samyagavadhr̥taṁ bhavatā samāsavidvacaḥ। padārthā---
ntarasaṁbandhapradhānasya samastasyāpi samāsō niruṇaddhīti tasyārthaḥ, na punaḥ
samāsapadanirapēkṣasyārthāntarasaṁbandha iti। nanu cāsamarthasamāsā api
vyākhyātr̥bhiruditāḥ। satyaṁ, uditō yatra tatraiva tē bhavantu। atra
punaḥ samarthaḥ padavidhirityētadēva nyāyyam। asāmarthyādarśanāt।
﻿<pb n="b351"/>
nana cēdamēvāsāmarthyam māhēndrō grahayajiḥ aindrī stutiriti। ēvaṁ cāja-
hatsvārthatōpapannā। ēvamitarētarāśrayaṁ prāpnōti। cikīrṣitārthatvē mahē-
ndrasya asāmarthyaṁ, asāmarthyē cikīrṣitārthatvamiti। itarētarāśrayāṇi
﻿<pb n="b352"/>
na prakalpyanta ityuktam। yadyēvamasamarthasamāsō'pi na prāpnōti।
prādhānyē bhāvārthasya sāmarthyaṁ sāmarthyē ca prādhānyamiti। maivaṁ vōcaḥ
abhidhānataḥ sāmarthyāvagatēḥ tasmāt saguṇaiva dēvatā। avaśyaṁ
caitadēvamavagantavyam। anyathā guṇavacanamasaṁsparśi syāt। na
ca saṁbhavantyāṁ gatau tad‍yuktam। tasmādutkarṣa ēva prāpnōti।
bhavatu tarhi utkarṣaḥ। naitāvatā cikīrṣitārthatvaṁ tyak‍tuṁ śak‍yatē।
﻿<pb n="b353"/>
atantrē hi kramasannidhī vipakṣabhūtē sāmarthyē। nanu cōtkarṣē sati bahūnāṁ
mantrāṇāṁ niṣprayōjanatā prāpnōti maṇḍūkasūktādīnām। na niṣprayōjanatā,
yasya yatrārthaḥ sa tatra yātīti darśitaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa। kathaṁ punarvācastēmē
āśvinē ca sāmarthya bhinnārthānāṁ ? vacanādēkārthatā bhaviṣyati aindrīvat।
api vā śrutisaṁyōgāt। api ca na stautiśaṁsatī cikīrṣitārthau bhavataḥ।
﻿<pb n="b354"/>
kasmāt ? dēvatāpratyabhijñānābhāvāt। nanu cābhidhānataḥ pratyabhi-
jñānamuditam। tadayuktam yatra hi pramāṇāntarēṇa pratyabhijñānamasti
tadēvēdamiti tatrābhidhānaṁ na bhēdārthaṁ bhavitumarhati tathā ca darśitaṁ
---<q>vaśāyāmarthasamavāyāditi</q>। yatra punaḥ abhidhānādēva pratyabhi-
jñānaṁ tatra yāgānvayī stutyanvayīti na śakyatē pratipat‍tum।
﻿<pb n="b355"/>
na cānanviyinō'bhidhānamastīti tatra tatrōk‍tam। tasmānna cikīrṣitā-
rthatvaṁ stautēḥ śaṁsatēśca। atō niyōgaviṣayataivāvasīyatē। ata ēvāmī
śrutisaṁyōgā darśitā bhāṣyakārēṇa stutēḥ prādhānyāvagamahētavaḥ। kathaṁ punaḥ
prādhānyāvagamahētavaḥ saptamīsaṁyōgō hi abhidhānē'pi tulyaḥ। na, abhi-
dhānasya parārthatvāt। abhidhēyabhāvasthaṁ hyabhidhānaṁ stutau punaḥ stutyārtham।
﻿<pb n="b356"/>
tacca stutyaṁ kavatīṣvēva nānyatra pramāṇāntarānavagamāt। ataḥ kavatīṣu
stuvata iti yuktam। na cātra puruṣavaśāt vivakṣātaḥ kārakā-
bhidhānaṁ śakyatē vak‍tum। kathaṁ tarhi ? abhidhānata ēva। taccā-
bhidhānaṁ kavatīsthamityuktam। tathā dvitīyāśrutisaṁyōgaḥ prādhānya-
mutsargāt gamayati। anyatō hi guṇabhāvō vaktavyaḥ।
tathā indrasya nu vīryāṇīti nābhidhānē paryavasānamiti kathayati।
﻿<pb n="b357"/>
prathamā punarliḍādyabhihitē hi padārtha upapadyatē। ēvamajahatsvārthatā ca stutēḥ
prāpnōti stutyābhidhānāditi pradarśitam। <q>śabdapr̥thak‍tvāditi</q> śāstra-
pr̥thak‍tvaṁ ca darśayati। tasya viṣayabhūtē bhāvārtha upapadyatē na tu guṇabhūtē,
niyōgaśūnyatvāditi pradarśitam। niyōgaśūnyatvaṁ ca tr̥tīyē vakṣyāma
﻿<pb n="b358"/>
ityapyuktam। kiñcāgniṣ‍ṭuti āgnēyīvidhānāt pradhānārthataiva gamyatē।
guṇapakṣē hi kāryata ēva prāpnōti। <q>anyaścārthaḥ pratīyata iti</q>।
anēnāpi śāstrabhēda ēva kathyatē। iyāṁstu viśēṣaḥ pūrvatra svataḥ।
iha tu saṁbandhōpādhikaḥ। <quote>“pradhānakarmavadabhidhānaṁ”</quote> iti pradhānasyaivōcitaṁ
﻿<pb n="b359"/>
nāmēti kathayati। kutaḥ ? bhēdāvagamāt। guṇakarmaṇāṁ bhēdō nāstīti
sōmaṁ kīṇātītyatra darśayiṣyāmaḥ। bhēdānupāti ca nāma। tasmādanucitaṁ
guṇakarmaṇāṁ bhinnaṁ nāma। phalanirvr̥ttiṁ ca karmaṇaḥ sakāśāddarśayati
na cikīrṣitāt dēvatātaḥ। tasmādacikīrṣitārthatvaṁ siddham। prayōjanaṁ
tvanyatrētyuk‍taṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa।</p>
﻿<pb n="b360"/>
<p><q>vidhimantrayōraikārthyamaikaśabdyāt। kiṁ yadvad‍brāhmaṇē bhāva-
śabdō vidhāyakaḥ tadvanmantrēṣvapi, uta tanmantrē'vidhāyaka iti</q>।
kimidamupanyastam ? nanu na śrutaṁ bhavatā yadupanyastam। satyaṁ śrutaṁ
kintu asambaddhamiva pratibhāti। kathamasambaddham ? viniyuktō hi
mantra iti sthitam। prayōgasamavāyī ca mantraḥ smaraṇēnōpayujyata iti
sthitam। ataḥ kā'tra vidhāyakāśaṅkā ? atha manyasē niyōga-
﻿<pb n="b361"/>
śravaṇāt bhavatyāśaṅkēti tadapi nirākr̥taṁ <quote>‘ya ēvaṁ vidvān paurṇamāsīṁ yajata’</quote>
ityēkārthatāvagamāt। ēvaṁ tarhi ēkārthatayaiva vidhāyakatāśaṅkā brāhmaṇaprati-
pāditamarthaṁ mantrō'bhidhatta iti। atō'bhinnārthatvāt abhinnāthasya vidhāna---
mābhidhānaṁ ca na sambhavatīti pūrvapakṣaḥ। arthataścaikatvaṁ nānātvaṁ na śabdā-
nām। nanu caivamabhidhāyakatvaṁ hīyatē mantrāṇāṁ samidādīnāmiva parasparam।
﻿<pb n="b362"/>
ucyatē---naitat। tannimittatvādvidhēḥ। nimittaṁ hi vidhirna bādhata iti
nyāyavidbhiruk‍tam। ataḥ siddhamaviśēṣāt dvayōrvidhāyakatvam।</p>
<p><q>api vā prayōgasāmarthyāt</q>। ucyatē। abhidhāyakatayā hyēkārtha-
tvaṁ mantrasya pratipannam। kasyābhidhāyakatayā ? vihitasya। na ca
vihitābhidhānē vidhānaṁ śakyatē। vidhānē hi karmāntarāpattiḥ।
﻿<pb n="b363"/>
karmāntaratvē vā anabhidhāyakatvaṁ samidādīnāmiva parasparam। tataśca
viniyōgaśrutēḥ bādhaḥ। bhavatviti cēt na, abhidhāyakatayā hi niyōga-
saṁsparśasiddhēḥ। tasmānna niyōgāntaramarhati। <q>stutyarthatāyāmapyanarthakya-
miti। kēyamakāṇḍē stutyarthatāśaṅkā</q>। ucyatē---stutāvapi vihitābhidhānaṁ﻿<pb n="b364"/>
dr̥ṣṭam। tataḥ kim ? ēkavākyatāyāmēvaitadupapannaṁ, vihitābhidhānaṁ nāma
na vākyabhēdē, abhinnaṁ ca vidhivākyānmantravākyam। tasmādābhidhāyakatva-
mupapādayituṁ duśśakam। nanu ca viniyōgēna vihitābhidhāyakatvam।
ucyatē---aidamarthyē hi prabhaviṣṇutā viniyōgasya nēdaṁ kāryatvē। satyam।
﻿<pb n="b365"/>
yatra padanibandhanamēkavākyatvaṁ tatra śrutyaiva vihitābhidhānam। iha punaḥ
upādānataḥ। tasmānna stutiḥ saṁbhavati। padanibandhanōttarakālabhāvitvāt।
atō bhinnavākyānāmapi bhavati vihitābhidhāyakatvam। idaṁ
kāryatvē hya‍upādānaṁ bhavati। tasmātsiddhaṁ vihitābhidhānaṁ mantrāṇāṁ
kāryam।</p>
<p><q>taccōdakēṣu mantrākhyā। uktaṁ mantragatō bhāvaśabdō'bhi-
dhāyaka iti</q>। abhidhāyakō na vidhāyaka ityētāvadvak‍tavyam।
﻿<pb n="b366"/>
kiṁ mantraśabdēna ? na ca mantraśabdābhidhēyatayā । kathaṁ tarhīṣētvētyē-
vamādibhiḥ pratīkaiḥ ? tasmānmantraśabdābhidhānamatiricyata itīva prati-
bhāti । kriyamāṇē'pi mantraśabdābhidhānē na mantratvādabhidhāyakatvaṁ,
vidhāyakatvamapi mantrēṣu vasantāya kapiñjalanālabhata ityēvamādiṣu
dr̥ṣṭam ।</p>
<p>yadapi bhāṣyakārēṇōktam&mdash;<q>ajñātē mantraśabdē tadratō bhāva-
śabdaḥ kathaṁ vicāryō bhaviṣyati ? idamarthatō'dhikaraṇaṁ pūrvaṁ draṣṭa-
vyamiti ।</q> ētadapyayuktamiva । na mantratvādabhidhāyakatvaṁ; kiṁ tarhi ?
viniyuktatvāditi । viniyōgaśca iṣētyēvamādibhiḥ pratīkaiḥ ityuktam ।﻿<pb n="b367"/>
anyathāpi cāyaṁ sūtrārthōṁ gacchatyēva। mantraśabdō'bhidhāyakēṣu pūrva-
sminnadhikaraṇē prayuktaḥ। tadvayākhyānārthamabhidhāyakēṣu kiṁ mantraśabdā---
bhidhānamasti। bāḍhamasti। taccōdakēṣu mantraśabdamabhiyuk‍tāḥ prayuñjatē।
ēvaṁ ca <quote>“prāyikaṁ”</quote> ityētadapi na vak‍tavyam। mantrābhidhānaprasiddhi-
kathanārthamityētatsūtraṁ na mantralakṣaṇaparam। <quote>“lakṣaṇēna tu siddhānāṁ”</quote> ityēva-
mādyasamañjasamēva। tasmādavyāpitālakṣaṇadōṣakathanēna svakauśalapradarśa-
nārthaṁ lakṣaṇasūtratvamadhyārōpyatē। atrabhidhīyatē---bhāṣyakārasyāpi pūrvōktamantra-
padavyākhyānamēvaitadabhiyuktā upadiśanti। <q>mantrā āvartanta iti vadataḥ
﻿<pb n="b368"/>
padārthakathanaparaṁ caitadbhāṣyam। atō yadanyat tallakṣaṇadūṣaṇaparamēva।
prāyikamētaditi prakaṭitam। ata ēva vr̥ttikārōdāharaṇaprapañcōktirapi
naiva mr̥ṣyatē bhāṣyakārēṇa। lakṣaṇābhidhānapakṣē hi lakṣaṇaviśēṣābhidhāna-
mupapadyētāpi। padārthavyākhyānē punaḥ anavasara ēva tallakṣaṇaviśēṣābhidhānasya।
taccaitat vr̥ttikārēṇōdāharaṇāpadēśēnēti vadatā asaṁbaddhataiva kathitā।
tasmānmantrapadārthakathanamēvaitat sūtraṁ na mantralakṣaṇaparam।</p>
﻿<pb n="b369"/>
﻿<pb n="b370"/>
<p><q>śēṣē brāhmaṇaśabdaḥ ।</q> taccōdakēṣu mantrākhyēti mantraśabdārthakathanaparē
sūtrē kaḥ punaḥ prasaṅgaḥ śēṣē brāhmaṇaśabda iti । lakṣaṇaparē punaḥ sūtramupapa-
dyata ēva, lakṣaṇaparē'pyuk‍tō dōṣaḥ । atō na vidmaḥ kathamidamiti । atrō-
cyatē&mdash;śabdārthakathanaparamēvaitatsūtradvayaṁ vidhimantrayōraikārthyamiti । kimidaṁ﻿<pb n="b371"/>
vidhimantrāvityāśaṅkyatē ? astīdaṁ dvayaṁ vēdē kēcinmantrāḥ
kiñcida‍brāhmaṇamiti । yatrābhiyuktā mantraśabdaṁ prayuñjatē sa mantraḥ । yatra
ca vidhiriti ca bruvatē tad‍brāhmaṇam । vr̥ttikāramatōpanyāsastu pūrvavat
draṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b372"/>
<p><q>anāmnātēṣvamantratvam ।</q> ūhapravaranāmadhēyāni cintyantē&mdash;kiṁ
mantraśabdābhilapyānyētāni uta nēti । nanu taccōdakēṣu mantrākhyēti
yatrābhiyuktā mantraśabdaṁ prayuñjatē sa mantra ityuktam । na cābhidhāya-
katvaṁ mantratvē lakṣaṇam । na cōhādīnyabhiyuk‍taiḥ mantratvēnābhilapyantē
tasmādanupapannaḥ saṁśayaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;ūhapravaranāmadhēyairhi
kratuṣu mantrakāryaṁ kriyatē । na cāmantraiḥ mantrakāryaṁ niṣpadyata iti
pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ । rāddhāntavādītu manyatē-satyaṁ amantraiḥ mantrakāryaṁ
na bhavati na punaramantrānugr̥hītaiḥ mantraiḥ । ūhapravaranāmadhēyāni ca mantrāṇā-﻿<pb n="b373"/>
mupakāraṁ kurvanti santyanugrāhakāṇi prayat‍nakaraṇādivat । na
cānugrāhakaṁ mantraśabdābhilapyaṁ prayatnakaraṇamiva । tasmādamantratvam । kaḥ
punarēbhiranugrahō mantrasyēti ? yathaiva tālvādibhirarthābhidhānē sāhāyyam ।</p>
<p>nanu cōhapravaranāmadhēyāni svayamabhidhānaṁ kurvanti na sāhāyyam ।
na khalvatra kaścidviśēṣaḥ । kēcita pradhānakāryē upakurvanti kēcidaṅga-
kāryē । yathā svamisaṁskārāḥ prayājādayaśca । tasmādupapannamamantratvaṁ
svāmisaṁskārāṇāmiva na prādhānyam । prayōjanaṁ bhāṣyōktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b374"/>
<p><q>tēṣāmr̥gyatnārthavaśēna pādavyavasthā ।</q> kēna prasaṅgēnēdamāyātaṁ ?
anēnēdamāyātam । mantrabrāhmaṇaśabdayōḥ vēdābhidhēyasyārthasya vācya&mdash;
tayā niyama uktaḥ । r̥gādiśabdaiśca vyavahārō dr̥śyatē vēdaśabdābhi-
dhēyārtha ēva । r̥cō yajūṁṣi sāmānīti r̥gyajussāmaśabdairēvābhidadhati ।
ataḥ kō bhāgaḥ r̥kśabdēnōcyatē ? kō vā yajuśśabdēna ? kō vā
sāmaśabdēnēti ? tatra r̥kśabdābhidhēyapradarśanārthamidamārabdham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b375"/>
<p>yatra pādavyavasthā sa r̥k‍śabdābhidhēyō'rtha iti nirūpitam ।
arthagrahaṇaṁ tvanuvāda ityuktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa । kaḥ punarayaṁ pādō nāma ?
gāyatryādīnāṁ chandasāṁ bhāgasammitō'kṣarasamūhaḥ pādaḥ ।<p>
<p><q>gītiṣu sāmākhyā ।</q> pragītē mantraḥ sāmēti vaktavyē gītiṣu sāmākhyē
tyucyatē । kathaṁ nāma rathantarādayaḥ sāmaviśēṣaśabdāḥ gītiviśēṣasya
﻿<pb n="b376"/>
vācakāḥ syuriti । nanu ca gītimātrē nābhiyuktāḥ sāma-
śabdaṁ prayuñjatē, yatō rathantaramadhīṣvētyuktaḥ sarkāmēva gītimadhītē na gīti-
mātram । nākṣarāntarēṣvavasthitam । nākṣarāntarēṣvapyanyatra vacanāt ।
athāyamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;na ca padaśūnyaṁ gītakamastīti; sarkā hi gītiḥ
sāmaśabdavācyā । gītisvarūpābhivyak‍tyarthamakṣarōpādānamiti cēt viparītaṁ﻿<pb n="b377"/>
tat, akṣarābhivyañjikā hi gītiriti vakṣyāmaḥ । atō gītimātra-
vacanatvē pratibhāmātraṁ sūtrakārasya ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;anvayavyatirēkāvagamyaṁ hi padapadārthanirūpaṇam ।
tatra yā abhivatī r̥k‍samāmnāyē paṭhyatē sā na rathantaraśabdābhilapyā । kiñca
rathantarabuddhērutpādikā gītiḥ । na punaḥ r̥gēva r̥gādiṣvapi prayujyamānā
adhyētdr̥ṇāṁ rathantarabuddhimutpādayati । bruvatē ca rathantaramanēna ślōkēna
na gītamiti । tasmāt sūktaṁ gītiṣu sāmākhyēti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b378"/>
<p><q>śēṣē yajuḥ śabdaḥ ।</q> gītipādabaddhābhyāṁ yadanyanmantvajātaṁ tadyajuḥ
anayōḥ yallakṣaṇaṁ tacchūnyataiva lakṣaṇaṁ yajuṣaḥ । kathitaḥ trividhō mantraḥ
r̥cō yajūṁṣi sāmānīti ।</p>
<p><q>nigadō vā caturthaṁ syāt ।</q> uktaṁ r̥cō yajūṁṣi sāmānīti
trividhā mantrāḥ । ayamaparaḥ caturthō vyapadēśaḥ śrūyatē nigadā iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b379"/>
ēvamadhyētārō vyapadiśanti nigadā vartantē na yajūṁṣi, yajūṁṣi vartantē na
nigadā iti । upāṁśutvēna prayōgō nēṣyatē nigadānām । kimiti﻿<pb n="b380"/>
nēṣyatē ? vacanāt । kāryasyāsiddhērnēṣyata iti syāt, na; vacanapūrvakatvāt
kāryasya । ata ēvēdaṁ caturthaṁ mantrajātamiṣyatē । mābhūt kāryavirōdhō vacanasya﻿<pb n="b381"/>
ajahatsvārthaṁ vacanamiti sthitam । nanu cōccairnigadēnētyapi vacana-
masti । ayamaparō dōṣaḥ avibhāgē hi vikalpaḥ prāpnōti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b382"/>
tasmāt siddhaṁ nigadō vā caturthaṁ syāditi । atrābhidhīyatē । nēdaṁ caturthaṁ
mantrajātam । yajūṁṣyēva nigadāḥ apādabaddhatvādapragītatvācca । vyapadēśaścaiva-
mupapadyatē । yaduktaṁ vyapadēśādanyatvamiti tat prakarṣābhidhānātparihr̥tam । yadu-
ktamupāṁśutvaṁ vacanāditi tadapyuccairnigadēnēti prakarṣābhidhānōpapattēḥ parihr̥tam﻿<pb n="b383"/>
gōbalīvardavat । na cōccaiṣṭ‍vaina r̥k‍tvaṁ apādabaddhatvādityuktam । tasmāt
siddhaṁ r̥cō yajūṁṣi sāmānīti ।</p>
<p><q>arthaikatvādēkaṁ vākyam ।</q> uktaṁ triprakārō mantra iti ।
pāṭhādēva jñātaparimāṇaṁ dvividhaṁ mantrajātam । yajūṁṣi punaḥ pāṭhāt
parimāṇataḥ na śakyantē jñātuṁ kiyadēkaṁ yajuriti।</p>﻿<pb n="b384"/>
<p>nanu viniyōgādyajūṁṣyapi jñātuṁ śak‍yantē parimāṇataḥ । iṣētvētyā-
c‍chinatti ūrjētvētyanumārṣṭi iti । maivam । viniyōgāddhi tādarthyamava-
sīyatē na parimāṇam tadarthō'yaṁ prayāsaḥ jñātaparimāṇaviniyōgādaidamarthyam ।
nanu cēti śabdaḥ pūrvōktasya karaṇatāmāpādayati । kasya pūrvōktasya ? varṇasya
vēti na vidmaḥ । na cārthasaṁbandhādr̥tē varṇō varṇasyānvayī bhavati padaṁ vā padasya ।﻿<pb n="b385"/>
tasmāt tasyaikasya pūrvōktasyētiśabdaḥ karaṇatāmāpādayati । sa tvanyatō
vijñēyō varṇapadavākyatayā । na hyarthādr̥tē varṇavyatirēkēṇa śak‍yatē varṇasa-
mūhasyēti śabdasaṁbandhō vak‍tum । nanu ca brāhmaṇavākyavat mantravākyamapi
ēkavāk‍yatayā'vasīyatē । satyaṁ, yadi svatantrādarthapratipattiḥ syāt । vini-
yōgasavyapēkṣaṁ hi mantrāṇāmarthapratipādanasāmarthyamityuktaṁ mantrādhikaraṇē ।﻿<pb n="b386"/>
ēvaṁ cēt r̥cō'pi viniyōgāpēkṣatvādarthasya arthaparattvācca mantrāṇā-
manyata ēva parimāṇāvagatiḥ । satyamarthaparijñānamanyataḥ । parimāṇaṁ tu
chandasaḥ sakāśādvijñāyata ityuktam । tasmāt‍kiyadvāk‍yaṁ yajurityē&mdash;
(vama)tāvānasya vyāpāraḥ । sāmāni tu gītakānyabhiyuktaiḥ parimāṇataḥ smaryantē
tadidaṁ parimāṇalakṣaṇaṁ yajuṣāmucyatē । arthaikatvāt sākāṅkṣatvāccēti ।
kimidaṁ arthaikatvaṁ ? anuṣṭhēyasya smaraṇam । ēvaṁ tarhi padaṁ padamātra-﻿<pb n="b387"/>
mēkārthamēkaṁ vāk‍yaṁ; padēna padēna hyanuṣṭhēyasya smaraṇaṁ na vāk‍yēna ।
nanu cānanvitasya padābhidhēyatā nāstīt‍yuktaṁ, ēvaṁ tarhi dvayōrdvayōrēkārthatvaṁ
padārthēna hi padārthō'nvīyatē na padārthasamudāyēna । upapadyatē caitallakṣaṇam
arthaikatvāt sākāṅkṣatvāccēti । ēvaṁ tarhi prayōjanavācyō'yamarthaśabdaḥ
parigr̥hyatē na pratipādyavācī । kathaṁ tarhi sākāṅkṣatvam ?</p>﻿<pb n="b388"/>
ucyatē । dvayōrdvayōḥ saṁbandhaḥ । ēvaṁ cēdupapannamēva sākāṅkṣatvam ।
kintu pradhānapadēna sakalaṁ padajātamabhisaṁbadhyatē prayōjanaṁ ca pradhānāmi
tyucyatē । tasmāt prayōjanavācyē'pi siddhaṁ sākāṅkṣatvam । kimarthamubhayaṁ
sūtritam । uktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa ।</p>
<p><q>samēṣu vākyabhēdaḥ syāt ।</q> yatrēdānīṁ vidhyantara&mdash;﻿<pb n="b389"/>
vihitaprayōjanasaṁbandhō nāsti yajuṣaścaikārthatvaṁ viniyōgādityuktam;
tatra kiṁ tata ēva viniyōgādēkārthatvaṁ utānyatō mr̥g‍yam ।﻿<pb n="b390"/>
pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yajuṣa ēva ēkārthatā yuktā na viniyōgataḥ
pārārthyamātraparyavasānādviniyōgasya । ya(dya)dīṣētvētyatrādhyāhārādēkārthatvaṁ
ēvamūrjētvētyēvamādisahitasyāpi । tasmādēkaṁ vāk‍yam pratipattiprayōjana
guṇapradhānabhāvō bhaviṣyati r̥cāmiva kāryāntarē prayujyamānānāmiti ।﻿<pb n="b391"/>
atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;viniyōgādēvaikaṁ prayōjanaṁ yuktam । kasmāt ?
yatra viniyōgaḥ tat prayōjanaṁ yasmāt । na tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ, śākhā
hi prayōjanam । vacanāntaravihitatvānnirvāpavat । satyaṁ prayōjanam ।
na tu pratipādyatayā । pratipādyēna prayōjanēna prayōjanavantō mantrāḥ ।
tasmādadhyāhārāpēkṣatvāt pratipādyasya sarvārthamēkaṁ bhaviṣyatīti pradarśitam ।﻿<pb n="b392"/>
rāddhāntavādinastvayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;adhyāhr̥tasyaikasya anēkāryatayā guṇa-
pradhānārthatā dr̥ṣṭārthatā vā kal‍panīyā । taccōbhayamap‍yanyāyyam । tasmā-
dyathāviniyōgaṁ vāk‍yam । iṣētvēti padārthadvayasaṁbandhāt śak‍yata itiśabdēna
saṁbandhaḥ pratipat‍tumiti, niyōgō hi vāk‍yārthasya karaṇatāmāpādayati
padārthasyēva vibhaktiyōgaḥ । tasmādyathāviniyōgaṁ vāk‍yabhēdaḥ । ēvaṁ
<quote>‘k‍lr̥ptīrvācayati’</quote> iti bahūnāṁ viniyuktatvāt tanniṣpattyarthaṁ k‍lr̥ptēḥ prādhānyaṁ
nādriyatē vibhāgavat ।</p>﻿<pb n="b393"/>
<p><q>anuṣaṅgō vāk‍yasamāptiḥ ।</q> saivēyaṁ yajurgatā kathā vartatē । nanu
cēyaṁ vr̥ttā । viniyōgataḥ sāmarthyataḥ parimāṇamuk‍taṁ yajuṣaḥ । satyamuktam ।
uktaviṣaya ēvāyaṁ punarvicāraḥ । kaḥ punarasau । ayamasau, yatra bahūni vāk‍ya-
śēṣāpēkṣāṇi vāk‍yāni ēkaśca vāk‍yaśēṣaḥ kiṁ yasyānantaraṁ tēnaiva saṁbadhyatē
uta yāvadbhirākāṅkṣayata iti । kiṁ punaratra yuktam ? pūrvapakṣavādī tvēvaṁ﻿<pb n="b394"/>
manyatē । ākāṁkṣā sannidhiḥ yōgyatvaṁ ca saṁbandhahētuḥ sannidhiścāpēkṣikaḥ ।
tasmādanantaraṁ sannihitamucyatē'vyavadhānapēkṣam । atō[nā]nuṣaṅgaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;satyamākāṅkṣā sannidhiḥ yōgyatvaṁ ca saṁbandhē hētuḥ
sannidhānaṁ punarnāvyavadhānāpēkṣam । kiṁ tarhi ? sajātīyāvyavadhānāpēkṣam ।
na cātra sajātīyō vāk‍yaśēṣō vyavadhāyakō (dr̥śyatē)vidyatē । śōṣiṇastvasajā-
tīyatvānna vyavadhāyakāḥ । na hi yō yamapēkṣatē sa tasya vyavadhāyakō bhavati﻿<pb n="b395"/>
yathā bahūni ākhyātākāṅkṣāṇi nāmāni । tatra sambandhē
ānantaryamātrānna vyavadhānaṁ kurvanti । atha manyasē padadharmō'ya&mdash;
miti na padatvātsaṁbandhaḥ । kiṁ tarhi ? ākāṅkṣitatvādēva ।﻿<pb n="b396"/>
yat‍punaridaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa samudāyāpēkṣatayā''nantaryamupanyastam samudāyi-
bhiśca sambandhaḥ kastasyārthaḥ ayamēvārthō yō'smābhirvyākhyātaḥ ।
ētaduktaṁ bhavati&mdash;padasamudāyasyaiva ēkapadasaṁbandhē nānantaryaṁ viśēṣyatē ।﻿<pb n="b397"/>
pratipadaṁ ca sambandhaḥ । ēvañca paurvāparyamap‍yatantram । kiyāṁstu
sannidhiriti yadēvōktaṁ yāvadanyatsajātīyaṁ nōpanipatatīti tadēvēdam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b398"/>
<p><q>anuṣaṅgaḥ ।</q> yatrēdānīṁ śēṣīṇi nirākāṅkṣāṇi śēṣaśca sākāṅkṣaḥ,
tatrāpi saiva kathā asajātīyavyavadhānāt sarvaiḥ saṁbandhaḥ । kimarthaṁ tarhi
punarlikhitam ? tadēva tu na jñāyatē । kiṁ śēṣitāmātramēva sajātī-
yatvaṁ uta pradhānapadābhiprāyamiti । tatra pūrvēṇa nyāyēna śōṣitamātraṁ sa-
jātīyamiti prāptaṁ tadvayudāsāyēdaṁ punarlikhitam । ēkākhyātasaṁbandhē satīti﻿<pb n="b399"/>
pūrvatra vā'bhinnākhyātasaṁbandhē sati kiṁ bhavatyanuṣaṅgaḥ ? kimida&mdash;
mākhyātagrahaṇam ? pradhānapadapradarśanārthamēva । ēvaṁ tarhi pūrvatrāpi
pradhānapadābhēdādēvānuṣaṅgaḥ । tasmādanarthakaṁ punarlēkhyam ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē&mdash;pradhānapadābhēdēpi nirākāṅkṣēṣu pradhānēṣu ēkatvādvāk‍ya-
śēṣasya ēkēnaiva saṁbandhō yuktaḥ śak‍yatē ca viśēṣō'vagantuṁ, ānantaryāṁt ।
satyaṁ yatrārthabhēdaḥ । yatra tvartha ēva na bhidyatē tatra pūrvavadēvānuṣaṅgaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b400"/>
<p><q>vyavāyānnānuṣajyēta ।</q> yatra punaḥ sajātīyēna vyavadhānaṁ tatra
vyavāyānnānuṣaṅgaḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ dvitīyādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।<yatrailer>﻿<pb n="b401"/>
<head>br̥hatī</head>
<trailer>dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
<p><q>śabdāntarē karmabhēdaḥ ।</q> śabdāntarē karmabhēda iti śrūyatē ।
kaḥ punaratra śabdō'bhiprētaḥ kiṁ vā karma ? śāstraṁ śabdō'bhiprētaḥ,
niyōgārthaḥ karma । kathaṁ tarhi anubandhabhēdādbhēda ucyatē karmaṇaḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b402"/>
kimiti vā nōcyatē ? śāstrāddhi karmaṇō'nubandhaḥ । ēvañcētarētarāśrayaḥ
tasmācchāstraparimāṇajñānōpāyastāvadanyatō vaktavyaḥ । tasmācchāstrāntaratvē
yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ । atrōcyatē । dvayamapyatraiva pratipādyatē । kathaṁ ?
śāstrāntarē sati karmabhēda iti vadatā śāstrātkarmabhēda ityuktam । nānu-﻿<pb n="b403"/>
bandhāt । kathaṁ punaḥ śāstrāntaraparijñānam? atrāpi kr̥tānubandhatvādityu-
ktam । nanu ca karmānubadhyatē na śāstram । kēna cōk‍taṁ nēti ? parimāṇa-
parijñānē hi śāstrāsyānubandha upakarōti । na tarhi kr̥tānubandhaṁ śāstraṁ bhavati ।﻿<pb n="b404"/>
pratipādakatayā kr̥tō'nubandhaḥ pratītiryēna tat kr̥tānubandham । yadvā
kr̥tānubandhatvātkarmaṇaḥ । anubandhāntarēṇānvayasyānabhidhānāt । anu-
bandhāntaratvē śāstrāntaratvaṁ śāstrāntaratvē śāstrārthāntaratvam । kathaṁ
tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ? ēvamatra pūrvapakṣayanti । ayuktamidaṁ anubandha-
bhēdāt śāstraṁ bhidyata iti । kasmāt ? dr̥ṣṭaṁ hi anēkānubandhamēkaṁ
śāstraṁ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṁ svargakāmō yajētēti । ēvaṁ yāgadānahōmānu-
bandhēṣvapi mābhūdbhēdaḥ । nanu ca karaṇētikartavyatāvyavasthānāttatrābhēdaḥ﻿<pb n="b405"/>
anubandhāntarē'pi tāvadabhēda iti pratipannam । avasthānaṁ tu viniyōga-
tō'vagamyam । na cāyamēkāntaḥ karaṇētikartavyatāvyavasthānādēvēti
kēvalakaraṇāvasthitānāmapi bahūnāmēkaśāstrāvagamyatvaṁ dr̥ṣṭaṁ darśapūrṇa-
māsayōḥ; rājasūyē ca utpattāvapi prājāpatyāniti । nanu ca prājāpatyēṣu
saṅkhyayā bhēdaḥ bhavatu, anubandhabhēdastāvanna bhēdakaḥ । asati cānubandhabhēdē
saṅkhyā bhēt‍trīti namō bhēdavidbhayaḥ । tasmāt pracayāvagamyō'yamanu-
﻿<pb n="b406"/>
bandhasamudāya ēkaśāstrāvagamyaḥ । ēkaśāstrāvagabhyē ca ēkō niyōgārthaḥ
tadēvāpūrvam । yadvā pratyayāvagamyatvāt niyōgārthasya sānubandhataiva na
pratīyatē । padārthasyēva padārthāntarēṇa ।</p>
<p>nanu ca padārthō'pi padārthāntarēṇānubaddha ēva । parasparānvayitā
hyanubandhaḥ ucyatē । anabhijñō bhavānanuvandhānvayayōḥ । kaḥ
punaranayōḥ viśēṣaḥ? ayamanayōrviśēṣaḥ । kriyākārakaguṇiguṇyaida-
marthyasaṁbandhitā'nvaya ucyatē । niyōgasya viṣayitāpantiranubandhaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b407"/>
na ca śabdāntarābhidhēyō viṣayatāmāpadyatē । aviniyuktaviniyōgāpēkṣitvē
cāgr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣaṇatvaṁ prayājādīnāmiva । tasmātsiddhamēkaśāstrābhidhēyatvam ।
yadvā yāgadānahōmēṣvayamaparō viśēṣaḥ । anubandhānāṁ nānātvamapi(vai)na
śakyatē vak‍tum । parasparānuvādasaṁbhavāt yadāhavanīyē juhvatītivat ।
ēvaṁ guṇakarmasu guṇavidhānēṣu ca draṣṭavyam । pradhānānupravēśāttadvidhānasya ।
﻿<pb n="b408"/>
ēvañca sarvaphalānubandhaṁ sarvaguṇānubandhaṁ sarvadhātvarthānubandhamēkaṁ karma ।
ēkō niyōga ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē । na ca sarvaviṣaya ēkō niyōgārthaḥ pratipat‍tuṁ
śakyatē । bhāvārtha ēva hi karmaśabdō bhāvārthāntaranirapēkṣō viṣayama-
vacchinatti । karaṇāpattau hi bhāvārthāntarāpēkṣā bhāvārthasya na viṣayāpattau ।﻿<pb n="b409"/>
viṣayībhūtasya hi niyōgārthaṁ prati sādhanabhāvō'vagamyatē na punaḥ tatsādhana-
tayaiva niyōgasaṁbandhaḥ । yathā caitadēvaṁ tathā ṣaṣṭhē vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmāt
dhātvarthabhēdānniyōgamēdaḥ niyōgabhēdācca siddhaṁ karmāntaratvam, yadapyuktam
niyōgārthasya pratyayavācyatvāt, agr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatvāt sarvabhāvārthābhi-
saṁbandha iti । tadayuktam । agr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatā hi niyōgē na viṣayē ।
﻿<pb n="b410"/>
taduktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa&mdash;yajirapyēvaṁ svōccāraṇāvagamyaviṣayē nōccāraṇāntarama-
pēkṣatē । yā punarēkārthatā yāgahōmānāmupavarṇitā sā nōpapadyatē bhinnārthāvagatēḥ ।
na ca vidhēyārthatvē saṁbhavati anuvādatā yuktā । yatpunaridamuktam
darśapūrṇamāsayōrivānēkānubandhaviṣayatā ēvāvagamyanta iti । parihr̥ta-
midamasmābhiḥ । viniyōjyatayā tadavasīyatē na viṣayatayā ।
﻿<pb n="b411"/>
ata ēva cāgnēyādayō'bhinnaviṣayā ēva na bhinnaviniyōjyāḥ । tasmātsiddhaṁ
prativiṣayaṁ śās‍trabhēdaḥ tadbhēdācca karmabhēda iti ।</p>
<p><q>ēkasyaivaṁ punaḥ śrutiḥ ।</q> uktaṁ kr̥tānubandhatvācchās‍trabhēdaḥ
śāstrabhēdātkarmabhēda iti । yatra punaranubandhō'pyēkaḥ tatra kathaṁ ? bhavatu
tatraikaṁ śāstram, ēkaṁ ca karma । nanu cānarthakaṁ bhavati ।</p>﻿<pb n="b412"/>
kimidamānarthakyaṁ nāma ? yadi tāvannārthapratipādakatvaṁ, tadayuktam, pratyu-
tārthāntaratvē'pratipādakaṁ bhavati । atha niṣprayōjanatvaṁ, avagamyamānaṁ hi
yadi prayōjanaṁ na bhavati mābhūt kō dōṣaḥ । tasmādēkaṁ karma ।
atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;vidyata ēvānubandhabhēdō'trāpi । kutaḥ aviśēṣāt ।
naitacchakyatē vak‍tum । asyārthasyētthaṁ punaḥ śrutirvartata iti । yāgadāna-
hōmādīnāmapi hyarthabhēdādēvānubandhatā bhidyatē taccātrāpi tulyam । nanu
cātraikō yāgārthaḥ pratīyatē satyamēvaikō yāgaḥ na tu vidhēyatayā ।
﻿<pb n="b413"/>
kathaṁ punarēkaḥ pratīyamānō'pi vidhēyatayā nānātvaṁ bhajatē yathā jyōtiṣṭōma-
darśapūrṇamāsayōḥ । ādhastyamadhikaraṇamidānīṁ k‍vōpayujyatē ? viśēṣāddhi
tatrānubandhabhēdaḥ । iha tvaviśēṣādityupayōgaḥ । ata ēva bhāṣyakārēṇa
pūrvapakṣē sa ēva śabdaḥ punaḥ punaruccāryata iti vadatā na viśēṣādr̥tē'nubandha-
nānātvaṁ siddhayatīti pradarśitam । guṇavidhānaṁ punaḥ kimarthamāśāṅkitam ?﻿<pb n="b414"/>
punaḥ śrutērudāharaṇaṁ durlabhamiti manvānēnēdamāśaṅkitam । guṇanā-
nātvāddhi śrutyantaramēva bhavati । nāmāni vā bhavantu । tathāpi
śrutyantaramēva । parihārastu na kēvaladhātvarthavidhāvasati guṇavidhānaṁ nāma vā
na saṁbhavati guṇō hi vidhīyamānaḥ samidhō yajatīti kva vidhīyatām ? yadi
tāvatpradhānayāgē, guṇāntarāvarōdhāt na saṁbhavati । atha samidyāgaēva, yāga-﻿<pb n="b415"/>
vidhānamapi prāpnōti yāgavidhānē ca nivr̥ttiḥ guṇavidhānasya śrutēḥ nāma&mdash;
tāvagamāt । ēvaṁ pañcasvapi draṣṭavyam । nāmnō'nuvādatvāt yajiśrutirēva
kēvalaṁ viṣayaviśēṣaṇaṁ tasmādētānyēvōdāharaṇāni punaḥ śrutēḥ । na cātra nāma
bhēdakaṁ vidhānōttarakālabhāvitvānnamabhāvasya । abhēdakamēva tarhi sarvatra nāma,
vidhānōttarakālabhāvitvāt । ucyatē । samidādiṣu tu na bhēdakam ।
﻿<pb n="b416"/>
jyōtiṣṭōmādiṣu tu yathā bhēdakaṁ tathā tatraiva viśēṣaṁ varṇayiṣyāmaḥ ।
tasmādaviśēṣādanubandhabhēdaḥ anubandhabhēdācchastrabhēdaḥ śāstrabhēdātkāryabhēda
iti siddham ।</p>
<p><q>prakaraṇaṁ tu paurṇamāsyām ।</q> uk‍taṁ punaḥ śrutērapyanubandhānya-
tvamaviśēṣāditi । asyāmidānīṁ punaḥ śrutau ya ēvaṁ vidvān
paurṇamāsīṁ yajatē ya ēvaṁ vidvānamāvāsyāṁ yajata iti kimanu&mdash;
