bandhabhēdō vidyatē nētīti cintyatē । pūrvōk‍tēna nyāyēnā&mdash;﻿<pb n="b417"/>
viśēṣādanubandhabhēdaḥ । śabdāntaratvaṁ kimityupanyastam ? abhyāsādēvā-
viśēṣāditi yuktirgamyatē । atrābhidhīyatē । ubhayaprakārō'tra bhēdaḥ
cintyatē karaṇētikartavyatākr̥tō viṣayakr̥taśca । tatrābhyāsādviṣayakr̥tabhēda-
siddhiḥ, śabdāntarāt karaṇētikartavyatābhēdaḥ tasmādyuk‍tamubhayamupanyaratam ।
ata ēva samapradhānāṅgāṅgibhāvānuvādavidhānāni kramēṇōpanyastāni ।
﻿<pb n="b418"/>
na vidhānamātrāt samapradhānabhōvasiddhiḥ । nāpyanuvādamātrāt guṇapradhāna-
bhāvaḥ । kiṁ rhi ? śabdāntaratvāt guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ, abhidhānā-
ntaratvādityarthaḥ । abhidhānaikyācca samapradhānabhāvaḥ । kiṁ punaraḍga-
pradhānatayā bhēdakathanē prayōjanam ? (na)viṣayatō vā bhēdakathanē kiṁ
prayōjanam ? kathaṁ nāma bhēdēnānuṣṭhānaṁ syāditi । ēvaṁ cēt
atrāpyaṅgapradhānatayā kathaṁ nāmānuṣṭhānaṁ syāditi । nanu cāḍga-
pradhānatā viniyōgādēvāvagamyatē phalavadaphalatayā । kimabhinnasyaiva
viniyōgādavagatiḥ ? na brūmō'bhinnasyēti । kintu viṣayamātra-﻿<pb n="b419"/>
bhēdādbhinnasyētyucyatē । yadi viṣayabhēda ēva aṅgāṅgitvē hētuḥ kimiti na
pradhānāni parasparāṅgam ? samidādīni vā । tasmāt kāryacōdanātō bhēdō-
'ṅgāṅgitvē hētuḥ na viṣayacōdanātaḥ atō viṣayatvēna bhinnānāṁ kāryē śabdā-
ntarataivānubandhabhēdē hētuḥ bhinnānāṁ ca viniyōgāt । phalavadaphalatayā
cāṅgāṅgitvamavagamyatē । tasmāt prayōgacōdanātō bhēdō'pyatraiva
pradaśanīyaḥ । taduktam । śabdāntaratvādabhyāsācca samapradhānā-
nīti bhāṣyē bahuvacanādviṣayabhēdaḥ prātipadikātkāryānyatvam ।﻿<pb n="b420"/>
tadidaṁ lakṣaṇādāvuktaṁ pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣyantē bhinnānyabhinnāni cēti ।
pradhānānītyaṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ apradhānānīti viṣayaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;<q>prakr̥tānāmanuvaditārau paurṇamāsyamāvāsyā-
saṁyuktau</q>, kutaḥ ? viśē, viśēṣāvagamāt । pūrvasyāḥ śrutēriyaṁ punaḥ śrutirgamyatē ।
kasmāt ? kālasaṁbaddhā hōyaṁ cōdanā । yadyatna kālasaṁsparśō'rthō na
gr̥hyatē tadā tadarthasyāgrahaṇamēva । anyathānavagamāt । yadi punaḥ
kālasaṁsparśō na gr̥hyatē tadā pūrvasyāḥ śrutēriyaṁ punaḥ śrutiḥ spaṣṭā ।﻿<pb n="b421"/>
kālayōginī hi sā śrutiḥ । atha kasmānna viparītaṁ ? agnyādērabhyadhikasyā-
vagamāt । tasmādiyamēva punaḥ śrutiḥ tatō'nuvādaḥ anuvādatvācca kāryē
śabdāntaratvādbhēdaḥ । atrāgnēyādīni payō'ntāni pradhānāni prayā-
jādīnyaṅgāni । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ ? anuvāda ēva prayājādīnyaṅgāni na
punarvidhāvapi । kathaṁ vā vidhipakṣē'ṅgāṅgitā śaṅkayatē ? । ēvamā-﻿<pb n="b422"/>
śaṅkyatē । tayōrhi karmaṇōrvacanāntarēṇa kālavidhānaṁ <quote>“paurṇamāsyāṁ paurṇamāsyā
yajēta,”</quote> <quote>“amāvāsyāyāmamāvāsyayā yajēta”</quote> iti । tataḥ kiṁ ? idaṁ tatō
bhavati, aṣṭānāṁ yāgānāṁ darśapūrṇamāsaśabdavācyatā bhavati āgnēyādiguṇa&mdash;
vidhipakṣē vā dvayōrēva । ataśca tayōḥ phalasaṁbandhaḥ । tēṣāṁ vā । prayājādīnā-
maṅgataiva । tasmādanupapannāmidaṁ vidhau samaprādhānyam anuvādē'ṅgāṅgitēti ।﻿<pb n="b423"/>
ucyatē । na kālavidhirdvayōḥ saṁbhavati । prayōgaśēṣatā hi
paurṇamāsyāṁ paurṇamāsyā yajēta iti pratīyatē na viṣayaśēṣatā । yadyapya-
nayōrutpattikālayōgābhāvēna darśapūrṇamāsapadavācyatā nāsti tathāpi darśa-
pūrṇamāsābhyāmiti ṣaṇṇāṁ darśapūrṇamāsaśabdatā kēna vāryatē । anabhijñō
bhavān vidhyanuvādaśabdasāmarthyasya dēvānāṁ priyaḥ । yathā'nuvādaṁ
hi śakyatē saṅkhayā'vagantum । tātparyē ca viśēṣataḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b424"/>
atātparyē ayathānuvādē ca na saṅkhayāyōginaḥ upapadavaśānniyamaḥ﻿<pb n="b425"/>
śakyatē'vagantuṁ rājasūyavat । tasmānna saṅkhayā nāpyupapadaṁ viśēṣāvagatau
hētuḥ atō dvayaṁ dhātvarthānusāri tatra bhavatīti yuktamuktam । tatrētarē guṇa-
vidhaya iti yaduktamupanyāsē tadidamucyatē । atha kasmānnāgnēyādīni
guṇavidhānāni । ētau ca karmavidhī । śakyatē saṅkhayānusāritayā
dvayōḥ prādhānyaṁ vak‍tuṁ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṁ svargakāmō yajētēti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b426"/>
<p><q>cōdanā vā guṇānām ।</q> naitatsaṁbhavati । yadi tāvatpaurṇamā-
syāmaṣṭākapālē bhavatīti saṁbandhō vivakṣitaḥ, na tāvadayamarthaḥ aṣṭōkapōlaḥ
sattayā saṁbadhyata iti bhavatyarthēna na saṁbadhyata ityarthaḥ । athōg‍nēyaḥ
paurṇamāsyāṁ bhavatīti vivakṣyatē tadāpyāgnēyapurōḍāśayōrasaṁbandha ēva ।
pūrvēṇa sahōsya pakṣasya kō viśēṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśēṣaḥ guṇa-﻿<pb n="b427"/>
pradhānavivakṣā'tra । bhavatu yathēṣṭam tathāpi parasparasaṁbandhō naiva
śakyatē vidhātum । atha paurṇamāsyāmaṣṭākapālasyāgnēyatā vidhīyatē
atha tasyāmāgnēyasyāṣṭākapālatēti । idamapi pakṣadvayaṁ avivakṣōtsaṅkalanāyai-
﻿<pb n="b428"/>
vōbhayatra paurṇamāsīpadasaṁbandhō duśśakaḥ । yadapi padadvayaṁ
agniprajāpativat paurṇamāsīsaṁbandhitayā vidhīyata ityupanyastam
tatrāpi saṁbhavati padadvayavidhānam । arūpatā tu pūrvavadēvāg‍nēyāṣṭāka-
pālayōḥ saṁbandhābhāvāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b429"/>
<p>athāgnīṣōmīyavat saṁbaddhayōrvidhānamityucyatē, kauryatvātsaṁbandhasya na
vidhānādr̥tē siddhiḥ agnīṣōmau tu prasiddhau dvandvatayā mitrāvaruṇavat ।
athātrāpi pūrvakr̥taḥ saṁbandhaḥ kēnacit parigr̥hyatē tathāpi saivā-
rūpatā ihāvidhānāt । athāg‍nēya iti siddhavadvidhāya
punarāg‍nēyatōcyatē । na ca sakr̥duccaritasya arthadvayaṁ(vidhānaṁ)saṁbhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b430"/>
atha rātrisatravadagnirēva dēvatā kalpyatē, na; pramāṇābhāvāt । rātrisatrē
tarhi kathaṁ ? tatrārthavādānupapattēḥ; iha ca dravyamātratayōpapattiḥ । na dravyaṁ
dēvatāmapēkṣatē । dēvatā hi dravyāpēkṣiṇī dravyasaṁbandhitayaiva dēvatētyucyatē ।
tasmāddēvatāvidhānārthaṁ dravyadēvatāsaṁbandhō vidhātavyaḥ sa cēdvidhīyatē
siddhaṁ karmāntaratvam । na ca karma karmāntarasya rūpaṁ bhavatīti﻿<pb n="b431"/>
arūpatvāditi siddhō hētuḥ । atha yaduk‍taṁ lakṣaṇēti pramāṇāntarāvagamānna
dōṣaḥ । <quote>“vyapadēśaśca tadvat”</quote> iti prayājādibhyaḥ āg‍nēyādīnāṁ śabdā-
ntarābhidēyatāṁ kathayati śabdāntaratvācca siddhō guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ । tadvacca
﻿<pb n="b432"/>
liṅgadarśanamiti । kathaṁ punaḥ bahuṣvabhidhēyēṣu ēkavacanaṁ paurṇamāsīmiti ?
kiṁ kurmaḥ ? kamupālabhēmahi ? nityō'yaṁ vaidikaprayōgaḥ । tatra tatra bahupvē-
kavacanamiti jñātamasmābhiḥ । jñānamēvēdamasiddham । ēkavacanaśravaṇā-
dyajirupapadaṁ caikasyaiva pratipādakamiti yuk‍tamabhyupagantum । satyaṁ yuk‍taṁ,
na tu tadiha śakyatē yajyarthatulyatvāt paurṇamāsyarthatulyatvācca । agr̥hya-
māṇaviśēṣatvē cāpratipattirvā syāt । sarvāvagatirvā । tatra kiṁ yuktam ?
nāpratipattiryuktā, avagamaviśēdhāt sarvāvagatēḥ svavagamānugrahaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b433"/>
nanu cātrāpyēkāvagamavirōdhaḥ । parihāryavirōdhastvasau । pracayāvagamāt ।
apratipattau tu aparihāryō'vagamavirōdhaḥ । tasmātsūk‍taṁ samudāyābhiprāya&mdash;
mēkavacanamiti । yad‌dvivacanavirōdhādvidhānapakṣē darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti
samaprādhānyamiti tadayuktamivēdānīṁ pratibhāti । atrāpi kāladvayā&mdash;
vacchinnapracayāvagamāt śakyaparihāramētad‌dvitvam । tasmādvidhāna-
pakṣē'pyaṅgaṅgitaiva nyāyyā । atrābhidhīyatē । saivātrānabhijñatā'parādhyatē ।
kathaṁ ? bahūṣu dhātōḥ prātipadikasya vā prayōgaḥ tantramēkaśēṣō vā । ubhayatra
darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti vidhipakṣē dvitvavirōdhaḥ । kathaṁ? yadi tāvat
tantratvaṁ ṣaṇṇāmēva hi tatpratīyatē । na punastrayāṇāṁ, tantradvayē hi
dviruccāraṇaṁ syāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b434"/>
na ca tadapyasti । ṣaṇṇāṁ ca tantratvē pracayadvayāvagatau pramāṇāntaraṁ 
mr̥gyam । ēkābhidhānāddhayēkapracayāvagatiḥ । ākhyātānusāri
ca nāmadhēyamityuk‍taṁ bhāvārthādhikaraṇē <quote>‘sthita ētasminnadhikaraṇa’</quote>
iti vadatā । tasmāt kāladvayamapyasmin pakṣē pravr̥ttimātraupayikaṁ
nāmnaḥ na punaravacchēdāyālam । agnihōtravat । tadanvayiravārthābhidhānaṁ
darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti yāgamātranāmatayā pratipattavyam । ēvamēkaśēṣō-
'pyayaṁ ṣaṇṇāṁ na trayāṇāṁ trayāṇāmiti । tasmāt pracayadvayāvagati-﻿<pb n="b435"/>
rdurlabhā vidhipakṣē । anuvādapakṣē punaḥ trayāṇāṁ trayāṇāṁ tantraikaśēṣayōḥ
siddhayōḥ pracayadvayāvagatau satyāṁ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti pracayadvayasyaivā-
yamēkaśēṣaḥ tantratvaṁ cēti siddhō guṇapradhānabhāvabhēdaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>paurṇamāsīvadupāṁśuyājaḥ syāt ।</q> uk‍taṁ caturdaśa paurṇamā-
syāmāhutayō hūyantē trayōdaśāmāvāsyāyāmiti । tatra yadyēka upāṁśuyājaḥ
tadaitadupapadyatē । atha trayāṇāmanuvādakamupāṁśuyājamantarā yajatīti, caturdaśa
paurṇamāsyāmāhutayō hūyantē trayōdaśāmāvāsyāyāmiti na ghaṭatē tatprasaṅgādi-
damadhikaraṇamārabdham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b436"/>
<p>kathaṁ punaratra saṁśayaḥ ? tatrāpyāg‍nēyādaya iva viṣṇurupāṁśu yaṣṭavya
ityēvamādayaḥ śrūyantē । kimēṣāmupāṁśuyājamantarā yajatīti samudāyānu-
vādaḥ uta vidhiriti । nanu caikamidaṁ vākyaṁ, kathamatra saṁśayaḥ । nahyē-
kasmin vākyē bahavō vidhayaḥ saṁbhavanti । tadēva tvēkavākyatva-
mākṣipyatē । kathaṁ ? jāmi vā ētadyajñasya kriyata ityupakramō'yaṁ viṣṇu-
rupāṁśu yaṣṭavya ityēvamādīnāṁ sādhāraṇa iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē ।﻿<pb n="b437"/>
bhavati ca sādhāraṇō vākyaśēṣaḥ । varṣiṣṭhādiṣu darśanāt । yad‌brāhmaṇā-
nīti cātidēśadarśanāt । tasmādupapannaḥ saṁśayaḥ । tatra tāvatpūrvapakṣa-
vādī manyatē sādhāraṇō'yaṁ vākyaśēṣō nyāyyaḥ iti । kutaḥ ? rūpāvacanāt
<q>nanūpāṁśuyājamantarā</q> yajatīti rūpamasti । <q>nēdaṁ rūpaṁ karmaṇaḥ ।</q> prayuvatē
syādapi । ēvaṁ tarhyupāṁśuguṇaḥ śrūyatē । nātra guṇavidhiḥ śakyatē'dhvavasātuṁ
yājayōgāt avayavārthavatvē hi asyōpāṁśuyāga iti rūpaṁ rūpavidō manyadhyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b438"/>
tasmādarūpatvāt ayamanuvādaḥ । ēvaṁ ca paurṇamāsyāṁ yajan‍nityanēna trayā-
ṇāmēvaitatkālavidhānam । tataścaturdaśa paurṇamāsyāmiti duḥstham । kiṁ punaḥ
kāraṇaṁ guṇavidhipakṣa ēvaitadrūpam na punarnāmadhēyapakṣē; śabdāntaramapi
hyupapannaṁ nāmadhēyapakṣē śakyatē vak‍tum । guṇavidhipakṣē punaḥ yajyartha ēva
yajiḥ । nanu ca nāmadhēyapakṣē'pi yajyartha ēvāyam । satyaṁ yajyarthō na yajiḥ ।
kiṁ tarhi upāṁśuyājaḥ śabdaḥ । yajyarthasya hi yajēḥ kutvaṁ smaranti na punarya-
jyarthāvayavasya । tasmādupapadyata ēvōpāṁśuyāja iti nāmadhēyam । yatra puna-
ravayavayōgāparityāgēna yajirnāmatāṁ pratipadyatē tatra bhavatyēva kutvam ।
﻿<pb n="b439"/>
tathā cāpavādaṁ smarati bhagavān pāṇiniḥ <quote>‘prayājānūyājau yajñāṅgē’</quote> iti
nōpasargā avayavāpahnavaṁ kartuṁ samarthāḥ । ānarthakyē(nā)pyupasargatvasya
saṁbhavāt । nanu ca kriyāyōgē satyānarthakyē(nā)pyupasargatvam । astyēva
ayaṁ kriyāyōgō yāja iti karmaṇa ēvaitē nāmanī prayājānūyājāviti ।
ata ēva cōpāṁśuyāja iti nāpavādaṁ smr̥tavān śabdarūpavit ।</p>
<p><q>cōdanā vā prakr̥tatvāt ।</q> atrābhidhīyatē । nātrānuvādaḥ
saṁbhavati । kutaḥ ? anūdyamānasyāsaṁbhavāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b440"/>
<p>nanu viṣṇurupāṁśu yaṣṭavya iti yāgacōdanāḥ santītyupanyastam,
ayuktaṁ tadupanyastam । kutaḥ ? nahi vidhyantaraṁ asmin vākyē
saṁbhavati । spaṣṭē hi vidhibhēdē vākyaśēṣasya sādhāraṇatōpapadyatē na punaḥ
sādhyē । vākyaśēṣasya sādhāraṇyādvidhitvaṁ vidhitvē sādhāraṇyamiti
itarētarāśrayam । saṁbhavati ca vākyaśēṣatayā viṣṇvādīnāmarthavattā
upāṁśuyājamantarā yajatītyanēna saṁbandhāviśēṣāt । saṁbhavati caika-
vākyatvē vākyabhēdō vikalpārtha ēva bhavati ।</p>﻿<pb n="b441"/>
<p>nanu ca rūpaṁ nāstītyuktam । vākyāntarēṇāgnihōtra iva bhaviṣyati ।
dr̥śyantē ca vākyāntarāṇi <quote>‘paurṇamāsyāṁ yajan’</quote>, <quote>‘sarvasmai vā ētadājyaṁ’</quote>
iti ca । kiñca na viṣṇurupāṁśu yaṣṭavya iti yāgavidhirgamyatē upapadaśrava-
ṇāt raktapaṭavat । nanu cōpāṁśuyājamantarā yajatītyatrāpyupapadaśravaṇam ।
satyam । bhāvārthatā tvatra vidhiviṣayatayā'vagamyamānā na viniyōgē-
nākṣēp‍tuṁ śakyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b442"/>
<p>pradarśitaṁ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti । tacchūnyē punarviniyōgānusārī
vidhirbhavatīti viśēṣaḥ । taduktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa-sa tu vidhīyata
upāṁśutvādisambandha iti । nanu cātra guṇavidhānaṁ pratīyatē । nētyucyatē ।
arthavādatō guṇaprāptēraguṇavidhisvarūpatvāccēti pratyuk‍tam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b443"/>
kathamēkavākyatvamiti ? kō'bhiprāyaḥ pr̥cchataḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ
parasparāsaṁbandhādviṣṇvādīnāṁ asaṁbaddhānāṁ ca padāntarasaṁbandhastantrēṇaiva bhavati ।
yathāha bhagavān । astyatrōpādhyantaram । kiṁ tata ? prādhānyē
satīti vaktavyam । iha punarupāṁśuyājamantarā yajatīti pradhānaṁ
tatprādhānyē ca viṣṇurityēvamādīnāṁ aruṇādīnāmivaikavākyatā
nyāyyētyuktam । kaḥ<q>punaratrārthavāda</q> iti ? kēnābhiprāyēṇāyaṁ
praśnaḥ ? śrūyatām । yēnābhiprāyēṇa, antarā yajatītyantarālakāla-
sambandhastāvatprāpta ēva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b444"/>
<p>kiṁ punararthavādēna kriyatē । yadi hyarthavādādēvāyamarthō labhyatē rātri-
satrapratiṣṭhāvat tadā yuktō'rthavādaḥ । iha punaḥ antarā yajatītyantarāla-
sambandhabhāvāt kimarthavādēnēti manvānasya praśnaḥ । uttaravādī tu jāmitā-
dōṣasaṅkīrtanāt tannirharaṇaprayōjanādapi bhavatyēvārthavattēti pradārśitavān ।
aucityēna stutiruktā । na cāprāptānāmaucityamastīti manvānaḥ
kathaṁ punaḥ viṣṇvādaya iti pr̥ṣṭavān । ayaṣṭavyānvēti na stutau
pramāṇāntarāpēkṣētyuttaravādinō'bhiprāyaḥ । nanu ca nirālagbanataivaṁ prāpnōti
﻿<pb n="b445"/>
mr̥gyatāṁ stutyuttarakālaṁ avalambanaṁ mukhyayā gauṇyā va vr̥ttyā na puna-
rnimittāpēkṣaṁ kāryaṁ kāryatāvagatirbhavatyēva । (yadi bhavati) bhavatu kāryā-
nnimittāvagatiḥ, tathāpi nimittabhāvō vaktavyaḥ । sō'bhidhīyatē । atra
kēcidāhuḥ viṣṇvādayaḥ prāptā ēvēti । kutaḥ ? śākhāntaravidhānāditi ।
sarvaśākhāpratyayamēkaṁ karmēti cōk‍tam । athāpi śākhāntarē prāptirnōpala-
bhyatē । tathāpi yāgasya cōditatvāt dēvatākāṅkṣatvācca tasya
dēvatāviśēṣāpēkṣāyāṁ vākyaśēṣatō'pyavagatirbhavatyēva । kataṁ punarvā-
﻿<pb n="b446"/>
kyaśēṣabalēna dēvatōpatiṣṭhatē ? ucyatē । upāṁśuyājavākyē upāṁśutvaṁ kīrtya-
mānaṁ tāvat taddharmatvēna svīkriyatē । anyathā hi tatpākṣikaṁ syāt nityavacca
tadanūdyatē । tatra yau pramāṇāntarēṇōpāṁśuyājadharmāṇau viṣṇuprajāpatī pratītau
tāvēva buddhisthau svadharmadarśanādbhavadaḥ iti tayōrēvānvitābhidhānānupravēśa
iti । nanu yatkiñcitprājāpatyamiti vākyaśēṣōpanyāsō na yuktaḥ, upāṁśu-
tvasamānyaṁ cōpanyasya viṣṇōrmantrābhidhānamapyatiricyatē । ucyatē । naivē-
daṁ pūrvōk‍tasya pramāṇāntaratayōpanyasyatē dvayamapi, kintu tasyaiva dāḍharyārthaṁ
﻿<pb n="b447"/>
viṣṇōrmantraviśēṣāmnānamēvamupapadyatē । prajāpatēśca vākyāntarē vīpsā ।
ag‍nīṣōmīyayōstu vidhāyakaṁ udāhriyata ēva । <quote>‘tāvabratāmagnīṣōmāvājyarayaiva
nāvupāṁśu paurṇamāsyāṁ yajam’</quote> iti । kimidamagnīṣōmayōrvidhāyakaṁ iti ?
kiṁ jātam ? idamēva jātam viṣṇvādēraprāptiḥ । aprāptaviśēṣaṁ hi
vākyamarthavādādviśēṣaṁ labhatē vihitaviśēṣaṁ punarnirākāṅkṣatvāt na sambadhyatē ।
ēvaṁ tarhi agnīṣōmīyayōstu kathaṁ ? yasmādvidhāyakē vākyē udāhriyētē
tāvabratāmiti । kasya vidhāyakē ? paurṇamāsyāṁ yajanniti kālasya ।﻿<pb n="b448"/>
yaduk‍tamarūpatvāditi parihr̥taṁ tat vacanāntaravihitatvādrūpasyēti । tadidaṁ
pradarśyatē bhāṣyakārēṇa paurṇamāsyāṁ yajannityēvamādinā । kimidaṁ
agrayaprāyē likhitamiti ? idamidaṁ pradhānaprāyē darśanamupāṁśuyājasyētyarthaḥ ।
nanu cānuvādapakṣē'pi prādhānyaṁ kēna vāryatē paurṇamāsyāṁ yajanniti kālayōgāt ।﻿<pb n="b449"/>
athāyamabhiprāyaḥ ag‍nīṣōmāvityarthavādadarśanāt tasyaiva kālayōga
iti । tadayuktam । agr̥hyamāṇaviśēṣatvātkālasya upāṁśuyāja-
mityarthavādasya ca daṇḍinyāyādērapyupapattēḥ agrayaśabdasya caikēnā-
pyupapannatvāt । varṇyatē tarhyayamabhiprāyaḥ viṣṇurupāṁśu yaṣṭavya ityētasmin
vidhānē guṇabhūtasya ca yajēḥ vidhiḥ; tataśca nādhikārayōgyatā karmaṇaḥ ।
ak‍taṁ na saṁskārā adhikāramarhantīti । ataścāgrayaprāyē darśanaṁ nōpapadyata
iti । antarā yajatīti punarbhāvārthasya prādhānyāvagatēḥ adhikārayōgyaprāya-
(agraya)darśanamupapannaṁ bhavati । tasmānnānuvādō'yam । kintarhi ? vidhiḥ
ēvaṁ caturdaśapaurṇamāsyāmāhutayō hūyanta iti iti sustham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b450"/>
<p><q>āghārāgnihōtramarūpatvāt ।</q> uktaṁ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdāḥ
niyōgasya viṣayatāṁ pratipadyanta iti । yatrēdānīṁ guṇavidhayaḥ tatra kathaṁ
bhāvārthatvaṁ ? tasmāt sarvatrākhyātārthavidhānaṁ prāptaṁ dadhnā juhōtītyēva-
mādipu । yadyēvaṁ kathaṁ tadā agnihōtraṁ juhōtīti samudāyānuvādāśaṅkā ।
sarvatra hi dhātvarthavidhānam । aviśēṣāc‍ca karmabhēda iti । atrōcyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b451"/>
dadh‍nā juhōtīti guṇavati (guṇa)śabdō vartatē । tataḥ kim ? idaṁ
tatō bhavati । guṇavadvidhānaṁ prāptaṁ dadh‍nā juhōtītyēvamādiṣu । guṇava-
dvidhānē hi aparityaktabhāvārtha ēva vidhiḥ । ēvaṁ ca sati śakyatē-
'gnihōtraṁ juhōti iti punaḥ śrutirvak‍tuṁ dadh‍nā juhōtītyēvamādīnāṁ nirguṇa-
tvādagnihōtrapadārthasya । nanu ca guṇavacanatā vidyatē'gnihōtrapadasya ।
satyaṁ vidyatē । na juhōtītyasya sakalēnāgnihōtrapadēnāyaṁ tadvān pratīyatē ।
matvarthaścāyamagnihōtrapadārthaḥ । atō na matvarthēna tadvān pratipat‍tuṁ śakyatē ।
ata ēva śabdavidbhiruditaṁ na matubantānmatubutpadyata iti । tasmānnaṣṭāvayavaṁ
﻿<pb n="b452"/>
nāmaivaitat vaiśvadēvaśabdavat । ataḥ samudāyānuvādaḥ agnihōtraṁ juhō-
tīti । nanu ca guṇavān vihitō na guṇaḥ abhāvārthatvāt guṇasya ।
mābhūd‍guṇavidhānam tadviśipṭatā nāpanhōtuṁ śakyatē viśiṣṭasaṁpattyarthama&mdash;
bhāvārthasyāpyupādānaṁ na viruddhayatē । yasya punaḥ agnihōtraṁ juhōtīti
vidhiḥ tasya dadh‍nā juhōtīti vihitasyaiva guṇavattā pratīyatē । tataśca
guṇamātrāvaśēṣādavidhāyakānyētāni vākyāni bhavanti guṇavataśca kēvalasya
vihitatvāt । upādānamapi guṇānāṁ na siddhayati guṇavatpratītirhi
vidhiśūnyaiva tadā । atha guṇavidhānamapyāśrīyatē bhāvārthēbhyaḥ kriyā
pratīyata iti viruddhaṁ nāmanāmivyavahārōcchēdaśca । bhavatviti cēt ।
﻿<pb n="b453"/>
nākarmaṇi niyōgaḥ śakyēta'vagantum । tasmān‍nyāyyaṁ vacanaṁ bhāvārthēbhyaḥ
kriyā pratīyatē iti । nyāyyaṁ cābhyupagamēna na śakyatē bādhitum ।
atō dadh‍nā juhōtītyēva vidhānamabhyupagantuṁ yuktam । upādānēnāpi tāvat
guṇaśrutērarthavattā bhavatviti । vihitēṣu guṇavatsu nirguṇā punaḥ śrutiḥ ।
kathaṁ punarguṇavatsu nirguṇā punaḥ śrutiḥ ? bhāvārthamātraparyavasāyī vidhirityu-
ktam । tasmādvidhēyatvēna punaḥ śrutiḥ vidhyapēkṣaścāyamanuvādō nābhidhānā-
pēkṣaḥ । nanu ca nāviniyuktamupādīyatē । kēna cōk‍taṁ na vini-
yuktō guṇa iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b454"/>
<p>anabhijñō bhavān । ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati&mdash;nāviniyuktaṁ vidhīyatē
nāvihitamupādīyata iti। vidhyartha ēva hi viniyōgō na
viśēṣaṇārthaḥ tadvattā ca viśēṣaṇaviśēṣyatāmādāyēti naidamarthyam ।
nanu gōmāniti gavāṁ gōmadarthatā pratīyatē । naivam । śarāvatyādiṣva-
darśanāt । tasmād‌gōmati pramāṇāntaratastādarthyaṁ mr̥gyam । ṣaṣṭhayā
tādarthyamiti cēnna mātr̥māt pitr̥mānityanaikāntyāt । ucyatē ।
aviniyuk‍tēpi śēṣatā nāsti । asati ca śēṣatvē aidamarthyaṁ mābhūta ।
﻿<pb n="b455"/>
upādānaṁ punaḥ vi(śiṣṭā)śēṣaṇatvāvagamapūrvakamēva yathā paś‍vēkatvasya paśunā
yajētēti ।</p>
<p>nanu ca tadēkatvaṁ viniyuktapaśuviśaṣaṇam । ata upādīyatē
viniyuktasyōpādēyatvāt । dadhyādēstu kathamupādānam ? dadhyādyapi
viniyuktaviśēṣaṇamēva । karmaṇō viniyuktatvāt phalē । ēvaṁ tarhi
upādānaśēṣaṁ dadhyādi । bhavatu na kaściddōṣaḥ । yathaiva hi dravya-
saṅkhyāliṅgaśūnyaṁ viniyuktamapi nōpādātuṁ śakyata ityēkatvādayaḥ
upādīyantē । ēvaṁ karmāpi na kārakaviśēṣaśūnyamastīti dadhyād‌yu-
pādānasiddhiḥ । yadyēvaṁ kimiti tarhyanyōpādānē vaiguṇyāśaṅkā ? upādānē
śēṣamapi śēṣamēvētyadōṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu cāsmin pakṣē paśvādīnāmapi naiva vidhānam । ōmityucyatē
﻿<pb n="b456"/>
kathaṁ tarhi paś‍vēkatvamivēti pradarśitam । abhyupagamyaitatpradarśitam ।
yathā satyapi guṇavidhāvaviniyuk‍tasyaiva paś‍vēkatvasyōpādānaṁ tadvaddadhyādēriti ।
tadēvēdamāpatitaṁ ghōṭārūḍhasya vismr̥tō ghōṭa iti । vidhēścāviṣayā guṇāḥ
vidhinā cōpādīyanta ita ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē । mugdhaḥ khalvasi kāryōpādānaviśēṣajñānē । yatra
niyuṅk‍tē tatkāryam । tatsiddhayē yadupādīyatē tadupādānam । viniyōgē
cāviṣayatā nāmārthasyōk‍tā । na punarakārakatāpi । nanu cōpādānamapi
vidhērvyāpāra iti ēva vyāpāratvācca kimiti niyōgaviṣayatāṁ na pratipadyatē ।
﻿<pb n="b457"/>
anubandhāvaskandāt । anyathā hi bhēdābhēdau śāstrasya durbhaṇau
syātām । tasmādviśēṣāvagatirēva viśēṣasyōpādānamākṣipati na
punarniyōgastamāskandati dravyōpādānamiva । tasmādidamēva nyāyyaṁ dadhnā
juhōtīti vidhiḥ agnihōtraṁ juhōtīti samudāyānuvādaḥ । saṁjñōpabandhāditi
kimabhyadhikamucyatē । idamabhyadhikam । prakr̥tēbhyaḥ saṁjñātō'nyatvaṁ
pratīyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । saṁjñāhi śrūyamāṇaiva prakr̥tēbhyō'nyatvamāpādayati
athaiṣa jyōtirityēvamādiṣu darśanāt । satyamēvaṁ viśēṣāvagatau satyām ।
jyōtirādiṣu tu sahasradakṣiṇādiviśiṣṭāḥ karmaviśēṣā avagamyantē tathēha
viśēṣāvagatiḥ । nanu vijñāyata ēvātrājyāghārahōmau kriyāntarēbhyō viśiṣṭau ।
﻿<pb n="b458"/>
yadyēvaṁ lōkata ēva tarhi vijñātau kimatra vidhiḥ kariṣyatīti
guṇaphalōpabandhēṣu saṁjñā niṣprayōjanaiva । atha viśiṣṭasya saṁjñā vāci-
kētyucyatē । uk‍taṁ tarhi prakr̥tēbhyō na viśēṣāntaramava़gamyata iti ।
api ca kriyāvidhānapakṣē guṇakarmavidhānaṁ prāpnōti dvitīyāntatvānnāmnaḥ ।
ataśca nāmadhēyānupapattiḥ । anuvādapakṣē punaḥ vihitapracayāvagamyatvāt
samudāyasya bhavatyavagatau samudāyaḥ sādhyaḥ । ataśca nāmadhēyē'pyavirōdhaḥ ।
agnihōtrapadamapi samudāyasya vācakaṁ prāpnōti । nēti brūmaḥ । dhātuvadēva
tantrēṇa samudāyināmēva vācakam dvitīyaikatvayōstu gamyamānapracayaviṣaya-
tayā parihārō'yamaprakr̥tatvāccēti kō'yaṁ kūṣmāṇḍaḥ । pratyutāprakr̥tatvāt 
dravyadēvatasya vidhānaṁ prāpnōti aviśēṣādityucyatē । na santatādibhyaḥ
kaścidanyō viśēṣō'vagamyatē āghārē yēna viśēṣāntaraniṣṭhāghārasaṁjñā syāt
tasyāḥ santatādiniṣṭhaivēyaṁ saṁjñā । tataścānuvādaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b459"/>
<p><q>saṁjñōpabandhāditi ।</q> paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇē'pyākṣēpaparihārau
draṣṭavyau । <q>cōdanā vā śavdārthasya । na</q> samudāyānuvādau agnihōtraṁ juhōti
﻿<pb n="b460"/>
āghāramāghārayatīti । kutaḥ ? prakr̥tānāṁ karmaṇāmabhāvāt । kathamabhāvaḥ
guṇavidhānāvagatēḥ dadhnā juhōtītyēvamādiṣu । nanu ca  nākarmaṇi guṇō
vidhātuṁ śakyatē । satyam । idamēva karma bhaviṣyati agnihōtraṁ juhōtīti
sāmānyāvagatēḥ । viśēṣaniṣṭhatvāt saṁjñāyā na vidhānaṁ sambhavati ।
vidhēyatvādēva viśēṣō lakṣyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । labdhē ca viśēṣē guṇayōga-
pravr̥ttyā nāmadhēyatvasiddhiḥ । kathaṁ punarabhāvārthatvāt guṇavidhiḥ ।
bhāvārtha ēva hi tarhi śābdō vidhīyatē । nanu ca dr̥ṣṭaṁ kathaṁ bhāvasya
viśēṣaṇam ? kimiti vā na viśēṣaṇam । akriyārūpatvāt dravyasya 
naivātra rūparūpitayā viśēṣaṇam । kathaṁ tarhi ? anubandhatayaiva ।
ēvamapyanubandhō vidhiviṣayō nā[na]nubandhaḥ । tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tatō
bhavati yatpūrvōk‍taṁ viśiṣṭasyāvihitatvāt viśēṣaṇaṁ upādānaśēṣaṁ bhavati na
﻿<pb n="b461"/>
vidhēyamityucyatē । yathaiva hi viniyōjya(tayā)sthatvāt aviniyōjya-
mupādēyaṁ, ēvamēva hi vidhēyamapi bhavatīti । idamayuktam । yuktō hi
viniyōgaḥ । aidamarthyāvagatirhi siddhasādhyatāṁ nāpēkṣatē । niyōgastu
kāryāvagatipūrvaka ēva । tasmādupādānamātramēva dadhyādēḥ śakyatē
vak‍tum । na punarvidhēyatā । nanu cāvidhēyatvē sādhanāntaranirākaraṇaṁ na
prāpnōti । anivāritē ca tasmin dadhyādipadamanarthakaṁ syāt ।
﻿<pb n="b462"/>
kiṁkriyatām ? sasyārthō nāsti kimanyata ānarthakyādityuk‍tam । kastarhi
parihāraḥ ? <q>sūtrakāraṁ pr̥ccha । yēna bhāvārthēbhyaḥ kriyā</q> pratīyata
ityuk‍tam । atrābhidhīyatē । bhāvārtha ēvātrāpi vidhīyatē dadhnā
juhōtīti । iyāṁstu viśēṣaḥ । dhātvarthānubandhāvacchinnaḥ ।
kārakamapi hi kriyāvacchē(dakamēva)dēnaiva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b463"/>
kārakavyāpārāvacchē(dakā)da ēva dhātavaḥ pravartantē । tadapi avibhāgataḥ
kārakaviśēṣaśravaṇē sa ēva vibhāgēnāvagamyatē । tataḥ kiṁ ? vibhāga-
śravaṇē hi vibhak‍tasyaiva vidhēyatā avagamyatē । na punaravibhak‍tasya
dhātvarthasya । tasmādyatra dhātvarthāvagati(tēḥ)statra dhātvarthavidhānam ।
tatsannidhau vibhāgāvagatēḥ vibhāgamātravidhānam । ataḥ siddhaṁ tatsannidhēḥ
guṇārthēna punaḥ śrutiriti । juhōtēruccāraṇamanuvādaḥ guṇasambandhārthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b464"/>
<p><q>yadi juhōtītyanuvādaḥ kēnēdānīṁ guṇō vidhīyata iti ?</q>
kō'yaṁ praśnaḥ । nanu ca vidhidvayamapyabhyupagatamēva agnihōtraṁ juhōtīti
dadhnā juhōtīti ca । tadēvēdaṁ nōpapadyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । kathamanupapattiḥ ?
ēkaivēyaṁ kartavyatā'vibhak‍tā । vibhaktau tvanubandhau । na cānubandhō dadhyādiḥ
vidhēyaḥ । kiṁ tarhi anubandhaḥ । ēkatvācca vidhidvayasyāviṣayaḥ ।
tasmādēkaṁ vākyaṁ vidhiśūnyam । tacca āśritatvāt guṇasaṁbandhyēvēti ।
punarapyavivakṣaiva guṇānubandhasya vākyārthō yaḥ taṁ vidhātumityanubandha-
vistārāt bhāvavistāra ityuk‍tam । tasmādviniyōga ēva
﻿<pb n="b465"/>
vidhērapi viṣayōpapattiḥ । <q>yaduktaṁ nāstyāghārasya prakr̥tadravyadēvatamiti
kimēvaṁ sati dravyadēvatēnēti ।</q> vidhāyakādēva (vi)śēṣāvagatirityu-
k‍tam । na ca nāsti vacanāntaravihitaṁ astyēvēti siddhaṁ nānuvādā&mdash;
viti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b466"/>
<p><q>dravyasaṁyōgāccōdanā paśusōmayōḥ ।</q> kiṁ punaḥ pūrvādhikaraṇēnāsya
vaiṣamyam । idamasti vaiṣamyam&mdash;rasahr̥dayādibhyō dravyāntaraṁ paśusōmau ।
ēvaṁ tarhi pūrvapakṣa ēva nāsti । na ca nāsti, kramasamuccayau hi pūrvapakṣahētubhūtau
﻿<pb n="b467"/>
ēkārthatvādavadānadēvatā vikalpyanta iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē । na
cātyantāsaṁbaddhamēvēdaṁ hr̥dayādibhyaḥ paśutvam । na ca sōmādrasaḥ
tasmādanuvādō nyāyya iti manyatē । kathaṁ punaḥ aindravāyavaṁ gr̥hṇātīti
hr̥dayasyāgnē'vadyatīti yāgacōdanā । grahaṇē tāvat dravyadēvatāsaṁyōgāt
nirvapativat gr̥hṇātirbhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b468"/>
avadyatau tu kathaṁ ? atrāpi yāgagatasaṁskāradarśanāt phalacamasa&mdash;
vat karmacōdanā bhaviṣyatītyamiprāyaḥ । yuk‍taṁ phalacamasē nirjñātayāgaśē-
﻿<pb n="b469"/>
ṣasya, avadyatau punarmr̥gyō'sau । saṁskārāditi cēnna ; vatsamāla-
bhētētyanaikāntyāt । nanu cāprayōjanavataḥ saṁskārō na bhaviṣyatīti
yuk‍taiva karmakalpanā । varaṁ tr̥tīyārthē ṣaṣṭhī na punaḥ karmakalpanā ।
﻿<pb n="b470"/>
kēyamanupāsitagurōḥ svapratibhāvataḥ ṣaṣṭhīkalpanā । bhavantu saṁskārā
avadyaticōdanāḥ agnīṣōmasaṁbandhāttu yāvatsaṁskāraṁ yāgacōdanāḥ
saṁpadyantē । tataśca pracayānuvādaḥ ālabhatiriti siddham । tataśca
kramasamuccayadarśanamupapannārthaṁ bhavati । nacānuvādē lakṣaṇādōṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b471"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē । naitacchabdādavagantu śakyatē । sōmēna yajētēti
sōmalatāviśiṣṭō yajirgamyatē । rasadravyakāśca gr̥hṇātayaḥ । (arthāt)
atō rūpāntarāvagamānnānuvādaḥ śakyatē'vagantum । anuvādē sati lakṣaṇā
tataścānuvāda itītarētarāśrayaḥ । karmāntarē punaḥ svatō'rthāntarāvagamā-
n‍nyāyyam । ēṁva(vai)paśāvapi । paśuśabdō hi pucchavati vartatē ।
hr̥dayādayastu māṁsasaṁsthānavacanāḥ । tasmānnānuvādaḥ saṁbhavati ।
kramasamuccayadarśanaṁ ca grahaṇādīnāṁ karmāntaratvē'pi naiva viruddham ।
﻿<pb n="b472"/>
kintu sōmēna yajēna paśumālabhēta iti yadainē karmacōdanē tadā'vadyati-
gr̥hṇātyōḥ saṁskārakarmataivāvasīyatē । kasmāt ? tadā hi gr̥hyamāṇa-
pradhānō gr̥hṇātiḥ[na] gr̥hyamāṇaguṇā śakyatē kalpayitum । nāpi
nirvapativat yāgavidhānārthaṁ prāptānuvādaḥ śakyatē vak‍tum । nanu ca
dravyadēvatāsaṁbandhāt na gr̥hṇātimātraparyavasāyinī cōdanā śakyatē
vak‍tum sauryaṁ caruṁ nirvapēditivat । na ca sōmēna yajētēti dēvatā prāptā
yā'nūdyēta saṁskāraṁ vidhātum ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b473/>
na ca saṁskārē dēvatā kārakabhāvaṁ pratipadyatē yāgasyaiva hi kārakaṁ dēvatā
na grahaṇādēḥ । atō'prāptadravyadēvatāsaṁyōgāt karmāntarāṇyēvaitāni ।
na sōmēna yajētētyatra saṁskāra iti śakyatē vak‍tuṁ sauryaṁ caruṁ
nirvapēditivat ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b474"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē-kutaścidupādānaṁ grahaṇamityucyatē । upādānañcātmārthaṁ
vā syāt parārthaṁ vā । tatra dēvatāśravaṇāt dēvatārthamiti gamyatē । nanu
na jātitaḥ kācit dēvatā nāma vidyatē । yā hi yasya haviṣaḥ saṁba&mdash;
ndhitvēna cōdyatē sā tasya dēvatēti । na ca sōmarasasyēndravāyvādayaḥ
prāptaḥ yēna tadarthamupādānamityavadhāryatē । athātraiva rasasya dēvatā cōdyatē
na tarhi grahaṇacōdanā kintu dēvatāvidhiparamēvaitadvākyaṁ syāt ।
tadā ca kramasamuccayadarśanaṁ nōpapadyatē । gr̥hṇātiśca pramādapāṭhaḥ
kriyānuvādō vā syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b475"/>
<p>tasmāt dēvatāviśiṣṭaṁ grahaṇaṁ cōdyata iti durbhaṇamidam । na
brūmō dēvatāviśiṣṭaṁ grahaṇaṁ cōdyata iti । ki tarhi ? indra-
vāyūddēśaviśiṣṭaṁ grahaṇaṁ rasasya । tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tatō
bhavati । yāgaśēṣatvād‌dravyasya indravāyvarthatvācca grahaṇasya gr̥hyamāṇa-
mukhaṁ ca tādarthyaṁ grahaṇasya । ata indravāyvarthō rasa iti gamyatē ।
nēndravāyū rasārthau yāvad‍grahaṇaṁ ca tādarthyaṁ na yāvadyāga&mdash;
bhāvi । ata ēva ca na yāgē cōdanā grahaṇēṣu dēvatātvaṁ ca
yāgārtharasatādarthyāt । na punaḥ cōdanātaḥ nātrēndravāyvādayō
﻿<pb n="b476"/>
dēvatātvēna cōdyantē । ata kāryatastatra dēvatātvaṁ nōpadēśataḥ ।
upadēśō hi grahaṇasyēndravāyvarthatāparyavasāyyēva । tasmādupapannāḥ
saṁskāracōdanāgrahaṇādayaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>tadbhēdāt karmaṇō'bhyāsaḥ ।</q> ēvaṁ ca kr̥tvā kramasamuccayōpapattiḥ ।
uk‍taṁ ca yāvad‍grahaṇabhāvīndravāyvādīnāṁ saṁbandhō na yāvadyāgabhāvīti ।
﻿<pb n="b477"/>
yāgaśēṣaścāsau sakalō daśamuṣṭiprabhavō rasaḥ । atō'yāgārthatvā-
dindravāyvōḥ sakalasya ca sōmarasasya yāgārthatvāt yāvad‍grahaṇa-
bhāvitvācca saṁbandhasya indravāyvādēravaśyamāvr̥ttyā bhavitavyam । satyāṁ
cāvr̥ttau siddhaḥ samuccayaḥ । na ca sarvasyaiva sōmarasasya
anyasyānyasya cōhēśēna grahaṇaṁ bhavati। tasmādavayavaśō grahaṇam ।
tathā ca pātraparimāṇadarśanam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b478"/>
<p>na ca vibhāgēna grahaṇaṁ punarēkī karaṇam । na ca dr̥ṣṭē saṁbhavati
adr̥ṣṭārthatā uddēśasya saṁbhavati । adr̥ṣṭārthasya vā grahaṇādēḥ(gr̥hṇātēḥ)dr̥ṣṭārthatā
tasmādavayavānāmēva dēvatōddēśēna tyāgaḥ । na caitāvatā karmabhēdō
bhavati । sōmēna yajētētyabhinnāvagatēḥ । tasmāt sa ēva punaḥ
punarāvartata iti siddham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b479"/>
<p><q>saṁskārastu na bhidyēta ।</q> khadirādiṣu punaḥ saṁskāraśēṣabhāvā-
vagamāt yuk‍tō vikalpaḥ ।</p>
<p><note n="(1)"> Page 473.</note>athaindravāyavādiṣu prakr̥tēṣu yāgēṣu latā vidhīyata ityucyatē, na
sā śakyā vākyēnaindravāyavī vijñātum śrutyā hi rasaḥ aindravāyava iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b480"/>
nanu cēdamayuktam । prakr̥tidravyatayā hi latāvidhānamanirastaṁ syāt ।
rasakāryavidhānaṁ cāsaṁbhavadēvāśāṅkitam । tasmāt vrīhibhiryajētētivat
dravyaprakr̥tidravyatayā latāvidhānamupapadyata ēva sōmēna yajētēti ।</p>
<p>kiṁ nāma nāśaṅkayatē mūḍhamatibhiḥ purōḍāśō hyanirūpitaprakr̥ti-
dravyaka āg‍nēyādiṣu pratīyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b481"/>
<p>tēna yuk‍taṁ tatra prakr̥tiviśēṣavidhānam । iha punaraindravāya-
vādiṣu sōmarasa ēvāvasīyatē । kimatra prakr̥tidravyavidhānaṁ karipyati ।
tasmādanāśaṅkanīya ēvāyaṁ pakṣaḥ । havirviśēṣaśaṅkā nōpapadyata ēvēti nirastā
bhāṣyakārēṇa ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b482"/>
<p><q>pr̥thak‌tvanivēśitvāt saṅkhayayā karmabhēdaḥ syāt ।</q> prājā-
patyāniti prājāpatyaprātipadikāt vibhaktaya utpadyantē । yataścōtpadyantē
tad‌yuk‍taṁ svārthamabhivadanti । taddhitāntaṁ caitat prātipadikam । tataḥ
taddhitāntasyaiva idaṁ bahutvaṁ na kēvalasya taddhitārthasya । ataḥ saṁśaya
﻿<pb n="b483"/>
ēvātra nōpapadyatē । prājāpatyāḥ saptadaśētyēvāvagamyatē na punaḥ
saptadaśaprājāpatyā iti । atō vikalpavilasita ēvātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ucyatē । pratyayārthagatamēvātra vibhak‍tayaḥ svārthaṁ pratipādayituṁ
kṣamāḥ na prakr̥tyarthagataṁ, kutaḥ ? prakr̥tyarthasya pratyayārthōpasarjanatvāt । pradhānaṁ
hi arthāntarēṇa saṁbadhyatē, nōpasarjanam । nanu caivamapi sandēhō
nōpapadyatē । upasarjanārthasya bhēdānavagamāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b484"/>
<p>satyamēvamētat । pradhānārtha ēvātra kiṁ bhinnaḥ san upasarjanēna
yuktaḥ uta sōpasarjanō bhinna iti । ēvaṁ saṁśayē sati pūrvapakṣavādī
manyatē bhinnasyōpasarjanayōgō yuktaḥ prakr̥tyarthasya bhēdāvagamē pramāṇā&mdash;
bhāvāt । bahutvāvagamapūrvikā hyēkaśēṣakalpanā । ataḥ pratyayārthasyai-
vaikaśēṣō bhavatu । tadbhēdāvagamāt । na punarabhinnasyāpi prakr̥tyarthasya ।
tasmādubhayasiddhamēkayāgāvadhāraṇamēva yuktam । tadidamuktam&mdash;<q>yō hi
bahūn yāgān kalpayati kalpayatyasāvēkamiti ।</q> kathaṁ panarasmin pakṣē
anēkasmādēkādaśāvadānasiddhiḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b485"/>
<p>arthādāvr̥ttirbhaviṣyati । grahaṇabhēdājjyōtiṣṭōmasyēva । atrō-
cyatē । na saptadaśabhirēkaṁ karmōpapadyatē । kutaḥ ? ēkādaśabhiravadānaiḥ
paśuyāgaḥ siddhayati । sa caikādaśāvadānagaṇaḥ ēkasmādēva paśōḥ
siddhayatīti na paśvantaraṁ dēvatayā saṁbandhayituṁ śakyatē । tataśca
prājāpatyāniti bahutvānupapattiḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b486"/>
<p>nanu cōk‍taṁ pratipaśvavadānagaṇasya āvr̥ttiḥ saptadaśānāṁ yāga-
saṁbandhārthaṁ gr̥hṇātīnāmiva jyōtiṣṭōmasya । yuktam jyōtiṣṭōmē gr̥hṇātīnā-
mupadēśāt । atra punaḥ kāryatō'vadānagaṇaḥ prāpnōti । sa ca
yāgasya saptadaśapaśudravyakō'yamēkō yāgaḥ । yāgasaṁbandhācca haviṣyava-
dānam । ataḥ kēnātra pratipaśvavadānagaṇaprāptiḥ haviṣṭvēnaikatvāt
paśūnām । havirbhēdē hi sati havissaṁskārabhēdē vā pradhānasyā-
vr̥ttirbhavati iha tad‍dvayaṁ nāsti । nātra saṁskāranibandhanaṁ pr̥thaktvam ।
﻿<pb n="b487"/>
havirnibandhanō haviḥ saṁskārabhēdaḥ । tasmādyāgaikatvapakṣē saptadaśasaṅkhayā&mdash;
nvayō na ghaṭatē । kimidamanyāyyamuktam । yāganirūpaṇōttarakālaṁ
hi saṁskāraprāptiḥ na saṁskārāpēkṣaṁ yāganirūpaṇam । saptadaśapasūdravyaścāya-
mēkō yāgō nirūpitaḥ ēvaṁbhūtasya saṁskārō yadi āvr̥ttyā anāvr̥ttyā vā na
saṁbhavati bādhyatāṁ nāma kr̥ṣṇalacarāvi(dam)vāvaghātaḥ। na punastadvaśā-
﻿<pb n="b488"/>
dutpattau vākyārthaḥ śakyatē nirūpayitum । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ । kiṁ
sōpasarjanasya bhēdaḥ utābhinnasyōpasarjanayōgaḥ ityasmin
saṁśayē vākyaśēṣād‍yuk‍tō nirṇaya iti । kasmādvākyaśēṣāt ?
prakr̥tivaditi । nāyaṁ vākyaśēṣaḥ । kāryataḥ prāptimaṅgānāṁ
darśayituṁ vākyaśēṣō'yaṁ vyākhyātdr̥ṇām । na punarupadēśē'ṅgānāṁ
﻿<pb n="b489"/>
na ca kāryata upadēśanirūpaṇam । upadēśāddhi kāryaṁ nirūpyatē ।
na cātra saṁśayō vidyatē । uktaṁ bhēdāvagamapūrvakaṁ ēkaśēṣavacanam । pradhānasya
ca vibhaktiyōgāt bhēdō'vagamyatē nōpasarjanasyēti । tasmāt pūrvapakṣa
ēvātra jyāyāniti ēkaśēṣavidō manyantē ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē । satyaṁ pratyayārthasya bhēdō'vagamyatē na punarupa-
sarjanarahitasya । kutaḥ ? prakr̥tipratyaryasamudāyādvibhaktyutpattēḥ ।
na vibhaktitaḥ pratyayōtpādaḥ । tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tataḥ । prakr̥ti&mdash;
yuktaṁ hi vibhaktyarthēna yujyatē na vibhaktyarthayuk‍taṁ prakr̥tyā ।
﻿<pb n="b490"/>
tasmāt saptadaśa yāgāḥ pratīyantē, na saptadaśadravyakō yāgaḥ । ataḥ
karmagataiṣā saṅkhayā, na dravyagatā । ēvaṁ ca sati naivēyaṁ karmāṇi vidhīyatē
yēnāruṇavat dravyamukhēnōpakāritā syāt । ataḥ siddhaṁ pr̥thaktvanivēśitvāt
saṅkhayayā karmabhēda iti । taccaikapaśūnāṁ pr̥thaktvaṁ bahuṣu yāgēṣu avakalpatē
naikasminniti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b491"/>
kaḥ punaratra hēturabhiprētō bhāṣyakārasya ? nanu caikādaśāvadānānu-
papattiḥ । ahēturayaṁ na kāryataḥ śāstrāvadhāraṇamiti । ucyatē । naiva
kāryēṇa śāstramavadhāryatē । śās‍trēṇaivēdaṁ kāryamavadhr̥tam । uk‍taṁ hi sōpa-
sarjanasya bhēdō'vagamyata iti । ēvaṁ sati ēkādaśāvadānabōdhō na śakyatē
vak‍tum । ēkasmāccāsau niṣpannaḥ । kutaḥ ? sōpasarjanaḥ pratyayārthaḥ
dvitīyādērupasarjanasaṁbandhānupapattiḥ । ataśca saptadaśasaṅkṣayā paśuṣu
na syāt । upasarjanārthāvacchēdō hi saṅkhayānivēśē hētuḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b492"/>
tadanupapattau saṅkhayānivēśānupapattiḥ । na cānyaḥ kaścit avacchēdakō
vidyatē ēkarūpaśravaṇāt । nānārūpaśravaṇē hi tēṣāmanyatam iti
syādapi saṅkhayānivēśaḥ । na tadasti । tasmāt paśuṣūpapadyatē nānyathēti
yuk‍tamuktam ।</p>
<p>1<q>nanvēkasminnapi yāgē saptadaśabhiravadānagaṇaiḥ pakṣyatē vaca-
nāditi ।</q> kimidamuktam ? idamuktam । yadyapi sōpasarjanasya
bhēdō'vagamyatē, tathāpi pradhānabhēdādēvōpasarjanasya bhēdō na bhavatu । sābhūt
﻿<pb n="b493"/>
pradhānasyaiva svataḥ kimēvaṁ bhaviṣyati ? idamēva bhaviṣyati । sapta&mdash;
daśasaṅkhayā haviṣō vikārikā bhaviṣyati, na punaryāgasya । bhavatyēvamidaṁ
yadi haviṣaḥ saṅkhayā śrūyatē iyaṁ punaḥ paśuṣu śrūyatē । kō viśēṣaḥ ?
ayamasti viśēṣaḥ । paśūnāmupasarjanayōgāt । tatsaṁbandhāvagatirēva
bhinnā'vagamyatē na havirmātram । atō yāgabhēdaḥ prayōjanamuktam ।</p>
<p><q>saṁjñā cōtpattisaṁyōgāt ।</q> <quote>“athaiva jyōtirathaiṣa viśvajyōtiḥ
athaiṣa sarvajyōtiḥ”</quote> kathaṁ punarēvamādīnāṁ</p>
﻿<pb n="b494"/>
karmavacanatā'vasīyatē । bhāvārthasāmānādhikaraṇyāddhi nāmadhēyatvamuktam ।
na ca tadihāsti । kēvalanāmaśravaṇāt । tasmāt kathamatra
saṁśayaḥ ? kiṁ prakr̥tasya karmaṇō vācakā uta vakṣyamāṇasyēti ।
ucyatē । astyatrāpi sāmānādhikaraṇyaṁ bhāvaśabdēna । ētacchabdāvamarśaḥ
<quote>‘sa ya ēvaṁ vidvānētēna yajēta’</quote> ityēvamādiṣu ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b495"/>
tasmādupapannaḥ saṁśayaḥ । atra pūrvapakṣavādī manyatē&mdash;darśapūrṇamāsavat
prakr̥tānāṁ karmaṇāṁ sākaṁ prasthāyyavadvā prakr̥tasya karmaṇō vācakā iti ।
tasmāttasyaivēdaṁ punarvacanaṁ guṇāntarasaṁbandhārthamityēvaṁ prāptam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b496"/>
<p>atrōcyatē&mdash;saṁjñāpyutpattyaiva arthāntarāvabōdhamutpādayati । kimida-
mutpattyaivēti ? uccāryamāṇaivētyarthaḥ । anyatvaṁ cāvagataṁ viśēṣāntarā-
bhāvāt । punaranyārthatayā na gr̥hyēta sākaṁprasthāyyavat । yatra punarviśē&mdash;
ṣō&mdash;vagamyatē prakr̥tādanyatra kimiti tatrautpattikaṁ bhēdavijñānaṁ kathyatē ।
asti cāyaṁ sahasradakṣiṇādibhiḥ viśēṣaiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ prakr̥tādanyaḥ । tasmāt
karmāntaraṁ saṁjñāta iti siddham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b497"/>
<p><q>guṇaścāpūrvasaṁyōgē ।</q> kathaṁ punaratra saṁśayaḥ ? yadā vaiśvadēvaśabdē-
nāmikṣāsaṁbandhō vājiśabdēna vājinasaṁbandhaḥ । śabdēna ca dēk‍tōpakarōti
iti <quote>‘vidhiśabdasya mantratvē bhāvaḥ syāt’</quote> ityatrōktam । atō'rthaikyē'pi
dēvatāntaramēvaitat । yathā sauryacarāvādityē ca । ucyatē । yatra hi śabdā-
dēva dēvatā'vagamyatē tatraivam, yatra punaḥ prakr̥tōpalakṣaṇaparaḥ śabdādiḥ tatra
﻿<pb n="b498"/>
pūrvaśabdabhidhēyaiva dēvatā । anyābhidhēyatayaiva lakṣaṇā lakṣayati ।
na svābhidhēyatāmāpādayituṁ kṣamā । tasmādupapadyatē saṁśayaḥ kimayaṁ
lakṣaṇayā vājibhya ityayaṁ śabdō'nvēti utābhidhānēnēti । nanu
ca yaugikatvāt vājibhya iti naiva lakṣaṇā śakyatē vak‍tum । sāmīpyē
tadvati vā lakṣaṇā, na punaḥ yāgāvagatau । nimittāntara&mdash;
balēna hi lakṣaṇā'vagamyatē । na padādēva । yōgastu padāvagamya
﻿<pb n="b499"/>
ēva । tasmāllakṣaṇānupapattiḥ । atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;kimatra rūḍhiryōgō vā
kariṣyati ? parābhidhēyatā lakṣaṇāhētuḥ । taccātra vidyata iti pūrvapakṣa-
vādinō'bhiprāyaḥ । vyaktiniṣṭhatvādyaugikānāṁ vaiśvadēvaśabdācca vyakti-
viśēṣāvagamāt । tasmād‌guṇadvayaviśiṣṭamēkaṁ karmēti pūrvapakṣitam ।
siddhāntavādī tu manyatē&mdash;yadyapi prakr̥tavyaktyavagamō bhavati tathāpi
karmāntaramēvaitat । āmikṣōpasarjanatayā pratīyamānatvāt viś‍vēṣāṁ dēvānām ।
﻿<pb n="b500"/>
nahyanyōpasarjanaṁ anyasaṁbandhitayā śakyatē'vagantum ; rājapuruṣaṁ
paśyētivat । tasmādanayōrēkēnāsaṁbandhaḥ । ataḥ saṁbandhadvayā-
vagamādēkatvē'pi saṁbandhinaḥ karmabhēdaḥ । atha kasmād‍yugapat aruṇā-
vatsaṁbandhō na bhavati । kimēvaṁ ? ēkatvēnāvagatirbhaviṣyati । satyamēvaṁ
﻿<pb n="b501"/> 
yatraikapramāṇāvagamyaḥ saṁbandhaḥ । nānāpramāṇagamyē punaḥ anivāryaiva
bhēdāvagatiḥ । tasmāt karmāntaram । nānāpramāṇagamyatā śrutyā
vāk‍yēna cēti vadatā darśitā । iha tarhi kathaṁ pramāṇabhēdē'pi dadhnau juhōti
payasā juhōti ityēkat‍vaṁ karmaṇaḥ ? anupasarjanatvāvagatēḥ । nātra
anyōpasarjanō hōmō'nyēna saṁbadhyata  iti aviruddhā prakr̥tāvagatiḥ ।
atō bhinnānāmapi śāstrāṇāṁ abhinnātmakakāryamiti vaiṣamyam । aprakr̥ta-﻿<pb n="b502"/>
grahaṇaṁ dēvatāntaragrahaṇaṁ ca dēvatāntarasaṁbandhābhiprāyam; na padārthābhiprāyaṁ
padārthābhēdē'pi bhēdāvagamādityuktam । nātra padārthabhēdaḥ śak‍yatē vak‍tum
annayōgādviśvēṣāṁ dēvānām । tasmāt saṁbandhitaivātra bhinnatvē hēturiti
siddham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b503"/> 
<p>adhikaraṇāntaraṁ vēti vadataḥ kō'bhiprāyō bhāṣyakārasya ?
nanu ca guṇārthēna punaḥ śrutirityatra naivaitāni karmāntarāṇatyuktam ।
atra vadāmaḥ, ayamabhiprāyō bhāṣyakārasya । atrāpi dadhyupasarjana-
tayā'vagamyatē । atō'nubandhāntarasaṁbandhāt naikāvagamyamanubanghaṁ
bhavati । tasmāt pradhānasyāp‍yupasarjanasyēvānyasaṁbandhasya nānyēna saṁbandha
upapadyatē । rāddhāntastu&mdash;satmēvaṁ yadyasaṁbaddhasya samarpakaṁ nāsti
vaiśvadēvavat, iha cāgnihōtraṁ juhōtīti sarvānubandhasaṁbandhitayā﻿<pb n="b504"/> 
asaṁbandhamēvānubandhāntaramavagamyata iti vaiṣamyam । vikalpōpanyāsastu
phalapradarśanaṁ bhēdāvagamasiddhayartham । uk‍tēna nyāyēna na bhēdaḥ
siddhayatīti vikalpasiddhiḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b505"/> ﻿<pb n="b506"/>
<p><q>phalaśrutēstu karma syāt ।</q> atha kimarthamidamanumānamupanyastam ?
punaśca vikal‍pasamādyā jātayaḥ । asiddhānaikāntikaviruddhābhidhānasyāna-
vasara ēva । bhēdābhēdaparīkṣaṇaṁ hyatra prakr̥tam । tacca śabdānta-
rādisamadhigamyam । kimatrānumānēna kriyatē tad‍dūṣaṇēna vā ।</p>﻿<pb n="b507"/> 
tasmādasaṁbaddhamēvēdaṁ granthakhaṇḍalakaṁ karmabhēdābhēdavidō manyantē । atō
yadēva vāk‍yabhēdabhayāt karmāntaratvamuk‍taṁ vaktavyaṁ pūrvapakṣē ।
na punaḥ pramāṇāntaramupanyasanīyam । atrōcyatē&mdash;nanu na śrutaṁ
bhavatā śāstrabhēdapratipattiranēna lakṣaṇēna kriyata iti । na ca śāstrā-
cchāstrabhēdō'vagamyatē । kiṁ tarhi ? anubandhānyatvāvagamya ēva । tasya
cānyatvaṁ pramāṇāntarāvagamyamēva । taccēdaṁ dadhnā'nubandhaṁ karma na
karmaśāstraṁ bhinattītyuktam । karmavattayā cākarmaṇi vidhānamuktam ।﻿<pb n="b508"/>
ēvaṁ cēt phalānubandhē'pi karmāpannamēva guṇarūpaṁ na svataḥ phalēna
saṁbandhayituṁ śak‍yatē । ataḥ karmaṇā phalasaṁbandhāt karmāntaramidaṁ
phalāntarānubandhāditi pūrvapakṣī manyatē ।</p>﻿<pb n="b509"/>
ēvamap‍yanumānabhāṣyaṁ kathaṁ ? it‍thamidaṁ idamanumānabhāṣyam । kiṁ
kāryataḥ karmāpattiṁ dravyāṇāṁ manyatē bhavān ? yadi hi kāryataḥ
karmāpattiḥ syāt akarmabhūtasya kāryayōgō na vidyata iti bhavati phalānta-
rānubandhāt karmāntaram । atha tu niyōgavaśāt karmāpattiravasīyatē
yāvanniyōgaviṣayaiva sā bhavati । na hi kāryataḥ sā śak‍yā'vagantum ।﻿<pb n="b510"/>
śēṣavadanumānagamyō hi kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ । tēna ca kāraṇamātrāvagatirēva na
punaṁrviśēṣasyaiva kāraṇatāvagatiḥ । nanu ca sāmānyatō dr̥ṣṭaṁ karmaṇa ēva
phalaṁ prati kāraṇatāmavagamayatītyabhiprāyaḥ kr̥ṣ‍yādiṣu darśanāt । tadi&mdash;
dānīṁ sāmānyaṁ kimiti na vidmaḥ sādr̥śyaṁ tāvat samudr̥śēna vyavadhīyatē﻿<pb n="b511"/>
atha viśēṣamātraṁ, kr̥ṣyantaramēva prāpnōtīti । atha sādhanādyanubandhakr̥taṁ
tatpāpi dvayamāpatati sādhanaviśēṣō vā'nubandhatayā gr̥hyatē ? sādhanamātraṁ
vā ? viśēṣagrahaṇē phaladēvatayōranyatvānna sāmānyāvagatiḥ । atha sāmānyaṁ,
na, kriyātvamātramēva tatra avaśiṣyatē । tasmiṁśca sāmānyē'naikāntikatvaṁ﻿<pb n="b512"/>
viruddhatā ca sarvatra guṇakarmāvagatēḥ । tasmānna kāryataḥ
karmāpattirdravyāṇāṁ śak‍yatē'vagantum । kiṁ tarhi ? niyōgata
ēva bhāvāpattiranugamanīyā, sa, cāyaṁ niyōgō dadhisādhanaṁ hōmamēva phala-
sambandhitayā'vagamayatīti karmabhēdaḥ । anyathā hi hōmāsaṁbandhānna
dadhnaḥ prāpnōti । ēvaṁ cātra dadhnaḥ karmāpattiḥ prāpnōti । na ca sā
tasmādvāk‍yādavasīyatē । anavagamyamānā phalē na saṁbadhyata ityuktam ।﻿<pb n="b513"/>
kimiti vā dadhnā hōmō nirvartyatē yadi na hōmārthaṁ dadhi syāt । tasmāt
padadvayānvita ēvāyamarthaḥ phalēna saṁbadhyata iti karmāntaratvam । anyathā
hyāśritatvātprayōgasyētyayuktiḥ syāt yadi kēvalasyāpi phalēna saṁbandhaḥ
syāt । atō(dhātu)viśiṣṭabhāvānupravēśitaiva phalasaṁbandhē hētuḥ । kambala-
nirṇējanōpanyāsastu na kāryataḥ karmāpattiriti prakaṭayati । kathaṁ tarhi ?
viniyōgāt kāryamiti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b514"/>
<p><q>atulyatvāt‍tu vāk‍yayōrguṇē ।</q> atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;satyaṁ karmatāmā-
pannasya guṇasya vidhānam । na punaḥ karmārthatayaivēti । kasmāt ? kriyākāraka-﻿<pb n="b515"/>
lakṣaṇaṁ hi saṁbandhamāśritya dravyāṇāṁ tadāpattiḥ । na punaḥ
tādarthyaṁ, akarmaṇaḥ akārakatvaprasaṅgāt । ataḥ phalārthataiva kārakabhūtasya
dadhnaḥ pratīyatē । hōmārthatvē vāk‍yabhēdastvavaivōktaḥ । viśiṣṭavidhānaṁ
kimiti nāśrīyatē ? agnihōtraṁ juhōtīti hōmāvacchinnasya karmaṇaḥ
prāptatvāt dadhyanubandhasya cāpraptatvāt tāvatā indriyakāmādhikāranirvr̥ttēḥ na
śak‍yatē prāptirbādhitum । nanu cāpr̥thagavagamādanubandhadvayasya na pr̥thak‍tvē-
nāvacchēdaḥ śak‍yatē'vagantum ।</p>﻿<pb n="b516"/>
<p>ucyatē । kimatra pr̥thak‍tvēnāvacchēdaḥ kariṣyati yāvadaprāptaṁ
hi niyōgasya viṣaya ityuktam । karmāpattēśca juhōtirviṣayaḥ ।
tasmājjuhōtyavacchinnavyāpārāśritō dadhivyāpāraḥ phalayā cōdyatē ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b517"/>
kimidaṁ āśrita iti ? kārakatāmāpanna ityarthaḥ । tasmāt
hōmē kārakaṁ phalāya cōdyatē । kēna punaḥ phalē(na)viniyuk‍taṁ tat ? karma-
vāk‍yēna viniyuktam । adhikārānupapattyēti cēt । tulyamatrāpi । <q>ata
ēvōcē vr̥ttikārēṇēti ।</q> vr̥ttikāravacanaṁ kiṁparaṁ bhāṣyakārasya ? idaṁ-
param । kārakāpattirēvāśrayaśabdēnōcyatē nārthāntaramiti pradarśayitum ।
ata ēvāśritatvātprayōgasya ityatrāpi ayamēvārthaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b518"/> 
<p><q>bādhyatētarāṁ śrutiriti<note n="(1)"> P. 515</note></q>। kaḥ punaratra tarabarthaḥ । ēkatra hōmō
vidhīyatē । anyatra dadh‍yarthaḥ । na kaścidatiśayaḥ pakṣadvayē'pi dr̥śyatē । 
ucyatē । ayamasti viśēṣaḥ dadhipadē hi bādhyamānē hōmapadamapi
bādhitaṁ bhavati । ataḥ tatsaṁbandhēna hi tadvidhēyamityuk‍tam । āśri&mdash;
tatvātprayōgasyēti । tasmāt sambandhibādhē saṁbandhyantarabādhaḥ । sō'yaṁ
tarabarthaḥ hōmamātrabādhē tu na kiñcidbādhitam । kēvalasyānavagamāt ।
prāptimātratayā hi kēvalāvagatiḥ । <q>kathamiti ? anayā'gnihōtrēti-
kartavyatayaivēti ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="b519"/> 
<p>nanu cōparitanaṣaṭ‍kacintēyam । kimityatrōpanyasyatē ?
astyatrōpanyāsakāraṇam । kiṁ tat ? idaṁ tat ? guṇaphalasaṁbandhē
hi itikartavyatāsaṁbandhō na śak‍yatē avadhārayitum । na cētikartavyatā&mdash;
śūnyō'dhikāravidhiḥ । kuta ētat ? adhikāraniṣṭhō hi vidhiḥ niyōgārtha-
sādhyatayā'vagamyatē । na ca sādhyamanitikartavyatākamasti, ananu-
gr̥hītasya karaṇatvānupapattēḥ । sarvadā hi karaṇaṁ karaṇaṁ syāt । kathaṁ punaḥ na
śak‍yatē'vadhārayitum । upadēśatastāvan‍na saṁbhavati । nityānityasaṁyōga-
virōdhāt । atidēśastarhi bhavatu ? sō'pi nōpapadyata
ityabhiprāyaḥ । kathaṁ nōpapadyatē ? dhātvarthasyānyaprayuktatvāt ।﻿<pb n="b520"/> 
tatprayōgāśritatvācca guṇaphalasaṁbandhasya । anyaprayōgaprayuktasyānyēna saṁbandhō
na ghaṭatē uk‍taṁ yajātithyāyā ityatra । atidēśō'pi naivāprayōjakasya ।
tasmād‍durbhaṇēyaṁ guṇādhikāracōdanā । na cātra prasaṅgaḥ śak‍yatē vak‍tum
prāp‍tyabhāvāt । prāptasya hi dharmajātasyānyadīyēna dharmajātēna kārya-
siddhiḥ prasaṅgaḥ । na cātra prāptirastīti darśitamupadēśātidēśayōra&mdash;
﻿<pb n="b521"/>
bhāvāt । ataḥ kimatra sannidhiḥ cōdanāliṅgaṁ vā karōti । atrōcyatē ।
bhavatvatidēśātsaṁbandhaḥ । nanu ca paraprayōgāśrayī guṇaprayōgavidhirityuktam ।
nāyaṁ dōṣaḥ । anyaprayuktasyānyēna saṁbandhōpadēśō nōpapadyata iti । ati-
dēśē punaḥ [kāryataḥ saṁbandhamatidēśavidō manyantē । tataḥ kiṁ ? kāryataḥ
saṁbandhē hi viniyōgāvagatērna virōdhaḥ । yatra hi kāraṇapurassarā kāryāvagatiḥ
sa viniyōgasya viṣayaḥ yatra punaḥ] kāryataḥ kāraṇāvagatiḥ sō'tidēśasya ।﻿<pb n="b522"/>
tasmānna viniyōgavaiṣamyāt vighātō yadātithyāyāṁ itivat । tasmāt
sūk‍taṁ <quote>‘anayā agnihōtrētikartavyatayā’</quote> iti । atha kasmādagnihōtra-
mēvētikartavyatā na bhavati ? āśraya ēvānugrāhakō dravyāṇām kāryaṁ
sādhayatām, āśritatvāt prayōgasyēti darśanam । bāliśabhāṣitamētat ।
agnihōtramēva karaṇaṁ dadh‍yanuraktamityuk‍tam । kēvalasyānavaga-
māt । prayuk‍tistu kēvalāśrayaprāp‍tyanusārēṇēti guṇaphalamityucyatē ।﻿<pb n="b523"/>
tasmāt ṣaṣṭhīsamāsa ēvāyaṁ agnihōtrētikartavyatayēti । atidēśaprāptasya ca
dharmajātasya prasaṅgāt kāryasiddhiriti siddhamanāvr̥ttyaiva anuṣṭhānam ।
<q><quote>“atha vā dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitārthatvāt”</quote></q> iti । kimidaṁ pakṣāntara-
mivōpanyasyatē । kimiti vā na pakṣāntaraṁ ? tadēvaṁ hi dadhyanurak‍taṁ hōmarūpaṁ
phalāyētyupasaṁhr̥tam । yuk‍taṁ caitat । saṁbandhasyānurāgā(bhā)vagamyatvāt ।
ucyatē । pakṣāntaraśaṅkānirākaraṇāyaitaddhāṣyam । na pakṣāntarapradarśanārtham ।</q>﻿<pb n="b524"/> 
kā punaratra pakṣāntaraśaṅkā ? dadhnā juhōtīti kēvalaguṇavidhānāt ।
avagatasya saṁbandhasya vidhānamastviti kēcit । tēṣāmidamuttaram ।
dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitatvānna saṁbandharayētyarthaḥ । ataḥ siddhō guṇavidhi-
phalādhikārasaṁbandhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>samēṣu karmayuk‍taṁ syāt ।</q> uktaṁ guṇānubandhāt karmaṇaḥ
phalamiti । tadidānīṁ kīdr̥śō viṣaya iti ( nirūpyatē । ) viṣaya&mdash;
nirūpaṇāyaitadadhikaraṇadvayam । nanu ca bhēdābhēdacintā atna lakṣaṇē﻿<pb n="b525"/> 
prakr̥tā । saivēyaṁ viṣayatō nirūpyatē । nanu ca viparītamatrēdaṁ
śāstrabhēdō hi guṇaphalasaṁbandhō'pi vidyata ēva । kathamatra tannirākaraṇādbhēdaḥ ।
śāstrabhēdakathā cēyāmiti bhāṣyavidaḥ । tasmādasamañjasamidaṁ bhēdābhēda-
nirūpaṇam । atrōcyatē&mdash;satyaṁ guṇaviśēṣataḥ śāstrabhēdaḥ aprayō-
jakastvāśrayasyēti na bhēdēna vyapadiś‍yatē । dhātvarthānubandhabhēdē punaḥ﻿<pb n="b526"/> 
saha prayōk‍tr̥tayā śās‍traṁ bhidyata iti bhēdēna vyapadēśaḥ । ata ēva ca
athātō dharmajijñāsēti śās‍trēṇa prayōk‍tr̥tvābhēdādabhēdaṁ manvānasya ida-
muttaram । atō dhātvarthānubandhabhēdē guṇānubandhabhēdē ca viśēṣō'stīti
viṣayavirūpaṇam । kathaṁ punaḥ agniṣṭōmasāma kr̥tvā yajēta iti﻿<pb n="b527"/>
pūrvāparībhāvaḥ ? kathaṁ vā nāsti ? । savanadvayē hyatītē agniṣṭōmasāma-
prayōgaḥ । ēkaścāyaṁ yajyarthaḥ । tasmādanupapattiḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu ca grahayajāvāpi sa ēvāyamagniṣ‍ṭut‍saṁjñakō yāga ityupapadyatē
pūrvāparībhāvaḥ । abhyāsō hi sakalasya dhātvarthasya naikadēśasya । ata
ēva nōpapadyatē । sakalasyānuṣṭhānāt । parastādastītyupapadyatē iti
cēnna । ayathābhūtatvādarthasya । yatra hi yathā pratīyamāna ēvārthaḥ śabdāt
svabhāvatō'pi tathaiva tatrāvipratipattiḥ anyathābhāvē tu nautpattikatvaṁ syāt ।
autpattikastu śabdasyārthēna saṁbandha iti gaditam । atō nābhyāsavaśāt﻿<pb n="b528"/> 
kr̥tvā yajētēti śabdādartha upapadyatē । sābhyāsasya hi dhātvarthasya
uttarakālīnatā'vadhāryatē । na caitad‍bhāṣyakārēṇāvamr̥ṣṭam । ucyatē ।
anavamarśanīyamēvaitat । samānakartr̥katvāpēkṣō hyatra pūrvāparībhāvaḥ ।
sa ca pratītāvēvōpapadyatē nānuṣṭhānē । samānakartr̥katvavyāghātāt ।
ēkārthānāmanēkadhātvarthānāmanuparatyā'nuṣṭhānaṁ samānakartr̥tvamucyatē । na ca
tatra pūrvamidaṁ kr̥tvā paścādidaṁ kartavyamiti śak‍yatē vak‍tum । vyavacchēda-
prasaṅgāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b529"/>
<p>kathaṁ tarhi <quote>‘darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭ‍vā sōmēna yajēta’</quote> iti ।
adhikāramātraṁ taditi vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmādavagatau pūrvakālatā <quote>‘mukhaṁ
vyādāya svapiti’</quote> itivat prayōgasiddhēḥ । kathaṁ punaratra guṇaphalā-
śaṅkā ? guṇāśravaṇāt, vāravantīyaṁ kr̥tvēti sannidhānācca karmaṇaḥ । 
sannihitē hi karmaṇi guṇaśrutiḥ tadanubandhaparatāṁ vidhērjñāpayatī-
tyuktam । atō dadh‍nēndriyakāmavat guṇānubandhāt । ēvaṁ caita-
syēti mukhyārthaṁ padamanvayi bhavati । nanu vāravantīyaṁ rēvatīṣu﻿<pb n="b530"/> 
kr̥tvēti aprāptā rēvatyō vidhātavyāḥ vāravantīyasambandhitā ca । viśiṣṭa-
yāgavādinō'p‍yayaṁ tulyō dōṣaḥ । ataḥ saṁbandhavidhānākṣēpāt bhavatāṁ
vidhānasiddhiḥ । atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;nānyaprayuktāt bhāvārthācchāstrāntara-
midam । kiṁ tarhi ? tathaiva sahaiva prayuk‍tyā bhidyatē śāstram । 
ētaduk‍taṁ bhavati । karmaṇaḥ sakāśāt phalamiti kutaḥ ? aprāpta-
tvāt rēvatīnām । na guṇāt phalamiti śak‍yatē vak‍tum । nanu
cōktaṁ saṁbandhividhānākṣēpāt rēvatīnāṁ vidhānasiddhiriti । satyaṁ siddhayati
na yāgānubandhatayā । guṇānubandhācca bhāvārthāt phalaṁ guṇaphala-
mityucyatē na kēvalād‍guṇāt phalanāmatvād‍guṇaphalānām । bhāvārtha-﻿<pb n="b531"/> 
viṣayabhāvācca niyōgasya । <q>athōcyēta&mdash;asyā pūrvā rēvatīrupādāya tāsu
ca vāravantīyaṁ kr̥tvā yajñēna yajētēti ।</q> anēna pūrvasmāt kō viśēṣa
upanyastaḥ ? aprāptā rēvatyaḥ kathamupādīyantē ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;rēvatī-
viśiṣṭaṁ vāravantīyaṁ yāgānubandhatayā pratīyamānaṁ rēvatīḥ ēkatvavat
upādānaśēṣīkarōti । satyamēvaitat । (a)tathāp‍yagniṣṭōma sāmēti
nāvakal‍patē । kimiti nāvakal‍patē ? yāgānubandhatayā hi vāra&mdash;
vantīyaṁ (pratī)vidhīyamānaṁ stōtraviśēṣasaṁbandhitayā śak‍yatē'vagantum ।﻿<pb n="b532"/> 
<p><q>athāg‍niṣ‍ṭōmasāmnaḥ kāryē bhavatītyucyata iti ।</q> kimida-
magniṣṭōmasāmnaḥ kāryē bhavatītyucyata iti । ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yāgānu-
bandhitayā pratīyamānaṁ vāravantīyaṁ na kāryāntaraśūnyamanubandhi bhavatīti ।
kāryaviśēṣāpēkṣāyāmagniṣṭōmasāmaśabdaḥ kāryasamarpakō bhavatīti na vāk‍ya-
bhēdaḥ । <q>ētasyētyētadavivakṣicaṁ syāt ।</q> kimityavivakṣitaṁ syāt ?
yadyayaṁ śabdalabhyō'rthaḥ syāt avivakṣitam । atra punaḥ prakr̥ta
ēvāyamagniṣ‍ṭut pratīyatē tasyāyaṁ ētasyētyanuvādaḥ । ataścāvivakṣāyā-
map‍yadōṣaḥ । tasmāt karmāntaratayōpanyāsō na ghaṭatē, rēvatyādhāravāravantī&mdash;
yānubandhatabā hi na prakr̥tō yāgaḥ śak‍yatē'vagantuṁ, r̥gantarādhāra-﻿<pb n="b533"/> 
tayāvagatēḥ । nanu phalārthatvē guṇasya nāyaṁ dōṣaḥ gōdōhanavat । tatra
hi camasānubandhaṁ praṇayanaṁ pratīyamānamapi gōdōhanānubandhatayā phalārthatvē
guṇānubandhasya na viruddhayatē । ēvamatrāpi kō virōdhaḥ, vak‍tavyō vā
viśēṣaḥ । ayamabhidhīyatē&mdash;tatra hi ap‍praṇayanārthakāryatayā gōdōhanasya
kēvalapraṇayanābhinirvr̥ttyā na virōdhaḥ śak‍yatē vak‍tum । iha punaḥ
yāgānubandhatayā pratīyatē ayāgārthaṁ ca nirvartayati na prakr̥tānubandhitayā﻿<pb n="b534"/> 
śak‍yatē'vagantum । prakr̥taṁ hyagniṣṭōmasāma vāyavyānavubandham । tasmāt
kāryānubandhayōḥ virōdhaḥ । akāryānubandhatvāt vāravantīyasya rēvatyādhārasya ।
tasmādētasyēti vivakṣitamityuktam । anuvādānupapattēḥ । karmāntaratvē﻿<pb n="b535"/> 
punaḥ saha prayuk‍tyā śāstrabhēdāt na dōṣō bhavatīti । ubhayasmin vivakṣya-
māṇa ityarthaḥ । na kaścidēkō viniyōga ubhayānubandhitāmāpādayituṁ
kṣamaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi sādhāraṇaguṇavidhānam ? aikarūp‍yē hi tat na
guṇapradhānavyavasthitānām । kathaṁ tarhi aṅgapradhānārthatā barhirādīnām ?
kēvalaprayōgaśēṣatayā nāvacchēdānubandhitayā । iha cānubandhāvacchē&mdash;
dānubandhatvē virōdha uktaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b536"/> 
<p>kathaṁ punaratrāpi prayōgānubandhitayaiva na vāravantīyaṁ parigr̥hyatē । na,
vāk‍yēna yāgāvacchinnāvagatēḥ । prakaraṇāvagamyā hi prayōgānubandhatā । anu-
pādēyagamyā vā vāk‍yādibhirapi, sāmarthyāvagamyā vā । pradhānasambandhō
dakṣiṇāvat । iha punaḥ vāk‍yēna yāgānubandhataivēti ētasyētyavivakṣā ।﻿<pb n="b537"/> 
<note n="(1)"> p. 533</note><q><quote>“atha karmāntarē kathamavāk‍yabhēda”</quote></q> iti viśiṣṭavidhānasiddhēḥ praśnō-
nōpapadyatē । avāntarastōtrasaṁbandhaḥ r̥k‍sāmayōrnōpapadyata ityabhiprāyaḥ ।
rāddhāntavādinastarhi kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;rēvatīvāravantīya-
saṁbandhaḥ stōtrē na syāt । yadyēkabhāvaviśēṣaṇaṁ r̥gdravyaṁ sāma vā syāt । atra
punaḥ rēvatīvāravantīyasaṁbandhābhinirvr̥ttō bhāvō bhāvāntarasya viśēṣaṇam । sa ca
bhāvaviśiṣṭō bhāvō vidhīyamānō yajinā viśēṣ‍yata ityadōṣa ityābhiprāyaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b538"/> 
yuk‍taṁ tāvat abhinirvr̥ttiṁ vadatīti, pūrvakālatāṁ cētyayuktam । na
rēvatīvāravantīyasaṁbandhōttarakālatā yajēḥ । ucyatē&mdash;pratipattāvēva tadi&mdash;
tyuktamasmābhiḥ । samānakartr̥katvaṁ tu ēkaprayōgatāmāpādayatīti
siddhaṁ viśiṣṭavidhānam । <q>artha iti prayōjanamabhidhīyata</q> iti
niyōgārthābhiprāyamētat । kathaṁ punaḥ ēkaniyōgavidhānamiti
taddarśayati&mdash;rēvatīṣu vāravantīyamiti । nādyāpi ca samāptiḥ ।﻿<pb n="b539"/> 
kriyāpēkṣiṇ‍yō hi vinā kriyāṁ na parisamāp‍yantē tataḥ kr̥t‍vēti
kriyāsaṁbandhaḥ । ayamapi ca karōtiḥ kr̥t‍vēti k‍tvāntaḥ san
naiva svakārasaṁbandhaparyavasāyī । kiṁ tarhi ? bhāvārthāntarāpēkṣa&mdash;
statkārakaiḥ saṁbandhamanubhavati । bhāvāntaraṁ yajyarthaviśiṣṭaṁ pratīyata
ityupapattyā ēkaprayōjanasaṁbandha iti na vāk‍yabhēdaḥ । guṇa-
phalasaṁbandhē punaḥ viparītamētat । atha punaḥ ētasyēti śrutyanurōdhāt
rēvatīvāravantīyaviśiṣṭō yāgaḥ prakr̥tāgniṣṭudaṅgatayaiva cōdyatē kō dōṣaḥ ?﻿<pb n="b540"/> 
na khalu kaściddōṣaḥ । adhikārāntarānarthak‍yaṁ tu bhavati । <q>athaivamucyatē
rēvatīṣu kr̥tēna vāravantīyēna paśukāmō yajētēti ।</q> kimidamarthāntara-
mupanyastam ? idam । bhāva ēvāyaṁ bhāvāntaramāśritaḥ kasmānna phala sādha&mdash;
yati ? yathaiva hi rēvatīvāravantīyaviśiṣṭaḥ karōtyarthō yajatērviśēṣaṇam ।  ēvaṁ
phalārthaḥ kimiti na bhavati । rāddhāntavādī tu vacanāddatē na na gōdōhanavat
praṇayanasya avihitaṁ sādhanaṁ sādhanaṁ bhavati । vihitaṁ hi sādhanaṁ bhavi-﻿<pb n="b541"/> 
tumarhati । kutaḥ ? rēvatīsthavāravantīyasya kāryāntarāśrayaṇā-
diti prāgap‍yuk‍tamēva tat । tadidamuk‍taṁ r̥gantarapragāṇāta
stōtrasādhanaviśēṣahānaṁ syāt । tataśca kratōrvaiguṇ‍yaṁ bhavēt । ayaṁ
cārthō <q>yāvat prakaraṇādaṅgabhāvaḥ</q> ityētēna bhāṣyēṇa pradarśitaḥ ।
prakaraṇaṁ hi vāk‍yēnāviniyuktasya aidamarthyāyālaṁ bhavitumarhati । tasmānna
gādōhanavat kratusādhanasya sataḥ phalārthatā upapadyatē kr̥tvēti bhāvasya ।﻿<pb n="b542"/> 
ataḥ prayōk‍tr̥śāstrasya bhēdaḥ <quote>“yāgaguṇakaṁ rēvatīṣu vāravantīyaṁ
tada‍guṇakō vā yāga”</quote> iti tāvat bhāvadvayasyāsyaikakartr̥katā-
lakṣaṇaḥ saṁbandhaḥ । aṅgāṅgibhāvastu anyatō mr̥gya iti darśa-
yati । kutō'nyataḥ pratyayasannikarṣāditi pradarśitam । <q>atha
punaḥ viśiṣ‍ṭē yāgē vidhīyamānē tadrēvatīṣu vāravantīyaṁ katha-
﻿<pb n="b543"/> 
magniṣ‍ṭōma sāma bhavatīti ।</q> yāgē hi viśiṣṭē agniṣṭōmasāviśēṣaṇatvaṁ
nāpapadyata ityarthaḥ । kāryasamarpaṇādagniṣṭōmasāmnō na dōṣa iti parihāraḥ ।
athēdānīmētasyēti kā kathā spaṣṭē'tra śāstrabhēdē ? ētaddharmakasyēti mantavyam ।</p>
<p><q>saubharē puruṣaśrutēḥ ।</q> uktō guṇādhikārasaṁbandhaḥ । yadā-
śritō guṇaḥ tatsaṁbandhinyadhikārē guṇādhikāra iti siddhaṁ anyāśritē guṇē﻿<pb n="b544"/> 
anyasya cā'dhikārasaṁbandhē bhāvādēva phalaṁ ityētadapi sthitam । ihēdānīṁ
yadāśritō guṇaḥ tatraivādhikāraḥ । kasmādadhikārāntaramidamiti manyatē ? ।
viśēṣamapaśyan sarvasya cōktahētutvāt । tasmin kāmābhidhā-
nārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ । satyamēvaṁ yadāśritō guṇaḥ sa iti,﻿<pb n="b545"/> 
sat‍yāṁ cāprāptau । prāptau punarabhidhēyapratyabhijñānaṁ nādhikārāntarāvagatiḥ ।﻿<pb n="b546"/> 
lakṣaṇāśabdēna cāsminnadhikaraṇē abhidhēyapratyabhijñānamēvōcyatē । na
padārthāntarasamarpaṇam । karmāntarānavagatiriva dadhnā juhōtīti । kimartha-
starhi punaḥ śrutiḥ ? vidhānārthēti brūmaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b547"/> 
<p>nanu cādhikāraśrutiriva nidhanaśrutirapi prakr̥tābhidhāyinyēva ।
satyamēvaṁ yadyēkanidhanamēva saubharaṁ syāt । vr̥ṣṭikāmādhikārō'yugapatprayō-
j‍yānēkanidhānaṁ tu tat । ataḥ pakṣē'pratyabhijñānāt siddhaṁ nidhanārthā
punaḥ śrutiriti ।</p>
<trailer>iti prabhākaramiśrakr̥tau mīmāṁsābhāṣyavivaraṇē
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>﻿<pb n="b548"/> 
<head>br̥hatī</head>
<head>atha dvitīyādh‍yāyasya</head>
<head>tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>guṇastu kratusaṁyōgāt ।</q> kiṁ punaratrāpratyabhijñākāraṇaṁ ? kratva-
bhidhānaṁ rathantarasāmākhyaḥ katuḥ nāsti prakr̥taḥ । <q>kathaṁ tarhi saṁśayaḥ ?</q>﻿<pb n="b549"/> 
yadiśabdaśravaṇāt। yadiśabdō hi prasiddhārthatāmāpadayati atō bhavati
saṁśayaḥ। kiṁ yadiśravaṇādupasarjanaparamidamabhidhānaṁ, utābhidhānasāmarthyāt﻿<pb n="b550"/> 
kat‍vantarābhidhānamastviti । kiṁ yuk‍taṁ ? abhidhānasāmarthyamantaraṅgaṁ antaraṅgaṁ
ca bahiraṅgādbalīyaḥ । paripūrṇaṁ hi padaṁ padāntaramākāṅkṣati । anvayānurōdhī ca﻿<pb n="b551"/> 
yadiśabdō na svatantraḥ । tasmāt yathā kratvantarābhidhānamupapadyatē
tathātasyārthō varṇanīyaḥ । pradarśitāśca prakārāḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b552"/> ﻿<pb n="b553"/> 
<p><q>ēkasya tu liṅgabhēdāt ।</q> atrōcyatē&mdash;yadyabhidhānavirōdhaḥ
syāt yadyarthō na vivakṣ‍yēta na tvatra abhidhānavirōdha upapadyatē । tarhyupa-
sarjanārthē cāpi nimittatayā parigr̥hyamāṇē kratōrēvābhidhānam । nanu
sāmāntarasaṁbandhē sati kratōrabhidhānaṁ na prāp‍nōti । maivam&mdash;virōdhāpēkṣaṁ
hi sāmarthyam । vr̥hatā ca rathantarasya kratusaṁbandhē virōdhaḥ na sāmamātrēṇa ।﻿<pb n="b554"/> 
tasmādanityaḥ śabda itivadupapannamabhidhānam । tadyōgācca nimittatvaṁ kratōḥ ।
kathaṁ tarhi upasarjanārthē nimittamityucyatē tadanubandhānusāriṇī hi
bhēdāvagatiḥ katōḥ । tasmāttannimittamityucyatē guṇaphalōpabandhavat ।﻿<pb n="b555"/> 
kratōrēva hi nimittatvaṁ na tadanubandhasya ।</p>
<p><q>avēṣ‍ṭau yajñasaṁyōgāt ।</q> atra vrāhmaṇādiśravaṇaṁ yadyartha&mdash;
yōgaśca saṁśayahētuḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b556"/> 
<p>yadi rājasūyē brāhmaṇānāṁ prāptiḥ tadā pūrvādhikaraṇavat
abhidhānāvirōdhāt nimittārthāni śravaṇāni । atha tu na
prāptiḥ tadā karmāntaravidhānaṁ tadanurōdhēna ca yadyarthō vyākhyēyaḥ pūrvādhi-
karaṇapūrvapakṣavat । kathaṁ punaḥ prāp‍tyaprāptī avagamyatē ? rājaśabdasyā-
bhidhēyānirūpaṇāt । yadi hi rājaśabdaḥ karmayōgāt kartari vartatē tadā﻿<pb n="b557"/> 
prāptiḥ । atha kartr̥(ri)yōgāt karmābhidhīyatē tadā na prāptiḥ tadā pika-
nēmasatatāmarasādīnāmiva m‍lēcchavyavahārādēva abhidhānāvagatiḥ kaḥ punaratra
nirṇāyakahētuḥ ? pūrvapakṣavādītu manyatē karmayōgāt kartaryabhidhānam, ārya-
vyavahārāt । m‍lēcchānāṁ punarāryavirōdhē hyuk‍tamaprāmāṇ‍yaṁ yavavarāhādiṣu । nanu
cāryāṇāṁ mūrdhābhiṣik‍tāḥ śabdavidaḥ kartr̥yōgāt karmaśabdaṁ smaranti;﻿<pb n="b558"/> 
satyaṁ, vyavahāramūlatvāt smr̥tēḥ prakr̥tiprat‍yayavibhāgārthamētadbhaviṣ‍yati ।
prakaraṇānugrahāt yadiśabdōpabandhācca nimittārthāni śravaṇāni । kiñca
m‍lēcchairapi karmayōgāt kartari prayuj‍yata ēva । tataḥ kim ? āviprati-
pattiḥ avipratipattēśca na pratipakṣatāṁ kartr̥pūrvakaḥ prayōgaḥ bhajata
ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b559"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyatē&mdash;prāpakāṇ‍yēvaitāni । kutaḥ ? smr̥tēḥ।
vipratipattau hi prayōgasya smr̥tiḥ pramāṇaṁ gavādiṣviva ।
smr̥tiśca kartr̥yōgāt karmaśabda iti । nanu cāpratipakṣaḥ
sārvabhaumaḥ prayōga ityuktam । sati ca pratipakṣē smr̥titō nirṇayaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b560"/>
āryaprayōgamūlatvācca vyākaraṇarabhr̥tēḥ prayōgadapi virōdhaḥ । ataśca virōdhē
t‍vanapēkṣamiti bādha ēva nyāy‍yaḥ । prātipadikārthavibhāgārthatayōpapadyata
it‍yuk‍tam । ucyatē । na smr̥tiravabādhituṁ śak‍yatē । mūlābhāvāddhi
s‍mr̥tērbādhaḥ । asti cēdaṁ mūlaṁ mantrāṇāṁ prayōgaḥ । nanu ca
sārvabhaumaprayōgaḥ āryavyavahāraśca virudhyatē । na viruddhayatē । andhra&mdash;
prayōgamūlāyāmapi s‍mr̥tāvupapadyata ēvāryavyavahāraḥ, sārvabhaumat‍vaṁ ca ।﻿<pb n="b561"/>
tas‍mādvirōdhē t‍vanapēkṣamityētadap‍yuktamayuk‍tam । apratyakṣatā siddhaiva । naivaṁ
sati sārvabhaumasya prat‍yakṣatōpapadyatē । kāryakaratvāt prayōgōpapattēḥ।
﻿<pb n="b562"/>
tasmāt prāpakāṇ‍yētāni vacanāni kṣatriyābhidhānādrājaśabdasya । yaduk‍taṁ
prātipadikārthavibhāgārthā s‍mr̥tiriti; na mūlē saṁbhavatyanyārthatā sūtrasya
śak‍yatē vak‍tum । ataḥ prāpakāṇ‍yētāni ।</p>﻿<pb n="b563"/>﻿<pb n="b564"/>
<p><q>ādhānē'sarvaśēṣatvāt ।</q> kimatra cintyatē ? ādhānagatō bhēdaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b565"/>
kiṁ bhinnamādhānaṁ utābhinnamiti । nanu ca ṣaṣṭhē'p‍yadhikārārthatayā
bhēda ēva cin‍titaḥ । ya ēvaṁ vidvānāgnimādhattē iti idamēva pratipakṣa-
tayōpanyastam । arthākṣēpaśca । tasmādvēdaṁ nārab‍dhavyam । ēkasyaiva nyāyasya
phaladvayamidam । tasmādatrōcyatē । (bhēdā)bhēdē hyanubandhabhēdō hētuḥ ।﻿<pb n="b566"/>
atō brāhmaṇādyanubandhabhēdō abhēdē na yuktaḥ । tatra adhikr̥tasyāgnayaḥ
uta sāgnikasyādhikāra ityanyaiva cintā । sa cāyaṁ viśēṣaḥ tatraiva
nipuṇataraṁ varṇ‍yatē । iha tu kēvalavidhānābhāvāt brāhmaṇādyanubandhabhēdādbhēda
ityuktam । kaḥ punaratra bhēdābhēdayōḥ karmaṇi viśēṣaḥ ? yasya
hi yasmin kālē ādhānaṁ vihitaṁ tasya hi tadaivādhānam ।﻿<pb n="b567"/>
nimittārthāyāmapi śrutau tul‍yamētat । ubhayaniyamāt । ēvaṁ tarhi
nakṣatrādyādhānamētatkālīnamēva trayāṇāmapi kathaṁ syāditi viśēṣaḥ ।
adhikārē punarviśēṣaṁ darśayiṣ‍yāmaḥ । nanu cātmanēpadōpanyāsō&mdash;
'dhikāra ēvōpayuj‍yatē kr̥trimādinivr̥ttyarthaṁ na punaḥ bhēdacintāyāṁ,﻿<pb n="b568"/>
pārārthyēpi hi ādhānasyānubandhabhēdāt siddhayatyēva bhēdaḥ tasminnimitta-
tvāt । ucyatē&mdash;ēvaṁ cādhikāravirōdhō na bhaviṣ‍yatītyabhyuccayō
draṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b569"/>﻿<pb n="b570"/>﻿<pb n="b571"/>
<p><q>ayanēṣu cōdanāntaram ।</q> saṁjñā cōtpattisaṁyōgāditi saṁjñā
bhēt‍trīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b572"/>
<p><q>vikārō vā prakaraṇāt ।</q> sat‍yaṁ saṁjñā bhēt‍trī yatra prakr̥tē karmaṇi
guṇāntarānuk‍tē sati guṇāntarānuraktāḥ sādhikārāścōdanāḥ śrūyantē ।</p>﻿<pb n="b573"/>
tatra saṁjñānyatvataḥ karmānyatvamākhyātasāmānādhikaraṇyaṁ pradarśayadbhiḥ prada-
rśitamasmābhiḥ ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="b574"/>
<p>yacca samāptaṁ ca phalē vāk‍yamiti na phalacōdanā karmāntaratvamā-
pādayituṁ kṣamā ananubandhatvāt phalānām । kathaṁ tarhi <quote>‘phalaṁ cā-
karmasannidhau’</quote> iti ? asannidhānamēva hi tatra kāraṇaṁ na phalam ।
na hyasannihitaṁ karma yajinā viśēṣataḥ pratipādayituṁ śak‍yatē । tasmā-﻿<pb n="b575"/>
dvidhānata ēva tatra viśēṣō'vagantavyaḥ । iha punaḥ sannihitamastīti
na phalaṁ bhēdakamityucyatē । saṁjñāntarōpalabdhasya prayōjanaṁ tatpravr̥tti-
nimittaguṇayuktasya kathaṁ nāma vidhānamiti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b576"/>
<p><q>saṁskāraścāprakaraṇē ।</q> <quote>‘vāyavyaṁ ś‍vētamālabhēta’</quote> ityasmin
vāk‍yē parasparasvarūpānanvitamēva padārthajātaṁ lakṣyatē ।  kathaṁ ? aya-
mālabhatirna dravyadēvatānvayi । tasmādālabhatērvidhānaṁ dravyadēvatāpadasaṁbandha-
nirapēkṣasya । anuvādō vā, prathamapūrvapakṣavādī anuvādaṁ manyatē ।
ś‍vētapadānvayalābhāt । atō yadālabhēta tacchvētaṁ iti vāk‍yārthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b577"/>
vāyavyabrahmavarcasakāmapadayōḥ kā vārtā ? parasparāsaṅgatērvāk‍yāntaraṁ aruṇā&mdash;
divaditi manyatē । yāvaduk‍taṁ vēti brahmavarcasakāmapadānvayā'pi labhyata
ityaparaḥ pakṣaḥ । ś‍vētamālabhēta brahmavarcasakāma iti paraṁ vāyavya-
padasyaikasyaivōddhāraḥ । ētadēva yuk‍taṁ īṣālambhasyāprakr̥tatvāt । atha
liṅarthō vihitōpalakṣaṇārthaḥ parigr̥hyatē vidhānaṁ na prāpnōti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b578"/>﻿<pb n="b579"/>
<p><q>yajatistu dravyaphalabhōk‍tr̥saṁyōgāt ।</q> atrōcyatē । syādēvaṁ
yadi samastapadānvayō na bhavati । bhavati tvasau । kathaṁ ? vāyavyaṁ
ś‍vētamālabhēta bhūtikāma iti vāk‍yārthō vidhīyatē । kathaṁ tarhyā-
labhatiḥ ? anuvādō'yaṁ anyataḥ prāptēḥ । aprāptasyānvayō na
saṁbhavati । nāvidhīyamānasya svargakāmavat । atō'yamālabhatirityēkaṁ
śāstram । asaṁbhavatyanvayē śāstrabhēdaḥ praviśa piṇ‍tībhitivat ।﻿<pb n="b580"/>
nanu guṇavidhidūṣaṇapakṣē'nēkaguṇavidhānaṁ darśayati । uktaṁ ca na vāyavya-
brahmavarcasakāmau saṁbadhyētē iti । ucyatē&mdash;nāyamabhiprāyaḥ īṣālabhbhē pada-
dvayavidhānamiti । kathaṁ tarhi ? yadi prāptānuvādēna īṣālambhē ś‍vētō guṇō
vidhīyatē [kiṁ na] prākr̥tēpi । atha kasmādālambhō vāyavyē brahmavarcasa-﻿<pb n="b581"/>
kāmē vā aprakr̥tē'pi na vidhīyatē ? kō nu khalu nirṇayaḥ
īṣālambhē ś‍vētaguṇavidhānamityatra ? na cālabhbhavyāptau pramāṇamastītyuktam ।
idaṁ cāpara; kathaṁ ālabhatē; ananvayamāśaṅkaya taccālabhatyarthaviśiṣṭamiti ।﻿<pb n="b582"/>
kathaṁ tarhi ? idantaduktam । nāyamēkasya vāk‍yasyātibhāraḥ yaduta kriyādvaya-
sambandhinarthaṁ vidhirvidadhātīti । aṅgāṅgibhāvasyānyataḥ siddhēḥ ।
tasmādālabhatyarthaviśiṣṭamityanvayābhiprāyamētat ।</p>﻿<pb n="b583"/>
<p><q>viśayē prāyadarśanāt ।</q> kimidaṁ viśayē prāyadarśanā-
diti ? sūtrasyānākṣiptaviṣayatāṁ darśayati । āgamagamyō'tra&mdash;﻿<pb n="b584"/>
viṣayō na sūtrāt gamyata ityarthaḥ । tathā ca darśitaṁ vr̥ttikāravacanāt
viṣayamavagacchāmaḥ upapadyatē caitaditi । kaḥ punaratra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ﻿<pb n="b585"/>
ālabhatisāmānyāt yajimatā bhavitavyamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । dravya-
dēvatāsambandhāśravaṇāt na yajimāniti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>saṁyuktastvarthaśabdēna ।</q> kimityadhikaraṇāntaramidaṁ kr̥tam ?
arthavādāt dēvatāsambandhanirākaraṇārtham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b586"/>
viśēṣākāṅkṣayāṁ hi arthavādānnirṇayaḥ । iha tūpadhānē viniyukta-
tvāt dravyastutiparaiva dēvatāśrutiriti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b587"/>
idamapi pūrvēṇa tulyam ।</p>
<p><q>pātrīvatē tu ।</q> uktaṁ dravyadēvatāsaṁyuk‍taṁ saṁskārakarmavadvāk‍yaṁ
yāgasya cōdakamiti tadidānīṁ sandihyatē । prakr̥tē yāgē dravyadēvatā-
saṁskārakarmavadvāk‍yaṁ kiṁ saṁskāramātrasya vidhāyakaṁ uta ētadapi yāgasya
vidhāyakamiti । kathaṁ punaḥ spaṣṭē prakr̥tayāgavacanatvē saṁśayaḥ ?﻿<pb n="b588"/>
saguṇanirguṇaśravaṇāt । saguṇaṁ hi prakr̥taṁ karma nirguṇaṁ cēha śrūyatē ।
tasmāt karmāntarē utsr̥jatiḥ । utsr̥jatiparyagnikr̥taśabdau ca
kāryataḥ prāptāvanūdyētē । kimidamuk‍taṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa <quote>“api ca tvāṣṭrasyō-
tsargē vidhīyamānē paryagnikr̥tasyēti viśēṣaṇaṁ nāvakalpata”</quote> iti । idamuktaṁ
viśiṣṭānuvādalakṣaṇō vāk‍yabhēda iti । nanu ca prakr̥taḥ paryagnikr̥ta﻿<pb n="b589"/>
ēva, kō'tra vāk‍yabhēda iti । prakr̥tatvēna hi avivakṣitānvayō labhyatē ।
na punarvivakṣāpyutsargē । idamaparaṁ&mdash;kiṁ paryagnikr̥ta ēva pātnīvatatā
vidhīyata iti pātnīvatatvamēva vidhīyatē । paryagnikr̥tatā prāptaiva ।
saivēyamanēna prakārēṇa darśitā bhāṣyakārēṇa ।</p>﻿<pb n="b590"/>
atrōcyatē&mdash;paryagnikr̥tasyāyamutsargaścōdyatē prakr̥tasya । nanu ca tvāṣṭaṁ
pātnīvataṁ iti śravaṇāt na pātnīvataśabdēna prakr̥tābhidhānamupapadyatē । ucyatē
na nōpapadyatē । yasya hi samāsēnābhidhānaṁ tatra vyastasyābhidhānānupapattiḥ ।
aindrāgna āg‍nēyavat । yatra punaḥ vyastayōrābhidhāna siddhaṁ prakr̥tē'pi
tatra nārthāntarē buddhirupapadyatē । tasmāt saṁskāravidhānamēvēdamavacchēda&mdash;
phalam । nanu paryagnikr̥tavivakṣā utsargē nōpapadyētētyuktam ।﻿<pb n="b591"/>
satyaṁ nōpapadyatē yadi pātnīvataśabdō vivakṣyēta । sa tu prakr̥tābhidhānāt
prāptānvayavacana ēvētyadōṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>adravyatvātkēvalē ।</q> sa ēvāyaṁ vicārō'nuvartatē । kiṁ yaji-
mati tatsaṁskārakarma uta kēvalasaṁskāravidhānamiti । tadiha cintyatē । kiṁ﻿<pb n="b592"/>
grahaṇamātracōdanē ētē uta yajitī iti । kiṁ yuktam ? yaji-
matī iti । kathaṁ ? aprayōjanavataḥ saṁskārābhāvāt । yāgaśabdaśravaṇācca
sāmayuktāt yajimatī ētē cōdanē । grahaṇādiśabdaścālabhativat prāpta
ēvānūdyatē sasōmaśabdakaḥ । nanu cāṁśau na sōmayuk‍tō yajiḥ
śrūyatē । uk‍taṁ niṣprayōjanasya saṁskārābhāvāt adābhyasāhacaryācca
tadvadbhaviṣyati iti । nanu ca jyōtiṣṭōmasyaivāyaṁ yajiranuvādaḥ﻿<pb n="b593"/>
kasmānna bhaviṣyati । aprakr̥tatvāt । prakr̥tē hi viśēṣē sāmānyaśabdō
viśēṣavacanō bhaviṣyati nāprakr̥tē । tasmādyajimatī ētē cōdanē ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē&mdash;saṁskāramātracōdanē ētē । kasmāt ? tāvanmātra-
śravaṇāt । nanu ca sōmavān yajiratra śrūyata ityuk‍taṁ; sat‍yaṁ śrūyatē ।
anyaparastu saḥ । nanu ca kēvalasaṁskāracōdanē anarthakē bhavataḥ, prayōjana-
vatō'śravaṇāt, sannidhānābhāvācca । atrābhidhīyatē । sōmayuk‍tō﻿<pb n="b594"/>
yajiḥ nānyārthatāṁ pratipat‍tuṁ śak‍nōti yadi na jyōtiṣṭōmamanuvadati ।
sa hyupadēśāt sōmavān । tasmāttat‍sambandhāttat‍saṁskāraḥ । tat‍sāha&mdash;
caryāc‍cāṁśāvapīt‍yuktam ।</p>
<p><q>agristu liṅgadarśanāt ।</q> ya ēvaṁ vidvānagniṁ cinuta iti
kimayaṁ saṁskāracōdanā vā uta yajimat‍karmēti । yajimat‍karmēti brūmaḥ﻿<pb n="b595"/>
<q>yajiśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt ।</q> agniṁ cinuta iti prāptēḥ । cinōti-
ridānīṁ kimarthaḥ । ālabhatītivadbhaviṣyatīti cēt tat nōpapadyatē । tatra
hi kāryataḥ prāptirālabhatēḥ । iha punarna cinōtēḥ anyataḥ kāryatāvagatiḥ ।﻿<pb n="b596"/>
upadēśāditi cēnna, vāk‍yabhēdaprasaṅgāt । prakaraṇamapīti vāk‍yabhēdasavya-
pēkṣamēva । ēvaṁ tarhīyaṁ kañcitsaṅghātaṁ kāryaprāptamaṅgīkr̥tyānuvādō bhaviṣyati ।
atha vā iṣṭakābhiragniṁ cinuta iti prāptasyāyamanuvādaḥ । tathā ca liṅga-
darśanamuktam ।</p>
<p><q>dravyaṁ vā syāccōdanāyāḥ ।</q> atrōcyatē&mdash;saṁskāracōdanaivaiṣā ।
kutaḥ ? saṁskāraśabdaśravaṇāt । agniśabdasya ca jvalanē rūḍhatvāt ।﻿<pb n="b597"/>
kathaṁ tarhi agniṁ anuyajatīti ? cayanasaṁskr̥tē'g‍nau paścādyajatītyarthaḥ ।
<q>cayanamabhinirvr̥tyēti yāvat ।</q> atha yalliṅgamuktaṁ tat cayana&mdash;
saṁskr̥tāgniyuktē draṣṭavyaṁ tāsvēva cōdanāsu ।</p>﻿<pb n="b598"/>
<p><q>prakaraṇāntarē prayōjanānyatvam ।</q> māsamagnihōtraṁ juhōtīti
śrūyatē । tatra śāstrāntarāmidaṁ agnihōtraśāstrāt uta nēti cintyatē । nanu
ca māsavidhānē'pi śāstrāntaramēvaitat । vāk‍yāntaramēvēdaṁ na śāstrāntaram ।
tulyakāryaguṇāntaravidhānāpēkṣaṁ bhavati śāstrāntaraṁ na kēvalabhāvavidhānāpēkṣam﻿<pb n="b599"/>
kiṁ yuktam ? na śāstrāntaramidaṁ naiyamika ēvāyaṁ guṇavidhiḥ ।
kutaḥ ? agnihōtraśabdapratyabhijñānāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b600"/>
<p>atrōcyatē&mdash;prakaraṇāntarē prayōjanānyatvam । kimidaṁ prakara-
ṇāntara iti ? aprakr̥tābhidhāna ityarthaḥ । nātra prakr̥tābhidhāyakō'yaṁ
juhōtiśabdaḥ dadhnā juhōti itivat । nanu cāgnihōtrābhidhānāt, naiya&mdash;
mika ēva guṇavacanatā'vagamyatē । na, juhōtērarthāntarāvagatēḥ । kathaṁ
punaranyārthāvagatiḥ । upasadbhiścaritvēti śravaṇāt । atō juhōtya-
rthānusāryayaṁ agnihōtraśabdaḥ na viparītaḥ । tasmāt siddhaṁ prakaraṇānta-
rat‍vam । prakaraṇāntaraṁ ca śāstrāntaratvam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b601"/>
<p><q>phalaṁ cākarmasannidhau ।</q> kimidamanyadēva bhēdakāraṇam ? nēti
brūmaḥ । atrāpyaprakr̥tābhidhānataiva pratipādyatē । kathaṁ ? pūrvatra upasadbhiśca-
ritvā iti aprakr̥tābhidhānatā uktā । idānīṁ punaḥ phalasaṁbandhēnāprakr̥tā-
bhidhānaṁ pratīyata iti pūrvapakṣavādinō'bhiprāyaḥ । karmaṇō vidhēyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="b602"/>
rāddhāntī tu manyatē । anyārthē bhavatyapi prakr̥tābhidhānam । svārthē
punaḥ na prakr̥tābhidhānaṁ pratīyatē । phalasaṁbandhē ca svārthō bhāvaśabdaḥ ।
nahyabhāvārthasya vidhānaṁ saṁbhavatītyuk‍tam । na ca dadhyādivat bhāvānu&mdash;
pravēśō'dhikārasya saṁbhavatīti vakṣyāmaḥ । anyathāpi aprakr̥tābhidhānaṁ
siddham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b603"/>
<p><q>sannidhau tvavibhāgāt ।</q> uk‍taṁ phalaṁ cākarmasannidhāviti ।
tasyēdaṁ pratyudāharaṇam । karmasannidhau phalayōgō na śāstrāntaratvamā&mdash;
pādayati । nanu ca vidhēyaparatvādbhāvārthasya kiṁ sannidhiḥ kariṣyati ?
satyaṁ vidhēyō bhāvārthaḥ । na punaḥ sannidhānamatikrāmati । nanu
atatparatvādabhidhānasya kiṁ sannidhiḥ kariṣyati ? idaṁ kariṣyati ।﻿<pb n="b604"/>
atatparē'pyabhidhānē'nyatō buddhiṁ niruṇaddhi । upadēśaparamapyabhidhānaṁ
sannidhau sati na viśēṣāntaramākṣēp‍tuṁ kṣamaḥ । tasmād‍yuk‍taṁ sannidhau tva-
vibhāgāditi ।</p>
<p><q>āg‍nēyastūktahētutvāt ।</q> aviśēṣāt karmāntaramityāśaṅkitaṁ
pūrvapakṣiṇā । āg‍nēyamātraśravaṇāt । avibhāgastu karmaṇō'bhyāsō
dviruk‍tēna pratīyēta ।</p>﻿<pb n="b605"/>
<p>atrōcyatē&mdash;rāddhāntavādī tu paurṇamāsīsaṁyuk‍taṁ vidhāyakaṁ manyatē । aprati-
pakṣatvāt । vihitasya ca punarvacanaṁ na śakyatē'rthāntaratayā pratipat‍tum । abhyā-﻿<pb n="b606"/>
sādhikaraṇē punarvidhānāviśēṣādityuktam । nanu ca niṣprayōjanaṁ punarvacana-
mityuktam । na prayōjanavaśādarthāntarapratipattiḥ avagamō hi tatvānyatvē
hētuḥ na cānarthakyam । aindrāgnavithānaṁ prayōjanamityuktam ।</p>
<trailer>iti vr̥hatyāṁ dvitīyādhyāyasya
tr̥tīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b607"/>
<head>atha caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>yāvajjīvikō'bhyāsaḥ ।</q> yāvajjīvamagnihōtraṁ juhōtītyatra cintyatē
kiṁ kāmyācchāstrāntaraṁ uta ēkamiti । kiṁ prāptaṁ ? karmaṇaḥ prāptatvāt 
guṇavidhiḥ । tataścaikaṁ śāstram । kaḥ punaratra guṇō vidhī&mdash;
yatē ? jīvanaṁ tāvat prāptatvādavidhēyam । ēvaṁ tarhi jīvanēna
﻿<pb n="b608"/>
lakṣitaḥ kālaḥ । nanu cāsāvapi nityaprāpta ēva ; na, yāvadanubandha-
tayā'prāptēḥ । tasmāt kālavidhiḥ । kō'yaṁ kālō nāma ? yaḥ
kālavidbhiruk‍taḥ । kē tē kālavidaḥ ? yē jyōtirvidaḥ ।
tathā ca liṅgadarśanam । tasmādēkaṁ śās‍tramiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b609"/>
<p><q>karturvā śrutisaṁyōgāt ।</q> atrōcyatē&mdash;adhikāracōdanaiṣā na
kālavidhiḥ । ataśca kāmyāt śāstrāntaratvam । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ adhikāra-
cādanaiṣā na kālavidhiriti ? kālavidhau hi padadvayamapi lakṣaṇa-
﻿<pb n="b610"/>
yā'nvapi bhavati । adhikārōpadēśē tu śrutyā । na ca saṁbhavantyāṁ
﻿<pb n="b611"/>
śrutau lakṣaṇāśrayaṇē kāraṇamasti । tasmādadhikāracōdanaivaiṣā । adhikāracōdanāyāṁ
﻿<pb n="b612"/>
ca prayōgāntarasiddhiḥ । ēvaṁ ca kr̥tvā liṅgadarśanāni ghaṭantē ।
jarāmaryavādō'pyupapadyata ityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b613"/>
<p><q>nāmarūpadharmaviśēṣapunarukti ।</q> atra bhēdapramāṇābhāsāni
pūrvapakṣē upanyasya rāddhāntē kēcit granthasaṁbandhitayā,
kēcit svādhyāyasaṁbandhitayā, kēcit karmāntarāśrayatayā,
kēcit yadēti kālayōgādityēvamādibhiḥ parihāraiḥ parihr̥tāti ।
﻿<pb n="b614"/>
tasmādvākyāntarāṇyēvaitāni na śās‍trāntarāṇīti siddham ।</p>
<trailer>iti br̥hatyāṁ dvitīyādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
